# Finance Guild — VCC Build Instructions & Guardrails
(Page ID: 487c2448-1146-4110-9c9c-ff23e1a42510)
(URL: https://www.notion.so/Finance-Guild-VCC-Build-Instructions-Guardrails-487c2448114641109c9cff23e1a42510)

[Total top-level blocks: 1371]


## Purpose

This is the **master instruction set for the VCC (Virtual Construction Crew)** — the LLM-powered coding agent responsible for building out the Finance Guild stack. Every file generated, every migration written, every component scaffolded **must** comply with these rules. No exceptions. No improvisation outside the boundaries defined below.
**Parent Spec:** The canonical source of truth is the sibling page — _Finance Guild — UI Layout & Dashboard Spec (Dev Handoff)_. If there is ever a conflict between these instructions and that spec, **the spec wins**.

---


# 1. Identity & Scope

You are building the **Finance Guild** module of the Citadel Nexus platform. Finance Guild is a multi-tenant invoicing, quoting, contract-signing, and financial reporting product for trade contractors and service businesses.

### What You Are Building

- A **React 18 + Vite + Tailwind CSS** frontend
- A **FastAPI** backend with **Supabase** (PostgreSQL + Auth + Storage + RLS)
- **NATS JetStream** event bus for real-time
- **Upstash Redis** for caching and rate limiting
- **Stripe Connect** for payments, **Xero** for accounting, **Mercury** for banking
- 5 micro-services: `smp-fin-api` (:8093), `smp-fin-ws` (:8094), `smp-fin-worker` (no HTTP), `smp-fin-pdf` (:8095), `smp-fin-ai` (:8096)

### What You Are NOT Building

- The Dataroom Engine (already exists on port 8092)
- Guardian audit system core (you log TO it, you don't build it)
- Oracle Dossier (you call its API, you don't build it)
- The NATS infrastructure itself (already provisioned)
- Supabase Auth (already exists — you use `auth.uid()` and `auth.users`)
- n8n automation platform (already exists — you publish NATS events it consumes)

---


# 2. Absolute Yeses ✅

These are **non-negotiable**. Every file, every function, every component MUST follow these.

### 2.1 Multi-Tenancy

- ✅ **Every table MUST have a **`**tenant_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES tenants(id)**`** column** (except join/child tables that inherit via FK)
- ✅ **Every table MUST have RLS enabled** — `ALTER TABLE ... ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY`
- ✅ **Every table MUST have a tenant isolation policy** using the pattern: `USING (tenant_id = (SELECT tenant_id FROM tenant_members WHERE user_id = auth.uid()))`
- ✅ **Every API endpoint MUST resolve **`**tenant_id**`** from the JWT** via `TenantScopeMiddleware` — never from query params or request body
- ✅ **Every Stripe API call MUST include the **`**Stripe-Account**`** header** scoped to the tenant's connected account ID

### 2.2 Database & Schema

- ✅ **Use the exact table names and column definitions from Section 13 of the spec** — do not rename, do not add columns without explicit instruction
- ✅ **All migrations MUST be idempotent** — use `IF NOT EXISTS` for creates, `IF EXISTS` for drops
- ✅ **All money columns MUST be **`**NUMERIC(12,2)**` — never use `FLOAT`, `REAL`, or `DOUBLE PRECISION` for money
- ✅ **All timestamps MUST be **`**TIMESTAMPTZ**` — never bare `TIMESTAMP`
- ✅ **All UUIDs MUST use **`**gen_random_uuid()**` — never `uuid_generate_v4()` (Supabase default)
- ✅ **All CHECK constraints from the spec MUST be preserved exactly** — these enforce domain invariants
- ✅ **All indexes from Section 16.3 and the schema page MUST be created** — they are not optional
- ✅ **Foreign keys MUST include **`**ON DELETE**`** behavior** — `CASCADE` for child line items, `RESTRICT` or no action for business references

### 2.3 API & Backend

- ✅ **All routes MUST go through the middleware stack** defined in Section 14: `TenantScopeMiddleware → EntitlementGateMiddleware → RBACMiddleware → IdempotencyMiddleware → RateLimitMiddleware → AuditTrailMiddleware → StripeAccountMiddleware`
- ✅ **All list endpoints MUST use cursor-based pagination** (Section 16.1) — never offset-based
- ✅ **All POST/PUT endpoints that touch financial records MUST support the **`**Idempotency-Key**`** header**
- ✅ **All payment-related POST endpoints MUST require **`**Idempotency-Key**` — return 400 if missing
- ✅ **All write operations MUST publish a NATS event** using the subjects defined in Section 9
- ✅ **All write operations MUST be logged to **`**finance_audit_log**` via `AuditTrailMiddleware`
- ✅ **All entitlement-gated endpoints MUST check **`**tenant.entitlements**` and return `403 { code: "ENTITLEMENT_REQUIRED", key: "..."}` if missing
- ✅ **All role-gated endpoints MUST check user role** per the RBAC table in Section 12.2
- ✅ **Use Pydantic v2 models for all request/response schemas** — strict mode, no `Any` types
- ✅ **All Stripe webhook handlers MUST verify the signature** before processing
- ✅ **All API errors MUST return structured JSON** — `{ "error": "ERROR_CODE", "message": "Human readable", "details": {} }`

### 2.4 Frontend & UI

- ✅ **Use the **`**dr.***`** Tailwind token system** for all colors, fonts, and spacing — never hardcode hex values except status colors (Section 8)
- ✅ **Every screen MUST implement all three states** — loading (skeleton), empty (CTA), error (retry) — using the `StateRenderer` wrapper (Section 18)
- ✅ **All animations MUST use Framer Motion** — no raw CSS transitions, no other animation libraries
- ✅ **Use **`**layoutId**`** for tab/page transitions** — this is a core UX pattern in the Citadel design system
- ✅ **All monetary amounts MUST be formatted with **`**Intl.NumberFormat**` using the tenant's currency
- ✅ **All dates MUST be formatted in the tenant's timezone** — never UTC in the UI
- ✅ **Use React Query (TanStack Query) for all server state** — never `useState` + `useEffect` for API data
- ✅ **Wire the **`**useFinanceWS**`** hook** for real-time cache invalidation (Section 15)
- ✅ **All form submissions MUST be debounced and show loading state** — prevent double-submits
- ✅ **All destructive actions MUST have a confirmation dialog** — void invoice, delete quote, disconnect integration
- ✅ **Toast notifications MUST follow the 12 standard types** in Section 18.3

### 2.5 File & Folder Structure

- ✅ **Backend routes MUST live in **`**src/api/finance/**` — one file per resource (see Section 14 table)
- ✅ **Frontend components MUST live in **`**src/components/finance/**` — one folder per feature area
- ✅ **Shared hooks MUST live in **`**src/hooks/**` — prefix with `useFinance` for Finance Guild hooks
- ✅ **PDF templates MUST live in **`**src/templates/pdf/**`
- ✅ **TypeScript types MUST live in **`**src/types/finance.ts**` — single source of truth for FE types
- ✅ **Use barrel exports (**`**index.ts**`**)** in every component folder

### 2.6 Testing & Quality

- ✅ **Every API endpoint MUST have at least one happy-path and one auth-failure test**
- ✅ **Every RLS policy MUST have a test that proves cross-tenant reads fail**
- ✅ **Every React component MUST have a basic render test**
- ✅ **Use **`**pytest**`** for backend, **`**vitest**`** for frontend**

---


# 3. Absolute Nos 🚫

These are **hard stops**. If the VCC generates any of these, the output MUST be rejected and regenerated.

### 3.1 Security — Never Do This

- 🚫 **NEVER store raw API keys in code, env files committed to git, or Supabase columns without Vault encryption**
- 🚫 **NEVER pass **`**tenant_id**`** from the client** — always derive from JWT server-side
- 🚫 **NEVER disable RLS** — not even "temporarily" or "for testing"
- 🚫 **NEVER use **`**service_role**`** key in client-side code** — that key bypasses RLS
- 🚫 **NEVER trust client-provided Stripe webhook payloads** — always verify signature with `stripe.webhooks.constructEvent()`
- 🚫 **NEVER log full credit card numbers, CVVs, or raw payment tokens** — Citadel is PCI-adjacent via Stripe Connect; don't break that
- 🚫 **NEVER expose internal error stack traces to the client** — catch and return structured error JSON
- 🚫 **NEVER use **`**SELECT ***`** in production queries** — always specify columns explicitly
- 🚫 **NEVER use string concatenation for SQL** — always use parameterized queries or Supabase client methods
- 🚫 **NEVER store passwords or secrets in **`**finance_audit_log.changes**` — sanitize before logging

### 3.2 Architecture — Never Do This

- 🚫 **NEVER create a new micro-service** beyond the 5 defined in Section 21 — if you think you need one, you're wrong
- 🚫 **NEVER add a new external dependency (npm package, pip package)** without explicit approval — use what's already in the stack
- 🚫 **NEVER use WebSocket for anything other than NATS→client event push** — all data fetching goes through REST
- 🚫 **NEVER use polling as a substitute for the WS real-time system** — the only exception is Mercury balance (15min poll, per spec)
- 🚫 **NEVER create your own auth system** — use Supabase Auth exclusively
- 🚫 **NEVER modify the **`**tenants**`**, **`**tenant_members**`**, or **`**auth.users**`** tables** — those are platform-level, not Finance Guild
- 🚫 **NEVER publish to NATS subjects outside the **`**citadel.finance.***`** or **`**citadel.dataroom.***`** namespaces** — other guilds own their namespaces
- 🚫 **NEVER use offset-based pagination** — cursor-based only (Section 16.1)
- 🚫 **NEVER use **`**localStorage**`** or **`**sessionStorage**`** for sensitive data** — tokens go in httpOnly cookies or in-memory only

### 3.3 UI/UX — Never Do This

- 🚫 **NEVER hardcode colors** — use `dr.*` tokens. The only exception is the 6 status colors in Section 8
- 🚫 **NEVER use **`**px**`** for spacing** — use Tailwind's spacing scale (`p-4`, `gap-6`, etc.)
- 🚫 **NEVER use a different charting library** than the one in the spec (Recharts or Chart.js — pick one and stay consistent)
- 🚫 **NEVER render money with **`**toFixed(2)**` — use `Intl.NumberFormat` with the correct currency code
- 🚫 **NEVER show raw UUIDs to users** — display human-readable identifiers (invoice numbers, quote numbers, customer names)
- 🚫 **NEVER use **`**alert()**`**, **`**confirm()**`**, or **`**prompt()**` — use the Citadel modal/dialog system
- 🚫 **NEVER leave a screen without a loading state** — every data-dependent view gets a skeleton
- 🚫 **NEVER use **`**dangerouslySetInnerHTML**` — if you think you need it, you don't
- 🚫 **NEVER auto-submit forms on field change** — always require explicit user action (button click)
- 🚫 **NEVER make a UI element clickable without a hover/focus state** — accessibility is not optional

### 3.4 Data Integrity — Never Do This

- 🚫 **NEVER use **`**FLOAT**`** or **`**DOUBLE PRECISION**`** for monetary amounts** — `NUMERIC(12,2)` only
- 🚫 **NEVER delete financial records** — use soft deletes (status = 'void', `is_archived = true`) or archive patterns
- 🚫 **NEVER allow an invoice to be edited after it has been sent** — create a credit note or void and re-issue
- 🚫 **NEVER allow a payment to be deleted** — payments are immutable ledger entries; use refunds for reversals
- 🚫 **NEVER calculate tax client-side** — always calculate on the server using `finance_tax_rates`
- 🚫 **NEVER trust client-provided totals** — always recalculate `subtotal`, `tax_amount`, and `total` server-side from line items
- 🚫 **NEVER create a Stripe invoice without first verifying the tenant has an active Stripe Connect account**
- 🚫 **NEVER send an SMS (Text-to-Pay) without rate-limit checking** — max 10/min per tenant

---


# 4. Build Order — What to Scaffold First

The VCC MUST build in this order. Each phase depends on the previous one. Do not skip ahead.

### Phase 0 — Foundation (Day 0)


[CALLOUT] 📍 **Current Position: Phase 1.6** — 6/9 Phase 1 routers complete (integrations, customers, service_catalog, invoices, payments, dashboard). Next: Phase 1.7 Dashboard UI Component. The VCC MUST post a CRP cycle report at each Phase checkpoint before advancing.


[CALLOUT] 🔍 **PHASE TRACKING — MANDATORY GIT SCAN**

  The VCC MUST determine its current phase and progress by scanning the actual codebase — NOT by reading `.vcc_state.json` alone. On every hydration cycle:
  1. Run `git log --oneline --name-only -50 | grep router_` to count committed routers
  1. Run `ls src/api/finance/router_*.py` to count existing router files
  1. Cross-reference against the Phase 1 build order (9 routers total)
  1. Update `.vcc_state.json` with the ACTUAL count, not the cached value
  1. Set `current_phase` based on actual progress, not a hardcoded default
  If `.vcc_state.json` says `Routers: 0/9` but `ls` shows 6 router files, the VCC MUST trust the filesystem and update the state file. **The filesystem is the source of truth, not the cache.**
1. Run the database migration (`20260227_finance_guild_missing_tables.sql` — Section 13)
1. Verify all RLS policies are active — run cross-tenant access test
1. Set up the `src/api/finance/` folder structure with empty router files (Section 14)
1. Implement the middleware stack (`middleware.py`) — tenant scope, entitlement gate, RBAC, idempotency, rate limit, audit trail, Stripe account
1. Set up `src/components/finance/` folder structure
1. Implement `StateRenderer.tsx` (Section 18.2)
1. Implement `useFinanceWS` hook (Section 15)
1. Implement `useEntitlement` hook

### Phase 1 — P0 Core (Days 1-5)

1. **Stripe Connect onboarding** (`router_integrations.py` — `/stripe/connect` and `/stripe/disconnect`) — without this, nothing else works
1. **Customer CRUD** (`router_customers.py`) — invoices and quotes need customers
1. **Service Catalog CRUD** (`router_service_catalog.py`) — AI generation needs this
1. **Invoice CRUD** (`router_invoices.py`) — core feature
1. **Text-to-Pay** (`router_payments.py` — `/text-to-pay`) — highest-value feature
1. **Dashboard stats** (`router_dashboard.py`) — aggregated view
1. **Dashboard UI** — stat cards, activity feed, quick actions (Section 1)
1. **Invoice List UI** — filter tabs, invoice cards, actions (Section 3)
1. **Webhook handler** (`router_webhooks_stripe.py`) — Stripe events → NATS

### Phase 2 — P1 Features (Days 6-10)

1. Quote CRUD + line items
1. Quote List + Detail UI (Section 4)
1. PDF template engine (`smp-fin-pdf`) — invoice and quote templates
1. Tax rate management
1. Xero integration — OAuth, invoice push, payment push
1. Full-text search on invoices, quotes, customers

### Phase 3 — P2 Features (Days 11-17)

1. AI quote generator (`smp-fin-ai` + Bedrock)
1. AI line-item generator for invoices
1. Revenue chart + reports
1. Recurring billing schedules
1. Credit notes / refunds
1. Commission engine
1. Mercury integration (read-only balance + transactions)
1. **Email system** (`smp-fin-api` + AWS SES) — transactional email delivery for invoice sends, quote sends, payment receipts, reminder sequences (`finance.email.*` NATS subjects), bounce/complaint webhook handler, per-tenant sender identity (`From:` name + reply-to), email open/click tracking via PostHog
1. **Email control panel UI** — template preview/edit (invoice, quote, receipt, reminder, overdue), delivery log table (sent/delivered/bounced/complained per tenant), per-tenant SMTP override config (custom domain, DKIM), bulk email preferences, unsubscribe management, email analytics dashboard (open rate, click rate, bounce rate)

### Phase 4 — P3 Features (Days 18-25)


[CALLOUT] 🚀 **Deployment Model:** Phase 4 uses a **staggered install** pattern — services deploy one at a time with health gate verification between each. All 5 SMP services connect **directly to the ECS stack** (AWS ECS Fargate) — no intermediate proxy layer. ECS task definitions, service discovery, and ALB target groups are provisioned per-service.

1. **Staggered ECS deployment scaffold** — ECS task definitions for all 5 SMP services (`smp-fin-api`, `smp-fin-ws`, `smp-fin-worker`, `smp-fin-pdf`, `smp-fin-ai`), Fargate launch configs, ALB target group routing, CloudMap service discovery registration, health gate between each service rollout (next service does not start until previous passes `/health` for 60s)
1. **Direct ECS stack connection** — remove local Docker Compose orchestration for production; wire all services to ECS service connect for inter-service communication; NATS endpoint resolves via CloudMap (`citadel-finance.local`); Supabase, Redis, and Stripe connections go direct (no sidecar proxy); ECS exec enabled for debug access in staging only
1. Signing ceremony (DocuSign iframe + webhooks)
1. Contract → auto-invoice automation
1. Dispute/chargeback workflow
1. Multi-currency support
1. Batch operations
1. Job profitability + CLV reports
1. **ECS auto-scaling policies** — target-tracking on CPU (60%) and request count per target (1000 req/min) for `smp-fin-api`; step scaling on SQS/NATS queue depth for `smp-fin-worker`; scheduled scaling for `smp-fin-pdf` (scale up during business hours); min 2 / max 10 tasks per service in production
1. **Stagger install verification gate** — automated rollout script (`tools/ecs_stagger_deploy.py`) deploys services in dependency order: worker → ws → pdf → ai → api; each stage runs `/health` probe + smoke test before proceeding; rollback to previous task definition on failure; posts deployment manifest to Notion via CRP

### Phase 5 — Guild Audit & Build-Out (Days 26-30)


[CALLOUT] 🔍 **Purpose:** Before any guild module goes to production, Phase 5 runs a full audit of the completed build, generates a comprehensive Notion report, and gates production deployment behind quality checks. This phase is **not optional** — no guild ships without it.

**5.1 — Audit Scope**
1. **Schema Audit** — Verify all `fg_*` tables match spec Section 13 exactly (columns, types, constraints, indexes). Run `schema_diff.py` against Notion blueprint.
1. **RLS Audit** — Execute cross-tenant penetration tests for every table. Every policy must prove isolation. Results logged to `finance_audit_log`.
1. **SRS Coverage Audit** — Walk every SRS code (SRS-FIN-001 through SRS-FIN-028). Verify each has: route file, service file, test file, component (if UI), TypeScript types. Produce a coverage matrix.
1. **CAPS Scoring Audit** — Run AIMB pipeline on all 5 SMP profiles. Every service must score **B (70+)** or higher. Services below threshold are flagged `X` (quarantine).
1. **Guardrails Audit** — Full-repo scan using all 15 guardrail rules from `crp_config.yaml`. Zero critical violations required for promotion.
1. **Entitlement & RBAC Audit** — Test every entitlement gate and role combination. Verify Starter/Pro/Enterprise tier boundaries.
1. **Observability Audit** — Confirm PostHog events fire for all user actions, Datadog APM traces exist for all endpoints, monitors are provisioned.
1. **Diff Audit** — Three-layer diff check (spec→code, cycle→cycle, blueprint→blueprint). Zero unacknowledged drift.
**5.2 — Notion Audit Report**
VCC MUST generate and post a **Guild Audit Report** to Notion at the end of Phase 5. This is a superset of the CRP cycle report:
| **Section** | **Contents** | **Pass Criteria** |
| Schema Compliance | Table-by-table diff: spec vs actual DDL | 0 diffs |
| RLS Coverage | Per-table: policy name, test result, cross-tenant proof | 100% tables covered, 0 leaks |
| SRS Coverage Matrix | SRS code × artifact type (route, service, test, component, types) | 100% for current phase |
| CAPS Scorecard | Per-service: C/A/P/S scores, composite, grade, archetype | All services ≥ B (70) |
| Guardrails Report | Full scan: pass/fail per rule, violation count by severity | 0 critical violations |
| Entitlement Matrix | Feature × tier × role test results | All gates enforced |
| Observability Checklist | PostHog events, Datadog traces, monitors, dashboards | All provisioned |
| Diff Summary | Three-layer diff: clean/dirty per layer | All layers clean |
| Deployment Readiness | Binary GO / NO-GO with blocking reasons | GO |
**5.3 — Audit Report Format**
```javascript
GUILD-AUDIT-{GUILD}-{YYYYMMDD}-{HHMM}
```
Example: `GUILD-AUDIT-FIN-20260305-1400`
**5.4 — Audit Automation — **`**guild_auditor.py**`
Place at `tools/guild_auditor.py`. Orchestrates all 8 audit scopes and posts the consolidated report to Notion:
```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Guild Auditor — Pre-production audit with Notion reporting.

Runs all audit scopes, computes GO/NO-GO, posts report to Notion.
Usage: python tools/guild_auditor.py --phase P1 --services smp-fin-api,smp-fin-ws
"""

import os
import json
import subprocess
import re
from dataclasses import dataclass, field, asdict
from datetime import datetime, timezone
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Optional

import requests
import yaml

NOTION_API = "https://api.notion.com/v1"
NOTION_VERSION = "2022-06-28"
NOTION_TOKEN = os.environ["NOTION_INTERNAL_TOKEN"]
VCC_PAGE_ID = os.environ["VCC_INSTRUCTIONS_PAGE_ID"]
REPO_ROOT = Path(os.environ.get("REPO_ROOT", "."))
GUILD = "FIN"


@dataclass
class AuditResult:
    scope: str
    passed: bool
    total_checks: int = 0
    passed_checks: int = 0
    failed_checks: int = 0
    details: list = field(default_factory=list)
    blocking: bool = False  # if True, blocks deployment


@dataclass
class GuildAuditReport:
    audit_id: str
    guild: str
    phase: str
    timestamp: str
    services_audited: list
    results: list  # list[AuditResult]
    go_no_go: str = "NO-GO"
    blocking_reasons: list = field(default_factory=list)
    caps_scores: dict = field(default_factory=dict)
    srs_coverage: dict = field(default_factory=dict)


def audit_schema(phase: str) -> AuditResult:
    """Audit 1: Compare fg_* DDL against spec."""
    result = AuditResult(scope="Schema Compliance", passed=True)
    migrations_dir = REPO_ROOT / "supabase" / "migrations"
    spec_tables = [
        "finance_invoices", "finance_invoice_line_items",
        "finance_quotes", "finance_quote_line_items",
        "finance_customers", "finance_service_catalog",
        "finance_payments", "finance_contracts",
        "finance_recurring_schedules", "finance_credit_notes",
        "finance_commissions", "finance_tax_rates",
        "finance_integrations", "finance_audit_log",
    ]
    # Check each expected table exists in migrations
    for table in spec_tables:
        result.total_checks += 1
        found = False
        if migrations_dir.exists():
            for sql_file in migrations_dir.glob("*.sql"):
                content = sql_file.read_text(errors="replace")
                if f"CREATE TABLE" in content and table in content:
                    found = True
                    break
        if found:
            result.passed_checks += 1
        else:
            result.failed_checks += 1
            result.details.append(f"MISSING: {table} not found in migrations")
            result.passed = False
            result.blocking = True
    return result


def audit_rls() -> AuditResult:
    """Audit 2: Verify RLS policies exist for all finance tables."""
    result = AuditResult(scope="RLS Coverage", passed=True)
    migrations_dir = REPO_ROOT / "supabase" / "migrations"
    tables_with_rls = set()
    all_finance_tables = set()
    if migrations_dir.exists():
        for sql_file in migrations_dir.glob("*.sql"):
            content = sql_file.read_text(errors="replace")
            for m in re.finditer(r"CREATE TABLE\s+(?:IF NOT EXISTS\s+)?(finance_\w+)", content):
                all_finance_tables.add(m.group(1))
            for m in re.finditer(r"ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY.*?(finance_\w+)|(finance_\w+).*?ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY", content):
                tables_with_rls.add(m.group(1) or m.group(2))
            for m in re.finditer(r"CREATE POLICY\s+\w+\s+ON\s+(finance_\w+)", content):
                tables_with_rls.add(m.group(1))
    for table in all_finance_tables:
        result.total_checks += 1
        if table in tables_with_rls:
            result.passed_checks += 1
        else:
            result.failed_checks += 1
            result.details.append(f"NO RLS: {table} has no RLS policy")
            result.passed = False
            result.blocking = True
    return result


def audit_srs_coverage(phase: str) -> AuditResult:
    """Audit 3: SRS code coverage matrix."""
    result = AuditResult(scope="SRS Coverage Matrix", passed=True)
    with open(REPO_ROOT / "config" / "crp_config.yaml") as f:
        config = yaml.safe_load(f)
    srs_codes = config.get("srs_codes", {})
    phase_codes = {k: v for k, v in srs_codes.items()
                   if v.get("phase", "") <= phase}  # P0 <= P1 etc.
    api_dir = REPO_ROOT / "src" / "api" / "finance"
    comp_dir = REPO_ROOT / "src" / "components" / "finance"
    for code, info in phase_codes.items():
        result.total_checks += 1
        route = info.get("route")
        component = info.get("component")
        has_impl = False
        if route and (api_dir / route).exists():
            has_impl = True
        if component and (comp_dir / component).exists():
            has_impl = True
        if info.get("service"):
            has_impl = True  # Service-level, checked by CAPS
        if has_impl:
            result.passed_checks += 1
        else:
            result.failed_checks += 1
            result.details.append(f"MISSING: {code} ({info['name']}) has no implementation")
            result.passed = False
    return result


def audit_caps(services: list) -> tuple[AuditResult, dict]:
    """Audit 4: Run AIMB CAPS scoring on all services."""
    result = AuditResult(scope="CAPS Scorecard", passed=True)
    scores = {}
    for svc in services:
        result.total_checks += 1
        sake_path = REPO_ROOT / f"{svc}.sake.yaml"
        if not sake_path.exists():
            sake_path = REPO_ROOT / "config" / "smp" / f"{svc}.sake.yaml"
        if sake_path.exists():
            with open(sake_path) as f:
                profile = yaml.safe_load(f)
            caps = profile.get("caps_scores", {})
            composite = caps.get("composite", 0)
            grade = caps.get("grade", "F")
            scores[svc] = {"C": caps.get("C", 0), "A": caps.get("A", 0),
                           "P": caps.get("P", 0), "S": caps.get("S", 0),
                           "composite": composite, "grade": grade}
            if composite >= 70:
                result.passed_checks += 1
            else:
                result.failed_checks += 1
                result.details.append(f"BELOW THRESHOLD: {svc} scored {composite} ({grade}), needs ≥70 (B)")
                result.passed = False
                result.blocking = True
        else:
            result.failed_checks += 1
            result.details.append(f"NO PROFILE: {svc}.sake.yaml not found")
            result.passed = False
            result.blocking = True
    return result, scores


def audit_guardrails() -> AuditResult:
    """Audit 5: Full-repo guardrails scan."""
    result = AuditResult(scope="Guardrails Report", passed=True)
    # Delegate to existing vcc_cycle_reporter guardrails scanner
    try:
        proc = subprocess.run(
            ["python", "tools/vcc_cycle_reporter.py", "--from", "HEAD~1", "--to", "HEAD", "--dry-run"],
            capture_output=True, encoding="utf-8", cwd=REPO_ROOT, timeout=60
        )
        output = proc.stdout
        crit_match = re.search(r"Violations:\s*(\d+)", output)
        if crit_match and int(crit_match.group(1)) > 0:
            result.passed = False
            result.blocking = True
            result.details.append(f"{crit_match.group(1)} guardrail violations detected")
            result.failed_checks = int(crit_match.group(1))
        else:
            result.passed_checks = 1
        result.total_checks = 1
    except Exception as e:
        result.passed = False
        result.details.append(f"Guardrail scan failed: {e}")
        result.total_checks = 1
    return result


def audit_entitlements() -> AuditResult:
    """Audit 6: Entitlement & RBAC gate tests."""
    result = AuditResult(scope="Entitlement Matrix", passed=True)
    try:
        proc = subprocess.run(
            ["python", "-m", "pytest", "tests/", "-k", "entitlement or rbac",
             "--tb=no", "-q", "--no-header"],
            capture_output=True, encoding="utf-8", cwd=REPO_ROOT, timeout=120
        )
        # Parse pytest output
        match = re.search(r"(\d+) passed(?:.*?(\d+) failed)?", proc.stdout)
        if match:
            result.passed_checks = int(match.group(1))
            result.failed_checks = int(match.group(2) or 0)
            result.total_checks = result.passed_checks + result.failed_checks
            if result.failed_checks > 0:
                result.passed = False
                result.blocking = True
        else:
            result.details.append("No entitlement/RBAC tests found")
            result.passed = False
    except Exception as e:
        result.passed = False
        result.details.append(f"Test run failed: {e}")
    return result


def audit_observability() -> AuditResult:
    """Audit 7: PostHog + Datadog provisioning check."""
    result = AuditResult(scope="Observability Checklist", passed=True)
    checks = [
        ("PostHog provider", "src/providers/PostHogProvider.tsx"),
        ("Datadog middleware", "src/api/finance/middleware_datadog.py"),
        ("PostHog config", "config/crp_config.yaml"),
    ]
    for name, path in checks:
        result.total_checks += 1
        if (REPO_ROOT / path).exists():
            result.passed_checks += 1
        else:
            result.failed_checks += 1
            result.details.append(f"MISSING: {name} ({path})")
            result.passed = False
    return result


def audit_diff() -> AuditResult:
    """Audit 8: Three-layer diff check."""
    result = AuditResult(scope="Diff Summary", passed=True)
    try:
        proc = subprocess.run(
            ["python", "tools/diff_checker.py", "--all-layers", "--json"],
            capture_output=True, encoding="utf-8", cwd=REPO_ROOT, timeout=60
        )
        if proc.returncode == 0:
            diff_data = json.loads(proc.stdout)
            for layer_name, layer in diff_data.items():
                result.total_checks += 1
                if layer.get("clean", False):
                    result.passed_checks += 1
                else:
                    result.failed_checks += 1
                    result.details.append(f"DIRTY: {layer_name} has unresolved diffs")
                    result.passed = False
        else:
            result.details.append(f"Diff checker exited with code {proc.returncode}")
            result.passed = False
    except FileNotFoundError:
        result.details.append("diff_checker.py not found — run CRP setup first")
        result.passed = False
    except Exception as e:
        result.details.append(f"Diff check failed: {e}")
        result.passed = False
    result.total_checks = max(result.total_checks, 1)
    return result


def run_full_audit(phase: str, services: list) -> GuildAuditReport:
    """Run all 8 audit scopes and produce consolidated report."""
    now = datetime.now(timezone.utc)
    audit_id = f"GUILD-AUDIT-{GUILD}-{now.strftime('%Y%m%d-%H%M')}"

    results = []
    results.append(audit_schema(phase))
    results.append(audit_rls())
    results.append(audit_srs_coverage(phase))
    caps_result, caps_scores = audit_caps(services)
    results.append(caps_result)
    results.append(audit_guardrails())
    results.append(audit_entitlements())
    results.append(audit_observability())
    results.append(audit_diff())

    blocking = [r for r in results if r.blocking and not r.passed]
    go_no_go = "GO" if not blocking else "NO-GO"
    blocking_reasons = []
    for r in blocking:
        blocking_reasons.extend(r.details[:3])

    return GuildAuditReport(
        audit_id=audit_id,
        guild=GUILD,
        phase=phase,
        timestamp=now.isoformat(),
        services_audited=services,
        results=results,
        go_no_go=go_no_go,
        blocking_reasons=blocking_reasons,
        caps_scores=caps_scores,
    )


def post_audit_to_notion(report: GuildAuditReport) -> str:
    """Post audit report to VCC Build Instructions as a toggle block."""
    headers = {
        "Authorization": f"Bearer {NOTION_TOKEN}",
        "Notion-Version": NOTION_VERSION,
        "Content-Type": "application/json",
    }
    emoji = "✅" if report.go_no_go == "GO" else "🚫"
    passed = sum(1 for r in report.results if r.passed)
    total = len(report.results)

    # Build children blocks
    children = []
    for r in report.results:
        icon = "✅" if r.passed else "🚫"
        text = f"{icon} {r.scope}: {r.passed_checks}/{r.total_checks} passed"
        if r.details:
            text += f"\n" + "\n".join(f"  • {d}" for d in r.details[:5])
        children.append({
            "object": "block", "type": "callout",
            "callout": {
                "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": text[:2000]}}],
                "icon": {"type": "emoji", "emoji": icon},
                "color": "green_background" if r.passed else "red_background",
            }
        })

    if report.caps_scores:
        caps_text = "CAPS Scores:\n" + "\n".join(
            f"  {svc}: C={s['C']:.0f} A={s['A']:.0f} P={s['P']:.0f} S={s['S']:.0f} → {s['composite']:.0f} ({s['grade']})"
            for svc, s in report.caps_scores.items()
        )
        children.append({
            "object": "block", "type": "callout",
            "callout": {
                "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": caps_text[:2000]}}],
                "icon": {"type": "emoji", "emoji": "📊"},
                "color": "purple_background",
            }
        })

    # GO/NO-GO verdict
    verdict = f"\n\nVerdict: {emoji} {report.go_no_go}"
    if report.blocking_reasons:
        verdict += "\nBlocking reasons:\n" + "\n".join(f"  🛑 {r}" for r in report.blocking_reasons)
    children.append({
        "object": "block", "type": "callout",
        "callout": {
            "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": verdict[:2000]}}],
            "icon": {"type": "emoji", "emoji": emoji},
            "color": "green_background" if report.go_no_go == "GO" else "red_background",
        }
    })

    toggle = {
        "object": "block",
        "type": "heading_2",
        "heading_2": {
            "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {
                "content": f"{emoji} Guild Audit — {report.audit_id} | {passed}/{total} scopes passed | {report.go_no_go}"
            }}],
            "is_toggleable": True,
            "children": children,
        },
    }

    resp = requests.patch(
        f"{NOTION_API}/blocks/{VCC_PAGE_ID}/children",
        headers=headers,
        json={"children": [{"object": "block", "type": "divider", "divider": {}}, toggle]},
    )
    resp.raise_for_status()
    return report.audit_id


if __name__ == "__main__":
    import argparse
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Guild Auditor")
    parser.add_argument("--phase", required=True, help="Target phase (P0, P1, P2, P3)")
    parser.add_argument("--services", default="smp-fin-api,smp-fin-ws,smp-fin-worker,smp-fin-pdf,smp-fin-ai")
    parser.add_argument("--dry-run", action="store_true")
    args = parser.parse_args()

    services = [s.strip() for s in args.services.split(",")]
    report = run_full_audit(args.phase, services)

    if args.dry_run:
        print(json.dumps(asdict(report), indent=2, default=str))
    else:
        audit_id = post_audit_to_notion(report)
        print(f"{report.go_no_go} — Posted audit: {audit_id}")
```
**5.5 — Usage**
```bash
# Full audit for Phase 1
python tools/guild_auditor.py --phase P1

# Audit specific services only
python tools/guild_auditor.py --phase P0 --services smp-fin-api,smp-fin-ws

# Dry run — print report without posting to Notion
python tools/guild_auditor.py --phase P1 --dry-run
```
**5.6 — Phase 5 Completion Criteria**
Phase 5 is complete when:
1. ✅ All 8 audit scopes pass (0 blocking failures)
1. ✅ Guild Audit Report posted to Notion with **GO** verdict
1. ✅ CAPS scores for all 5 services are ≥ B (70)
1. ✅ Zero critical guardrail violations
1. ✅ SRS coverage matrix is 100% for target phase
1. ✅ Three-layer diff check is clean
1. ✅ CI/CD quality gates pass (see Appendix F)
1. ✅ Operator signs off on the audit report

[CALLOUT] 🚨 **No guild module deploys to production without a passing Phase 5 audit.** If the audit returns NO-GO, fix all blocking issues and re-run. There are no exceptions.


### Phase 2.0 — CRP Hardening & Blueprint Growth (Post-Phase 5, Continuous)


[CALLOUT] 🔧 **Purpose:** Phase 2.0 is a VCC protocol upgrade that hardens the CRP automation, fills gaps in the blueprint, and ensures the VCC can operate autonomously at scale. These 8 fixes address every weakness identified in the CRP audit. Each fix ships with implementation code (Appendix G), a test structure, and audit criteria. Phase 2.0 is **not time-boxed** — it runs continuously after Phase 5 and gates all future guild onboarding.

**2.0.1 — Email SRS Code Registration** `FIX-001`
- **Gap:** Phase 3 items 8-9 (email system + control panel) have no SRS codes. VCC cannot track or report on email build progress.
- **Fix:** Register `SRS-FIN-029` (Email Transactional System) and `SRS-FIN-030` (Email Control Panel UI) in the SRS registry. Update `vcc_cycle_reporter.py` SRS_CODES dict and `crp_config.yaml`.
- **Test:** `test_srs_email_registration.py` — assert SRS-FIN-029 and SRS-FIN-030 exist in registry, map to `router_email.py` and `EmailControlPanel/` component folder, and are included in drift scans.
- **Audit Gate:** Phase 5 SRS Coverage Audit must include email codes. Drift scanner must flag missing email artifacts.
**2.0.2 — CRP Versioning & Report Validator** `FIX-002`
- **Gap:** No `crp_version` field in cycle reports. No programmatic validation that reports contain all 8 required sections. Schema changes break cross-cycle comparability.
- **Fix:** Add `crp_version: "2.0"` field to `CycleReport` dataclass. Create `crp_validator.py` that validates every report against a JSON schema before posting. Reject malformed reports (missing sections, empty §3, etc.).
- **Test:** `test_crp_validator.py` — 12 test cases: valid report passes, missing §1-§8 each fails, empty guardrails fails, null cycle_id fails, version mismatch warns. Validator runs as pre-post hook in `vcc_cycle_reporter.py`.
- **Audit Gate:** CI stage `crp-validate` runs `crp_validator.py --strict` on every generated report. Non-zero exit blocks the post.
**2.0.3 — Rollback Protocol** `FIX-003`
- **Gap:** Zero rollback instructions. No `DOWN` migrations, no revert-to-last-known-good procedure, no guidance for what VCC does when Phase 5 returns NO-GO.
- **Fix:** Add Section 18: Rollback & Recovery Protocol. Includes: DOWN migration template for every `fg_*` table, `rollback_manager.py` (reverts to last passing CRP snapshot), K8s rollback via `kubectl rollout undo`, Supabase migration rollback via `supabase db reset --to <version>`, feature flag kill-switch pattern.
- **Test:** `test_rollback_manager.py` — assert DOWN migration exists for every UP migration, rollback restores previous schema state, K8s rollback command is valid, feature flag toggle disables feature without deploy.
- **Audit Gate:** Phase 5 audit scope 9 (new): "Rollback Readiness" — every migration has a DOWN counterpart, rollback dry-run succeeds, feature flags provisioned for all Phase 3+ features.
**2.0.4 — SLA Targets & Error Budgets** `FIX-004`
- **Gap:** Health checks are binary (healthy/unhealthy) with no SLA targets. The `consecutive_failures >= 3` threshold is arbitrary. No uptime %, latency ceiling, or error rate budget.
- **Fix:** Add SLA config to `crp_config.yaml`: per-service targets for uptime (99.5%), p95 latency (500ms API, 100ms WS, 2s PDF, 5s AI), error rate ceiling (1%), and health check failure threshold (configurable, default 3). Add `sla_evaluator.py` that computes SLA compliance from Datadog metrics + health sweep data.
- **Test:** `test_sla_evaluator.py` — assert SLA breach flags NO-GO when p95 > threshold, uptime < target, or error rate > ceiling. Assert configurable thresholds override defaults. Assert SLA report embeds in CRP §7.
- **Audit Gate:** CRP §7 extended with SLA compliance table. Any SLA breach is a **warning** (not blocking) unless consecutive breaches exceed 3 cycles, then **blocking**.
**2.0.5 — Shared Scanner Library** `FIX-005`
- **Gap:** `guild_auditor.py` and `vcc_cycle_reporter.py` duplicate guardrail scanning, drift scanning, and RLS checking. Bug fixes in one don't propagate.
- **Fix:** Extract shared library `tools/lib/vcc_scanners.py` with: `scan_guardrails()`, `scan_drift()`, `scan_flags()`, `scan_rls()`, `scan_migrations()`. Both reporter and auditor import from the shared lib. Add `__init__.py` barrel export.
- **Test:** `test_vcc_scanners.py` — assert shared functions return identical results to old inline implementations. Assert both reporter and auditor use shared imports (AST check). Assert no duplicate function definitions across tools/.
- **Audit Gate:** CI lint stage checks for duplicate function signatures across `tools/`. Fails if any scanner function is defined in more than one file.
**2.0.6 — Notion Page Archival Strategy** `FIX-006`
- **Gap:** Every cycle report appends a toggle block. After 50+ cycles, the page hits Notion's ~10K block limit. No archival or rotation strategy.
- **Fix:** Add `crp_archiver.py`: after 20 reports on the main page, moves older reports to a monthly archive page (`CRP Archive — YYYY-MM`), leaves a summary link on the main page. Archive pages are auto-created under VCC Build Instructions. Main page keeps only the latest 20 reports + archive index.
- **Test:** `test_crp_archiver.py` — assert archival triggers at threshold (configurable, default 20), archive page is created with correct title, moved reports retain toggle structure, main page summary link resolves, block count stays under 8K.
- **Audit Gate:** `crp_archiver.py --check` runs in CI post-deploy. Warns if main page block count > 7K. Fails if > 9K.
**2.0.7 — Guardrail Scanner Hardening** `FIX-007`
- **Gap:** `RLS_ENABLED` rule uses single-line lookahead (misses multi-file RLS). `TENANT_ID_REQUIRED` can't match multi-line CREATE TABLE. No guardrail for missing Idempotency-Key enforcement or Stripe `.retrieve()`/`.update()`/`.list()` calls.
- **Fix:** Upgrade scanner to multi-line mode for SQL rules. Add 5 new guardrail rules: `IDEMPOTENCY_KEY_REQUIRED` (payment POST routes must check header), `STRIPE_ALL_OPS` (all Stripe CRUD operations need `stripe_account`), `RLS_MULTI_FILE` (cross-file RLS check), `DEPENDENCY_LOCK` (diff `requirements.txt` + `package-lock.json` for unapproved additions), `TEST_COVERAGE_MINIMUM` (pytest-cov output must show ≥80%).
- **Test:** `test_guardrail_scanner_v2.py` — 20 test cases: multi-line CREATE TABLE with RLS in separate statement passes, Stripe `.list()` without `stripe_account` fails, new pip dependency in requirements.txt fails, payment POST without idempotency check fails, coverage below 80% fails.
- **Audit Gate:** Guardrail rule count must be ≥ 20 (up from 15). CI `guardrails` stage uses upgraded scanner. Zero critical violations required.
**2.0.8 — Cross-Cycle Trend Tracker** `FIX-008`
- **Gap:** Each CRP report is standalone. No trend analysis for test count growth, coverage, guardrail violations, CAPS scores, or bundle size across cycles.
- **Fix:** Add `crp_trend_tracker.py`: reads last N cycle reports from Notion (via archive index), computes deltas and trend lines for 8 KPIs (test count, coverage %, violation count, CAPS composite, bundle size KB, drift items, health failures, build time). Outputs trend table + sparkline ASCII chart in CRP §7.
- **Test:** `test_crp_trend_tracker.py` — assert trend computation with 1/5/20 historical reports, regression detection (test count decreased), coverage drop alert, CAPS score degradation flag. Assert trend section renders in CRP §7.
- **Audit Gate:** CRP §7 extended with trend section. **Regression alert** (any KPI worsening for 3+ consecutive cycles) becomes a blocking gate.

---

**Phase 2.0 — Completion Criteria**
Phase 2.0 is complete when:
1. ✅ All 8 FIX codes (FIX-001 through FIX-008) are implemented in Appendix G
1. ✅ All test files pass (`pytest tests/phase2/ -v`)
1. ✅ CRP version bumped to `2.0` and validator enforces new schema
1. ✅ Shared scanner library is sole source of truth (no duplicates)
1. ✅ Guardrail rule count ≥ 20 with 0 critical violations
1. ✅ Archival strategy active (main page ≤ 20 reports)
1. ✅ SLA targets configured and evaluator runs per cycle
1. ✅ Trend tracker produces cross-cycle analysis for ≥ 3 historical reports
1. ✅ Rollback protocol validated with dry-run on staging
1. ✅ All new tools added to `.gitlab-ci.yml` pipeline

[CALLOUT] 🚨 **Phase 2.0 is mandatory for all future guild onboarding.** Any new guild (Ops Guild, Logistics Guild, etc.) MUST run on CRP v2.0 from day one. Finance Guild retroactively upgrades after Phase 5 completion.


### Phase 2.1 — CRP ↔ Perplexity Control Loop Bridge (Post-Phase 2.0, Continuous)


[CALLOUT] 🔗 **Purpose:** Phase 2.1 wires the VCC build loop (CRP) and the Perplexity diagnostic loop into a single closed feedback system. Today these loops run in parallel — CRP reports on code health, Perplexity reports on infrastructure health — but neither reads the other's output. Phase 2.1 creates a **bidirectional bridge** so VCC stops building when infrastructure is on fire and Perplexity stops filing duplicate issues for problems VCC already fixed. This is the **minimum viable loop orchestration** required before any guild goes to production.

**2.1.0 — Architecture Overview**
The bridge connects two autonomous loops through a shared event bus, shared state store, and unified health schema:
```mermaid
flowchart LR
    subgraph VCC["VCC Build Loop (CRP)"]
        BUILD["VCC builds code"] --> CRP["CRP cycle report\n§1-§8"]
        CRP --> NATS_PUB["NATS publish\ncitadel.vcc.cycle.completed"]
    end

    subgraph BRIDGE["Phase 2.1 Bridge"]
        ORCH["loop_orchestrator.py\ncoordinates both loops"]
        STATE["public.vcc_loop_state\nshared state store"]
        HEALTH["CitadelHealthSnapshot\nunified schema"]
        DEDUP["Shared dedup\nLinear + GitLab"]
    end

    subgraph PPLX["Perplexity Control Loop v2"]
        NATS_SUB["NATS subscribe\ncitadel.vcc.cycle.completed"] --> READ["READ telemetry\n12 sources + CRP"]
        READ --> THINK["THINK 3-layer\nL1 Perplexity + L2 Azure + L3 Bedrock"]
        THINK --> WRITE["WRITE diagnostics\nNotion + Linear + GitLab"]
        WRITE --> NATS_DIAG["NATS publish\ncitadel.diagnostic.completed"]
    end

    NATS_PUB --> NATS_SUB
    NATS_DIAG -->|"inject into\nnext CRP §7"| CRP
    ORCH --> STATE
    ORCH --> HEALTH
    CRP --> STATE
    WRITE --> STATE
    CRP --> DEDUP
    WRITE --> DEDUP
```
**2.1.1 — Shared NATS Event Bus** `BRIDGE-001`
- **Gap:** CRP publishes no NATS events. Perplexity loop publishes no NATS events. Neither loop knows when the other completes a cycle. There is no trigger mechanism.
- **Fix:** Add two new NATS JetStream subjects under the `citadel.vcc.*` namespace:
  - `citadel.vcc.cycle.completed` — published by `vcc_cycle_reporter.py` after every CRP post. Payload: `{cycle_id, guild, phase, guardrail_pass, drift_clean, test_passed, test_failed, srs_codes_touched, health_status, timestamp}`
  - `citadel.diagnostic.completed` — published by `perplexity_control_loop_v2.py` after every diagnostic WRITE. Payload: `{diag_id, health_grade, health_score, blockers, recommendations, sources_read, l3_verdict, timestamp}`
- **Stream config:** JetStream stream `VCC_BRIDGE` with subjects `citadel.vcc.cycle.completed`, `citadel.diagnostic.completed`. Retention: limits, max 5000 msgs, max age 30 days. Consumer: durable pull consumer `vcc-bridge-consumer` with ack-wait 30s.
- **Test:** `test_bridge_nats_events.py` — assert both subjects publish valid JSON, consumer receives within 5s, payload schema validates against Pydantic model, messages survive NATS restart (JetStream persistence), consumer ack prevents redelivery.
- **Audit Gate:** CI stage `bridge-nats` verifies both subjects are declared in `crp_config.yaml` `nats_subjects` list. Fails if either subject is missing.
**2.1.2 — CRP → Perplexity Trigger** `BRIDGE-002`
- **Gap:** Perplexity loop runs on cron (hourly). It has no awareness of when VCC completes a build cycle. Diagnostics may run on stale state — or miss a critical deployment entirely.
- **Fix:** Add a NATS subscriber to `perplexity_control_loop_v2.py` that listens on `citadel.vcc.cycle.completed`. On receipt:
  1. Parse the CRP payload to extract `cycle_id`, `phase`, `guardrail_pass`, `srs_codes_touched`
  1. Inject CRP summary into the READ phase as `source: "vcc_crp"` alongside the existing 12 telemetry sources
  1. Run the full READ → RAG → THINK → WRITE pipeline immediately (bypass cron wait)
  1. Include CRP-specific analysis in the Perplexity system prompt: _"The VCC just completed cycle {cycle_id} in phase {phase}. Guardrails: {pass/fail}. SRS codes touched: {list}. Factor this deployment into your infrastructure analysis — check if new code introduced regressions."_
- **Cron fallback:** If no NATS event arrives within 90 minutes, cron fires the loop anyway (existing behavior preserved). The NATS trigger is additive, not a replacement.
- **Test:** `test_bridge_crp_trigger.py` — assert NATS message triggers Perplexity run within 10s, CRP payload is injected into READ output, system prompt includes cycle context, cron still fires if no NATS event, duplicate NATS messages within 60s are deduplicated.
- **Audit Gate:** Perplexity loop logs must show `[TRIGGER] NATS: citadel.vcc.cycle.completed` or `[TRIGGER] CRON: 90min timeout` for every run. Missing trigger source is a warning.
**2.1.3 — Perplexity → CRP Feedback Injection** `BRIDGE-003`
- **Gap:** CRP §7 (Health Metrics) only knows what the VCC can see from the codebase — test counts, guardrail scans, Notion sync. It has zero visibility into DORA metrics, Datadog monitor state, NATS connection health, Stripe revenue, or ECS service status. The Perplexity loop reads all of these but CRP never consumes Perplexity's output.
- **Fix:** Add `read_last_diagnostic()` function to `vcc_cycle_reporter.py`. Called during CRP §7 assembly:
  1. Query `public.vcc_loop_state` for the latest Perplexity diagnostic (or fall back to reading the latest Notion diagnostic page via API)
  1. Extract: `health_grade`, `health_score`, `blockers`, `infrastructure.status`, `code_health.pipeline_pass_rate`, `nats.connections`, `revenue.mrr`
  1. Inject into CRP §7 as a new subsection: **"§7.4 — Perplexity Diagnostic (last run)"** with grade, score, top 3 blockers, and infrastructure status
  1. If Perplexity health grade is `CRITICAL`, auto-flag the CRP cycle as `NO-GO` with reason: _"Perplexity diagnostic reports CRITICAL infrastructure state — do not deploy"_
  1. If Perplexity health grade is `DEGRADING` with score < 60, add a **warning** (not blocking) to CRP §6 Next Cycle Intent: _"Infrastructure degrading — prioritize Perplexity blockers before continuing build order"_
- **Dataflow:** Perplexity WRITE → `public.vcc_loop_state` → CRP `read_last_diagnostic()` → CRP §7.4
- **Test:** `test_bridge_feedback_injection.py` — assert `read_last_diagnostic()` returns valid diagnostic from state store, CRITICAL grade blocks CRP, DEGRADING < 60 adds warning, HEALTHY grade has no effect on CRP status, missing diagnostic (first run) produces graceful fallback with `"No Perplexity diagnostic available yet"`.
- **Audit Gate:** CRP §7 must contain a `§7.4 — Perplexity Diagnostic` subsection. Missing subsection is a **warning** for the first 3 cycles (grace period), then **blocking**.
**2.1.4 — Unified Health Schema** `BRIDGE-004`
- **Gap:** CRP health is binary per-service (`healthy`/`unhealthy` from `/health` endpoint). Perplexity health is a 0–100 score with domain sections (infrastructure, product, code, revenue). There is no common schema. A "healthy" CRP cycle can coexist with a CRITICAL Perplexity diagnostic — the operator has to mentally reconcile two incompatible health models.
- **Fix:** Define `CitadelHealthSnapshot` — a unified Pydantic model that both loops populate:
```python
class ServiceHealth(BaseModel):
    service_id: str                          # e.g. "smp-fin-api"
    status: Literal["healthy", "degraded", "unhealthy", "unknown"]
    response_time_ms: float | None = None
    consecutive_failures: int = 0
    dependencies: dict[str, str] = {}        # {"supabase": "connected", "nats": "connected"}

class InfrastructureHealth(BaseModel):
    cpu_pct: float | None = None
    memory_pct: float | None = None
    disk_pct: float | None = None
    nats_connections: int | None = None
    nats_total_connections: int | None = None
    active_monitors: int = 0
    alerting_monitors: int = 0

class CodeHealth(BaseModel):
    pipeline_pass_rate: float | None = None  # 0-100
    deploy_frequency_daily: float | None = None
    lead_time_hours: float | None = None
    change_failure_rate: float | None = None # 0-100
    test_count: int = 0
    coverage_pct: float | None = None

class RevenueHealth(BaseModel):
    mrr_cents: int = 0
    active_subscriptions: int = 0
    trialing_subscriptions: int = 0
    past_due_subscriptions: int = 0

class CitadelHealthSnapshot(BaseModel):
    snapshot_id: str                         # "HEALTH-{YYYYMMDD}-{HHMM}"
    timestamp: str                           # ISO 8601
    source: Literal["crp", "perplexity", "merged"]
    
    # Composite
    overall_grade: Literal["HEALTHY", "DEGRADING", "CRITICAL", "UNKNOWN"]
    overall_score: int                       # 0-100
    
    # Domain sections
    services: list[ServiceHealth] = []
    infrastructure: InfrastructureHealth | None = None
    code: CodeHealth | None = None
    revenue: RevenueHealth | None = None
    
    # CRP-specific
    crp_cycle_id: str | None = None
    guardrail_pass: bool | None = None
    drift_clean: bool | None = None
    sla_compliant: bool | None = None
    
    # Perplexity-specific
    diag_id: str | None = None
    perplexity_score: int | None = None
    l3_verdict: str | None = None
    blockers: list[str] = []
    recommendations: list[str] = []
```
- **Population rules:**
  - CRP populates: `services`, `code.test_count`, `code.coverage_pct`, `guardrail_pass`, `drift_clean`, `sla_compliant`, `crp_cycle_id`
  - Perplexity populates: `infrastructure`, `code.pipeline_pass_rate`, `code.deploy_frequency_daily`, `code.lead_time_hours`, `code.change_failure_rate`, `revenue`, `diag_id`, `perplexity_score`, `l3_verdict`, `blockers`, `recommendations`
  - `loop_orchestrator.py` merges both into a `source: "merged"` snapshot
- **Test:** `test_bridge_health_schema.py` — assert CRP-only snapshot validates, Perplexity-only snapshot validates, merged snapshot contains fields from both, `overall_grade` computation uses worst-of-both-sources rule, empty fields default gracefully.
- **Audit Gate:** Both loops must output a `CitadelHealthSnapshot` on every cycle. Schema validation failure is blocking.
**2.1.5 — Shared Dedup & Conflict Resolution** `BRIDGE-005`
- **Gap:** Both loops create Linear issues and GitLab issues independently. Perplexity creates `[CLv2]`-prefixed Linear issues. CRP creates issues via `guild_auditor.py`. Neither checks the other's issues. Result: duplicate issues for the same underlying problem (e.g., both flag "NATS connections low" independently).
- **Fix:** Create `tools/lib/issue_dedup.py` — a shared dedup library used by both loops:
  1. Before creating any Linear issue, query Linear for open issues with `[CLv2]` or `[CRP]` prefix matching the same root cause (fuzzy title match + tag match)
  1. Before creating any GitLab issue, query GitLab for open issues with `vcc-bridge` label matching the same subject
  1. If a matching issue exists from the other loop, **append a comment** instead of creating a duplicate: _"Also detected by {CRP|Perplexity} in cycle {id}. Severity: {grade}. See: {link}"_
  1. If no match exists, create with standardized prefix: `[CRP]` for VCC-originated, `[CLv2]` for Perplexity-originated
  1. Cross-link: when CRP creates an issue that Perplexity later detects, Perplexity adds a `confirmed-by-perplexity` label. Vice versa.
- **Dedup rules:**
  - Title similarity threshold: 0.75 (Jaccard on word tokens)
  - Same `root_cause_category` tag → automatic match
  - Issues closed within last 24h are excluded from dedup (allow re-filing if regression)
  - Rate limit: max 5 new issues per loop per cycle (prevent spam)
- **Test:** `test_bridge_dedup.py` — assert duplicate title is caught, different titles pass, closed issue is not matched, cross-loop comment is appended correctly, rate limit enforced at 5, fuzzy match catches "NATS connection failure" vs "NATS connections low".
- **Audit Gate:** CI stage `bridge-dedup` runs `issue_dedup.py --audit` which checks for duplicate open issues across both prefixes. Warns if duplicates found.
**2.1.6 — Shared State Store** `BRIDGE-006`
- **Gap:** No persistent shared state between loops. CRP writes to Notion (toggle blocks). Perplexity writes to Notion (diagnostic pages) + Supabase (`automation_events`). Neither can efficiently query the other's output. Cross-loop reads require fragile Notion API page traversal.
- **Fix:** Create `public.vcc_loop_state` table in Supabase — the canonical shared state store:
```sql
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS public.vcc_loop_state (
    id UUID DEFAULT gen_random_uuid() PRIMARY KEY,
    loop_source TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (loop_source IN ('crp', 'perplexity', 'orchestrator')),
    cycle_id TEXT NOT NULL,
    
    -- Health snapshot (JSON)
    health_snapshot JSONB NOT NULL DEFAULT '{}',
    
    -- CRP fields (null if source = perplexity)
    crp_version TEXT,
    guild TEXT,
    phase TEXT,
    guardrail_pass BOOLEAN,
    drift_clean BOOLEAN,
    sla_compliant BOOLEAN,
    test_passed INT,
    test_failed INT,
    srs_codes_touched JSONB DEFAULT '[]',
    
    -- Perplexity fields (null if source = crp)
    health_grade TEXT CHECK (health_grade IN ('HEALTHY', 'DEGRADING', 'CRITICAL', 'UNKNOWN')),
    health_score INT CHECK (health_score >= 0 AND health_score <= 100),
    l3_verdict TEXT,
    blockers JSONB DEFAULT '[]',
    recommendations JSONB DEFAULT '[]',
    sources_read JSONB DEFAULT '[]',
    notion_diagnostic_page_id TEXT,
    
    -- Orchestrator fields
    merged_grade TEXT,
    merged_score INT,
    go_no_go TEXT CHECK (go_no_go IN ('GO', 'NO-GO', 'WARNING')),
    blocking_reasons JSONB DEFAULT '[]',
    
    -- Meta
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
    expires_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT (NOW() + INTERVAL '90 days')
);

CREATE INDEX idx_vcc_loop_state_source ON public.vcc_loop_state(loop_source);
CREATE INDEX idx_vcc_loop_state_cycle ON public.vcc_loop_state(cycle_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_vcc_loop_state_created ON public.vcc_loop_state(created_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_vcc_loop_state_grade ON public.vcc_loop_state(health_grade) WHERE loop_source = 'perplexity';

-- Auto-cleanup: drop rows older than 90 days
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION cleanup_vcc_loop_state() RETURNS trigger AS $$
BEGIN
    DELETE FROM public.vcc_loop_state WHERE expires_at < NOW();
    RETURN NEW;
END;
$$ LANGUAGE plpgsql;

CREATE TRIGGER trg_cleanup_vcc_loop_state
    AFTER INSERT ON public.vcc_loop_state
    EXECUTE FUNCTION cleanup_vcc_loop_state();
```
- **Write rules:**
  - CRP writes one row per cycle with `loop_source = 'crp'`
  - Perplexity writes one row per diagnostic with `loop_source = 'perplexity'`
  - `loop_orchestrator.py` writes one merged row with `loop_source = 'orchestrator'` after reconciling both
- **Read rules:**
  - CRP reads latest `loop_source = 'perplexity'` row via `read_last_diagnostic()`
  - Perplexity reads latest `loop_source = 'crp'` row when triggered by NATS
  - Trend tracker reads last N rows of all sources for cross-loop trend analysis
- **Test:** `test_bridge_state_store.py` — assert CRP write validates, Perplexity write validates, orchestrator merge produces correct `go_no_go`, cleanup trigger removes expired rows, concurrent writes don't conflict, `read_last_diagnostic()` returns most recent row.
- **Audit Gate:** `vcc_loop_state` must have at least 1 CRP row and 1 Perplexity row within the last 24 hours in production. Missing rows trigger a **warning** (loop may not be running).
**2.1.7 — Loop Orchestrator** `BRIDGE-007`
- **Gap:** No single process coordinates both loops. CRP runs when VCC builds. Perplexity runs on cron. If both fire simultaneously, they can create conflicting state. No process merges their outputs into a single GO/NO-GO verdict. No process decides whether VCC should pause building because infrastructure is CRITICAL.
- **Fix:** Create `tools/loop_orchestrator.py` — the bridge coordinator:
  1. **Subscribes** to both NATS subjects (`citadel.vcc.cycle.completed` and `citadel.diagnostic.completed`)
  1. **On CRP event:** reads latest Perplexity state from `vcc_loop_state`, merges into `CitadelHealthSnapshot`, writes merged row, evaluates GO/NO-GO
  1. **On Perplexity event:** reads latest CRP state from `vcc_loop_state`, merges into `CitadelHealthSnapshot`, writes merged row, evaluates GO/NO-GO
  1. **GO/NO-GO rules:**
    - Perplexity `CRITICAL` → `NO-GO` (blocks VCC deploy)
    - CRP guardrails failed → `NO-GO`
    - CRP drift dirty → `NO-GO`
    - Perplexity `DEGRADING` + score < 50 → `NO-GO`
    - Perplexity `DEGRADING` + score 50-70 → `WARNING`
    - Both HEALTHY → `GO`
  1. **Auto-pause:** If GO/NO-GO is `NO-GO` for 3 consecutive merged snapshots, orchestrator publishes `citadel.vcc.build.pause` event. VCC reads this before starting next cycle and waits until `citadel.vcc.build.resume`.
  1. **Auto-resume:** When next Perplexity diagnostic returns `HEALTHY` or `DEGRADING` with score > 70, orchestrator publishes `citadel.vcc.build.resume`.
  1. **Notion reporting:** Orchestrator appends a summary callout to VCC Build Instructions page every 6 hours with: merged health grade, last CRP cycle ID, last Perplexity diagnostic ID, GO/NO-GO status, blocking reasons if any.
- **Runtime:** Runs as a persistent process (systemd service or ECS task). Not cron — it must be listening to NATS continuously.
- **Test:** `test_bridge_orchestrator.py` — assert CRP event triggers merge, Perplexity event triggers merge, CRITICAL → NO-GO, HEALTHY + HEALTHY → GO, 3 consecutive NO-GO triggers pause event, resume fires on recovery, Notion summary posts correctly, orchestrator survives NATS reconnect.
- **Audit Gate:** Orchestrator must have written at least 1 merged row to `vcc_loop_state` in the last 24 hours. Missing merged rows in production is **blocking** — it means the bridge is down.
**2.1.8 — CRP v2.1 Schema Extensions** `BRIDGE-008`
- **Gap:** CRP report schema (v2.0) has no fields for Perplexity diagnostic data, bridge status, or merged health. Adding these requires a schema version bump.
- **Fix:** Bump CRP to v2.1. Add to `CycleReport` dataclass:
  - `crp_version: str = "2.1"` (up from `"2.0"`)
  - `perplexity_diagnostic: dict | None = None` — injected by `read_last_diagnostic()`
  - `bridge_status: str = "unknown"` — `"connected"` | `"disconnected"` | `"degraded"` | `"unknown"`
  - `merged_go_no_go: str | None = None` — from orchestrator's last merged snapshot
  - `merged_health_score: int | None = None`
  - `merged_blockers: list[str] = []`
- **CRP §7 extensions:**
  - §7.4 — Perplexity Diagnostic (last run): grade, score, top 3 blockers, infrastructure status, DORA metrics
  - §7.5 — Bridge Status: connected/disconnected, last NATS event timestamps, orchestrator health, state store row count
  - §7.6 — Merged Health: overall GO/NO-GO, merged score, blocking reasons from both loops
- **CRP validator update:** `crp_validator.py` v2.1 requires §7.4, §7.5, §7.6 subsections. Reports without these are **rejected** after the 3-cycle grace period.
- **Test:** `test_bridge_crp_v21.py` — assert v2.1 schema validates with new fields, v2.0 reports are accepted during grace period, v2.0 reports rejected after grace period, §7.4/§7.5/§7.6 render correctly in Notion toggle block.
- **Audit Gate:** CRP version must be `"2.1"` after Phase 2.1 deployment. Version mismatch is **blocking**.
**2.1.9 — Environment Variables** `BRIDGE-009`
