**Phase 2.1 — Completion Criteria**
Phase 2.1 is complete when:
1. ✅ All 9 BRIDGE codes (BRIDGE-001 through BRIDGE-009) are implemented in Appendix H
1. ✅ NATS stream `VCC_BRIDGE` is provisioned with both subjects
1. ✅ `public.vcc_loop_state` table is migrated and receiving writes from both loops
1. ✅ CRP v2.1 schema validates with §7.4, §7.5, §7.6 subsections
1. ✅ `loop_orchestrator.py` is running as a persistent service and producing merged snapshots
1. ✅ Perplexity loop triggers on CRP NATS events (verified in logs)
1. ✅ CRP §7.4 contains Perplexity diagnostic data (verified in last 3 cycle reports)
1. ✅ Shared dedup prevents duplicate Linear/GitLab issues across loops (verified with test)
1. ✅ `CitadelHealthSnapshot` schema validates for CRP-only, Perplexity-only, and merged snapshots
1. ✅ 3-cycle NO-GO auto-pause triggers correctly (verified in staging)
1. ✅ All test files pass (`pytest tests/phase21/ -v`)
1. ✅ All bridge components added to `.gitlab-ci.yml` pipeline (see Appendix H)

[CALLOUT] 🚨 **Phase 2.1 is mandatory before production deployment.** Without the bridge, VCC will continue building while infrastructure burns and Perplexity will file duplicate issues for problems VCC already fixed. The loops MUST be connected. There are no exceptions.


### Phase 2.5 — OAD Integration Bridge (Post-Phase 2.1, Continuous)


[CALLOUT] 🧠 **Purpose:** Phase 2.5 wires the OAD (OpenAI Dev) cognition loop into the loop orchestration system alongside CRP and Perplexity. OAD is the **operational maintenance layer** — it runs every 5-15 minutes on rig2, monitors GitLab pipelines, Supabase events, Linear issues, Notion pages, and Slack via a Reflex Engine (pattern-matching self-healer) and a College System (multi-agent FAISS-backed reasoning). Today OAD operates independently — its auto-fixes, pipeline failure detections, and mission dispatches are invisible to VCC and Perplexity. Phase 2.5 creates a **tridirectional bridge** so the orchestrator can dispatch missions to OAD, consume OAD's Reflex auto-fix reports, and query the College System for complex reasoning — completing the build→inspect→maintain triad.

**2.5.0 — Architecture Overview**
Phase 2.5 extends the Phase 2.1 bridge from a bilateral (VCC↔Perplexity) system to a trilateral (VCC↔Perplexity↔OAD) orchestration:
```mermaid
flowchart LR
    subgraph VCC["VCC Build Loop (CRP)"]
        BUILD["VCC builds code"] --> CRP["CRP cycle report\n§1-§8"]
        CRP --> NATS_VCC["NATS publish\ncitadel.vcc.cycle.completed"]
    end

    subgraph BRIDGE["Phase 2.5 Bridge"]
        ORCH["loop_orchestrator.py v2.5\ntrilateral coordinator"]
        STATE["public.vcc_loop_state\nextended with OAD fields"]
        HEALTH["CitadelHealthSnapshot v2.5\n+ OAD domain"]
        DEDUP["Shared dedup v2.5\nLinear + GitLab + OAD"]
        COLLEGE_Q["College Query Interface\nFAISS vector reasoning"]
    end

    subgraph PPLX["Perplexity Control Loop v2"]
        NATS_PPLX_SUB["NATS subscribe"] --> PPLX_READ["READ telemetry"]
        PPLX_READ --> PPLX_THINK["THINK 3-layer"]
        PPLX_THINK --> PPLX_WRITE["WRITE diagnostics"]
        PPLX_WRITE --> NATS_DIAG["NATS publish\ncitadel.diagnostic.completed"]
    end

    subgraph OAD["OAD Cognition Loop"]
        COGNITION["5-15 min cognition cycle\nrig2 primary"] --> REFLEX["Reflex Engine\nF924/F950/F960"]
        REFLEX --> AUTOFIX["Auto-fix applied"]
        COGNITION --> COLLEGE["College System\n33 professors + FAISS"]
        COLLEGE --> ANALYSIS["Compound analysis"]
        AUTOFIX --> NATS_OAD["NATS publish\ncitadel.oad.reflex.applied"]
        ANALYSIS --> NATS_OAD_THINK["NATS publish\ncitadel.oad.cognition.completed"]
    end

    NATS_VCC --> NATS_PPLX_SUB
    NATS_DIAG -->|"inject into\nnext CRP §7"| CRP
    NATS_OAD -->|"reflex fixes\ninto CRP §7.7"| CRP
    NATS_OAD_THINK -->|"college insights\ninto diagnostics"| PPLX_READ
    ORCH --> STATE
    ORCH --> HEALTH
    ORCH -->|"dispatch missions"| OAD
    CRP --> STATE
    PPLX_WRITE --> STATE
    AUTOFIX --> STATE
    ORCH --> COLLEGE_Q
    CRP --> DEDUP
    PPLX_WRITE --> DEDUP
    AUTOFIX --> DEDUP
```
**Key OAD Technical Details:**
- **Runtime:** Cognition loop every ~5-15 minutes on `rig2` (primary), with `rig1`/`rig3` as secondaries
- **Persona:** `npc_id='openaidev', role='oad'`
- **Reflex Engine:** Pattern-matching self-healer — `F924` (YAML syntax), `F950` (enum regen), `F960` (broken imports)
- **College System:** Multi-agent reasoning with FAISS vector DB, Perplexity sonar ("thought") + GPT-4o-mini ("compound")
- **Supabase tables:** `automation_events`, `oad_missions`, `oad_memories`, `contributors`
- **Logging:** Snapshots to Notion journal pages with JSON structure: `{rig, ts, gitlab{}, linear{}, supabase{}, notion{}, thought{}, compound{}}`
- **Broadcasts:** Slack `#all-citadel-nexus`
- **SRS tracking:** `SRS-OAD-010` through `SRS-OAD-017`
- **Linear integration:** Auto-creates tickets on failures (currently has API token issue — `"status": "error"`)

---

**2.5.1 — OAD NATS Event Bus** `OAD-001`
- **Gap:** OAD has no NATS integration. Its cognition cycle results are written to Supabase (`automation_events`) and Notion journal pages but never broadcast to the event mesh. The orchestrator cannot react to OAD events in real time.
- **Fix:** Add four new NATS JetStream subjects under the `citadel.oad.*` namespace:
  - `citadel.oad.reflex.applied` — published after every Reflex Engine auto-fix. Payload: `{reflex_id, rig, pattern_code, file_path, fix_description, before_hash, after_hash, timestamp}`
  - `citadel.oad.cognition.completed` — published after every full cognition cycle. Payload: `{cycle_id, rig, thought_summary, compound_analysis, gitlab_status, linear_status, supabase_status, notion_status, college_verdict, timestamp}`
  - `citadel.oad.mission.dispatched` — published when orchestrator dispatches a mission to OAD. Payload: `{mission_id, rig_target, mission_type, payload, priority, dispatched_by, timestamp}`
  - `citadel.oad.mission.completed` — published when OAD completes a dispatched mission. Payload: `{mission_id, rig, result, success, error_detail, duration_ms, timestamp}`
- **Stream config:** Extend existing JetStream stream `VCC_BRIDGE` with subjects `citadel.oad.>`. Retention: limits, max 10000 msgs (up from 5000), max age 30 days. Consumer: durable pull consumer `vcc-oad-consumer` with ack-wait 30s.
- **OAD-side integration:** Add NATS publisher to OAD's `cognition_loop.py` — after each Reflex fix and after each cognition cycle completion, publish to the respective subject. Requires `NATS_URL` env var on rig2.
- **Test:** `test_oad_nats_events.py` — assert all 4 subjects publish valid JSON, consumer receives within 5s, payload schema validates against Pydantic models, reflex event includes valid pattern_code (F924|F950|F960|custom), mission dispatch round-trips correctly.
- **Audit Gate:** CI stage `bridge-oad-nats` verifies all 4 OAD subjects are declared in `crp_config.yaml` `nats_subjects` list. Fails if any subject is missing.
**2.5.2 — OAD Reflex → Orchestrator Feed** `OAD-002`
- **Gap:** OAD's Reflex Engine applies auto-fixes (YAML syntax repair, enum regeneration, broken import resolution) silently. The orchestrator and CRP have no visibility into what OAD fixed. VCC may attempt to fix something OAD already repaired, or Perplexity may file an issue for a problem OAD already resolved.
- **Fix:** Add a NATS subscriber to `loop_orchestrator.py` that listens on `citadel.oad.reflex.applied`. On receipt:
  1. Parse the reflex payload to extract `pattern_code`, `file_path`, `fix_description`
  1. Write to `vcc_loop_state` with `loop_source = 'oad_reflex'` and the fix details
  1. Check shared dedup: if an open Linear/GitLab issue exists for the same file + problem, auto-close it with comment: _"Auto-resolved by OAD Reflex Engine (pattern {code}) in cycle {cycle_id}"_
  1. Inject reflex summary into next CRP §7.7 subsection: **"§7.7 — OAD Reflex Fixes (since last CRP cycle)"** — list of fixes with pattern code, file, and timestamp
  1. If reflex fix count exceeds 5 in a single OAD cycle, flag as `WARNING` — excessive auto-fixes may indicate systemic instability
- **Reflex pattern registry:** Maintain a `REFLEX_PATTERNS` dict in `crp_config.yaml`:
```yaml
oad_reflex_patterns:
  F924:
    name: "YAML Syntax Repair"
    severity: low
    auto_close_issues: true
  F950:
    name: "Enum Regeneration"
    severity: medium
    auto_close_issues: true
  F960:
    name: "Broken Import Resolution"
    severity: medium
    auto_close_issues: true
  custom:
    name: "Custom Reflex Fix"
    severity: high
    auto_close_issues: false  # manual review required
```
- **Test:** `test_oad_reflex_feed.py` — assert reflex event writes to `vcc_loop_state`, matching Linear issue is auto-closed, CRP §7.7 contains reflex summary, >5 fixes triggers WARNING, custom pattern does NOT auto-close issues, dedup correctly matches file path.
- **Audit Gate:** CRP §7.7 must exist after Phase 2.5 deployment. Missing subsection is a **warning** for 3 cycles, then **blocking**.
**2.5.3 — Mission Dispatch Interface** `OAD-003`
- **Gap:** OAD polls `oad_missions` table for work, but no external system dispatches missions to it. The orchestrator cannot ask OAD to investigate a specific failure, run a targeted Reflex fix, or query the College System on demand.
- **Fix:** Create `tools/oad_mission_dispatcher.py` — a mission dispatch interface used by the orchestrator:
  1. **Insert mission** into `oad_missions` table with: `mission_id`, `rig_target` (default: `rig2`), `mission_type` (`reflex_scan`, `college_query`, `pipeline_investigate`, `full_cognition`), `payload` (JSON), `priority` (`low`/`medium`/`high`/`critical`), `dispatched_by` (`orchestrator`), `status` (`pending`)
  1. **Publish** `citadel.oad.mission.dispatched` NATS event
  1. **Wait for completion** — subscribe to `citadel.oad.mission.completed` with a timeout (default 120s for reflex_scan, 300s for college_query, 600s for full_cognition)
  1. **Return result** — parsed mission result or timeout error
- **Mission types:**
  - `reflex_scan` — run Reflex Engine on a specific file or directory. Payload: `{target_path, pattern_codes[]}`
  - `college_query` — submit a reasoning query to the College System. Payload: `{query, context{}, max_professors, vector_search_k}`
  - `pipeline_investigate` — investigate a specific GitLab pipeline failure. Payload: `{pipeline_id, job_id, error_snippet}`
  - `full_cognition` — trigger a full OAD cognition cycle immediately. Payload: `{reason}`
- **Auto-dispatch rules** (in orchestrator):
  - CRP guardrails fail with import errors → auto-dispatch `reflex_scan` with `pattern_codes: ["F960"]`
  - Perplexity detects pipeline failure → auto-dispatch `pipeline_investigate`
  - 3 consecutive CRP NO-GO → auto-dispatch `full_cognition` with reason: _"3 consecutive NO-GO — requesting full OAD analysis"_
  - Merged health score drops below 40 → auto-dispatch `college_query` with context from both CRP and Perplexity latest state
- **Test:** `test_oad_mission_dispatch.py` — assert mission inserts into `oad_missions` table, NATS event publishes, completion callback fires, timeout returns error, auto-dispatch triggers on guardrail failure, priority ordering is respected, duplicate missions within 60s are deduplicated.
- **Audit Gate:** `oad_missions` table must show at least 1 dispatched mission in the last 7 days in production. Zero dispatches triggers a **warning** (orchestrator may not be auto-dispatching).
**2.5.4 — College System Query Interface** `OAD-004`
- **Gap:** OAD's College System (33 professors + FAISS vector DB) is a powerful multi-agent reasoning engine, but it's locked inside OAD's cognition loop. VCC and Perplexity cannot query it for complex analysis (e.g., "Why did the last 3 deployments fail?" or "Is this drift pattern a systemic architecture issue?").
- **Fix:** Create `tools/lib/college_query_client.py` — a client library that dispatches `college_query` missions and parses results:
```python
class CollegeQueryClient:
    """Query OAD's College System via mission dispatch."""
    
    async def query(
        self,
        query: str,
        context: dict | None = None,
        max_professors: int = 5,
        vector_search_k: int = 10,
        timeout_s: int = 300,
    ) -> CollegeQueryResult:
        """Submit a reasoning query to the College System.
        
        Args:
            query: Natural language question for the professors
            context: Optional dict of CRP/Perplexity state for grounding
            max_professors: Number of professors to engage (1-33)
            vector_search_k: Number of FAISS vectors to retrieve
            timeout_s: Timeout in seconds
            
        Returns:
            CollegeQueryResult with verdict, confidence, reasoning chain
        """
```
- **Integration points:**
  - `loop_orchestrator.py` calls `CollegeQueryClient.query()` when merged health drops below 40 — asks the College System to analyze the combined CRP + Perplexity state and recommend remediation
  - `vcc_cycle_reporter.py` can call `CollegeQueryClient.query()` when drift is detected across 3+ consecutive cycles — asks for root cause analysis
  - `guild_auditor.py` can call `CollegeQueryClient.query()` during Phase 5 audit for architecture review
- **Response schema:**
```python
class CollegeQueryResult(BaseModel):
    query_id: str
    verdict: str                    # Summary conclusion
    confidence: float               # 0.0-1.0
    reasoning_chain: list[str]      # Step-by-step reasoning
    professors_consulted: int
    vectors_retrieved: int
    thought_model: str              # "sonar-pro" or similar
    compound_model: str             # "gpt-4o-mini" or similar
    recommendations: list[str]
    duration_ms: int
```
- **Test:** `test_college_query_client.py` — assert query dispatches mission correctly, result parses into `CollegeQueryResult`, timeout returns graceful error, context is passed through to College System, max_professors cap is respected, empty FAISS results produce fallback reasoning.
- **Audit Gate:** College query availability is a **soft dependency** — if OAD is unreachable, orchestrator and CRP degrade gracefully with `"College System unavailable — OAD may be offline"`.
**2.5.5 — Extended Shared Dedup (v2.5)** `OAD-005`
- **Gap:** Phase 2.1 dedup (`issue_dedup.py`) only handles CRP (`[CRP]`) and Perplexity (`[CLv2]`) prefixed issues. OAD creates its own Linear tickets (unprefixed or with OAD-specific tags) when it detects failures. Three loops filing issues independently means triple-duplicate risk.
- **Fix:** Extend `tools/lib/issue_dedup.py` to v2.5:
  1. Add `[OAD]` prefix recognition alongside `[CRP]` and `[CLv2]`
  1. When OAD Reflex auto-fixes a problem, check for matching `[CRP]` and `[CLv2]` issues — if found, comment: _"Auto-resolved by OAD Reflex Engine (pattern {code})"_ and add `resolved-by-oad` label
  1. When CRP or Perplexity creates an issue, check for matching OAD-originated issues — if found, append cross-reference comment
  1. **OAD Linear token fix:** OAD's Linear integration currently shows `"status": "error"` (API token/team_id issue). Phase 2.5 adds a fallback: if OAD can't create Linear issues directly, the orchestrator creates them on OAD's behalf with `[OAD]` prefix using the bridge's `LINEAR_API_TOKEN`
  1. Rate limit: max 5 new issues per loop per cycle (now applies to 3 loops — 15 total max)
- **Dedup rules (extended):**
  - Title similarity threshold: 0.75 (unchanged)
  - Same `root_cause_category` tag → automatic match (unchanged)
  - OAD Reflex `pattern_code` + `file_path` match → automatic match (new)
  - Issues closed within last 24h excluded (unchanged)
  - Cross-loop labels: `confirmed-by-crp`, `confirmed-by-perplexity`, `confirmed-by-oad`, `resolved-by-oad`
- **Test:** `test_oad_dedup_v25.py` — assert OAD prefix recognized, reflex auto-fix closes matching issues, 3-way cross-reference works, OAD Linear fallback creates issues via orchestrator, rate limit enforced at 5 per loop per cycle.
- **Audit Gate:** CI stage `bridge-dedup-v25` runs `issue_dedup.py --audit --include-oad`. Warns if triple-duplicate issues found.
**2.5.6 — Extended State Store (v2.5)** `OAD-006`
- **Gap:** `public.vcc_loop_state` (Phase 2.1) only stores `crp`, `perplexity`, and `orchestrator` sources. No schema support for OAD cognition data, reflex fix history, or mission dispatch results.
- **Fix:** Extend `vcc_loop_state` with OAD columns and add `vcc_loop_state_history` for trend analysis:
```sql
-- Add OAD columns to existing vcc_loop_state
ALTER TABLE public.vcc_loop_state 
    ALTER COLUMN loop_source SET DATA TYPE TEXT,
    DROP CONSTRAINT IF EXISTS vcc_loop_state_loop_source_check;

ALTER TABLE public.vcc_loop_state 
    ADD CONSTRAINT vcc_loop_state_loop_source_check 
    CHECK (loop_source IN ('crp', 'perplexity', 'orchestrator', 'oad_reflex', 'oad_cognition', 'oad_mission'));

ALTER TABLE public.vcc_loop_state ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS
    oad_rig TEXT CHECK (oad_rig IN ('rig1', 'rig2', 'rig3'));
ALTER TABLE public.vcc_loop_state ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS

ALTER TABLE public.vcc_loop_state ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS
    oad_reflex_count INT DEFAULT 0;
ALTER TABLE public.vcc_loop_state ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS
    oad_gitlab_status TEXT;
ALTER TABLE public.vcc_loop_state ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS
    oad_linear_status TEXT;
ALTER TABLE public.vcc_loop_state ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS
    oad_thought_summary TEXT;
ALTER TABLE public.vcc_loop_state ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS
    oad_compound_analysis TEXT;
ALTER TABLE public.vcc_loop_state ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS
    oad_college_verdict TEXT;
ALTER TABLE public.vcc_loop_state ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS
    oad_mission_id TEXT;
ALTER TABLE public.vcc_loop_state ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS
    oad_mission_result JSONB;
ALTER TABLE public.vcc_loop_state ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS
    oad_snapshot JSONB DEFAULT '{}';

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_vcc_loop_state_oad_rig 
    ON public.vcc_loop_state(oad_rig) WHERE loop_source LIKE 'oad_%';
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_vcc_loop_state_oad_reflex 
    ON public.vcc_loop_state(oad_reflex_count) WHERE loop_source = 'oad_reflex';

-- History table for cross-loop trend analysis
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS public.vcc_loop_state_history (
    id UUID DEFAULT gen_random_uuid() PRIMARY KEY,
    state_id UUID REFERENCES public.vcc_loop_state(id),
    loop_source TEXT NOT NULL,
    cycle_id TEXT NOT NULL,
    health_grade TEXT,

CREATE INDEX idx_vcc_history_created ON public.vcc_loop_state_history(created_at DESC);
```
- **Write rules (extended):**
  - OAD Reflex writes one row per auto-fix batch with `loop_source = 'oad_reflex'`
  - OAD Cognition writes one row per cycle with `loop_source = 'oad_cognition'`
  - OAD Mission writes one row per completed mission with `loop_source = 'oad_mission'`
  - Orchestrator v2.5 merges all four sources (CRP + Perplexity + OAD) into `loop_source = 'orchestrator'`
  - Every write also inserts a summary row into `vcc_loop_state_history` for trend analysis
- **OAD snapshot storage:** The `oad_snapshot` JSONB column stores the full OAD snapshot structure: `{rig, ts, gitlab{}, linear{}, supabase{}, notion{}, thought{}, compound{}}`
- **Test:** `test_oad_state_store_v25.py` — assert OAD reflex write validates, OAD cognition write validates, mission result write validates, orchestrator v2.5 merge includes OAD data, history table receives entries, `oad_rig` constraint enforces valid rig names.
- **Audit Gate:** `vcc_loop_state` must have at least 1 OAD-sourced row within the last 2 hours in production (OAD cycles every 5-15 min). Missing OAD rows trigger a **warning** — OAD may be offline on rig2.
**2.5.7 — Trilateral Orchestrator (v2.5)** `OAD-007`
- **Gap:** `loop_orchestrator.py` (Phase 2.1) only coordinates CRP and Perplexity. It has no awareness of OAD's cognition cycle, reflex fixes, or mission completions. The GO/NO-GO verdict doesn't factor in OAD's operational health.
- **Fix:** Upgrade `loop_orchestrator.py` to v2.5 — trilateral coordinator:
  1. **Subscribe** to all 6 NATS subjects: `citadel.vcc.cycle.completed`, `citadel.diagnostic.completed`, `citadel.vcc.build.pause`, `citadel.vcc.build.resume`, `citadel.oad.reflex.applied`, `citadel.oad.cognition.completed`
  1. **On OAD Reflex event:** log fix to `vcc_loop_state`, run dedup against open CRP/Perplexity issues, inject into next CRP §7.7
  1. **On OAD Cognition event:** read OAD snapshot, merge with latest CRP + Perplexity state, write trilateral merged row, evaluate GO/NO-GO
  1. **Extended GO/NO-GO rules (v2.5):**
    - Perplexity `CRITICAL` → `NO-GO` (unchanged)
    - CRP guardrails failed → `NO-GO` (unchanged)
    - CRP drift dirty → `NO-GO` (unchanged)
    - Perplexity `DEGRADING` + score < 50 → `NO-GO` (unchanged)
    - OAD gitlab_status = `"error"` for 3+ consecutive cycles → `NO-GO` (new)
    - OAD reflex_count > 10 in single cycle → `WARNING` (new — excessive self-healing)
    - OAD cognition cycle missing for > 30 minutes → `WARNING` (new — OAD may be down)
    - OAD College System unreachable for > 1 hour → `WARNING` (new — reasoning degraded)
    - All three loops HEALTHY + OAD reflex_count = 0 → `GO` (optimal state)
  1. **Auto-dispatch integration:**
    - On CRP NO-GO with import errors → dispatch `reflex_scan` mission to OAD
    - On Perplexity CRITICAL with pipeline failure → dispatch `pipeline_investigate` mission to OAD
    - On 3 consecutive trilateral NO-GO → dispatch `full_cognition` + `college_query` asking: _"3 consecutive NO-GO across VCC, Perplexity, and OAD. Analyze combined state and recommend recovery plan."_
  1. **Notion reporting (extended):** Summary callout every 6 hours now includes OAD status: last cognition cycle, reflex fix count, active missions, College System availability, rig status.
- **Test:** `test_oad_orchestrator_v25.py` — assert OAD reflex event triggers dedup, OAD cognition event triggers merge, OAD gitlab error → NO-GO after 3 cycles, excessive reflex → WARNING, missing cognition → WARNING, auto-dispatch fires on import errors, trilateral merge produces correct GO/NO-GO, orchestrator survives OAD being offline.
- **Audit Gate:** Orchestrator must write at least 1 trilateral merged row (containing OAD data) to `vcc_loop_state` in the last 24 hours. Missing trilateral merges is **blocking** — bridge is not fully connected.
**2.5.8 — CRP v2.5 Schema Extensions** `OAD-008`
- **Gap:** CRP v2.1 schema has no fields for OAD cognition data, reflex fix history, mission dispatch results, or College System queries. Adding OAD integration requires a schema version bump.
- **Fix:** Bump CRP to v2.5. Add to `CycleReport` dataclass:
  - `crp_version: str = "2.5"` (up from `"2.1"`)
  - `oad_cognition: dict | None = None` — latest OAD cognition snapshot
  - `oad_reflex_fixes: list[dict] = []` — reflex fixes since last CRP cycle
  - `oad_reflex_count: int = 0` — total reflex fixes since last CRP cycle
  - `oad_missions_dispatched: list[dict] = []` — missions dispatched by orchestrator
  - `oad_missions_completed: list[dict] = []` — mission results received
  - `oad_college_query: dict | None = None` — last College System query result (if any)
  - `oad_rig_status: dict = {}` — `{"rig1": "standby", "rig2": "active", "rig3": "standby"}`
  - `trilateral_go_no_go: str | None = None` — from orchestrator v2.5 merged snapshot
  - `trilateral_health_score: int | None = None`
  - `trilateral_blockers: list[str] = []`
- **CRP §7 extensions (v2.5):**
  - §7.7 — OAD Status (new): OAD cognition cycle summary, reflex fix list, rig status, gitlab/linear/supabase status from OAD snapshot, College System availability
  - §7.8 — Trilateral Health (new): combined GO/NO-GO from all 3 loops, merged score, blocking reasons from VCC + Perplexity + OAD, auto-dispatch summary
  - §7.9 — Learning Report (new): output of `LearningEngine.run_learning_cycle()` — new/updated failure signatures, cross-loop correlations found, fix effectiveness verdicts, adaptive advisories issued, top recurring failures, risk-ranked SRS codes, health trend (improving/degrading). Generated by `get_crp_section_79()` in `tools/vcc_learning_engine.py` (§17.2)
  - §7.4-§7.6 — unchanged from v2.1
- **CitadelHealthSnapshot v2.5 extensions:**

```python
class OADHealth(BaseModel):

```
- **CRP validator update:** `crp_validator.py` v2.5 requires §7.7, §7.8, and §7.9 subsections. Reports without these are **rejected** after the 3-cycle grace period. v2.1 reports are accepted during grace period.
- **Test:** `test_oad_crp_v25.py` — assert v2.5 schema validates with OAD fields, v2.1 reports accepted during grace, v2.1 reports rejected after grace, §7.7/§7.8 render correctly in Notion toggle block, OADHealth model validates with partial data, trilateral GO/NO-GO computation uses worst-of-three-sources rule.
