1. ✅ `loop_orchestrator.py` v2.5 running as persistent service producing trilateral merged snapshots
1. ✅ OAD Reflex events feed into orchestrator and auto-close matching issues (verified in logs)
1. ✅ Mission dispatch interface operational — orchestrator can dispatch and receive mission results from OAD
1. ✅ College System query interface available to orchestrator, CRP, and guild auditor
1. ✅ Shared dedup v2.5 prevents triple-duplicate Linear/GitLab issues across all 3 loops
1. ✅ `CitadelHealthSnapshot` v2.5 schema validates for CRP-only, Perplexity-only, OAD-only, and merged snapshots
1. ✅ Trilateral NO-GO auto-pause triggers correctly with OAD data factored in (verified in staging)
1. ✅ `NATS_URL` configured on OAD rig2 and publishing events successfully
1. ✅ All test files pass (`pytest tests/phase25/ -v`)
1. ✅ All bridge + OAD components added to `.gitlab-ci.yml` pipeline (see Appendix I)

[CALLOUT] 🚨 **Phase 2.5 completes the build→inspect→maintain triad.** Without OAD integration, the orchestrator only coordinates build-time (VCC) and diagnostic (Perplexity) loops — operational maintenance runs blind. OAD's Reflex Engine self-heals problems that neither VCC nor Perplexity can fix, and its College System provides multi-agent reasoning that no single loop can match. All three loops MUST be connected. There are no exceptions.


---


### §17 — Trilateral Learning Engine (Perplexity + VCC + OAD)


[CALLOUT] 🧬 **Purpose:** §17 adds a **learning engine** that ingests, correlates, and learns from the outputs of all three autonomous loops — Perplexity Control Loop (diagnostics), VCC CRP (build results), and OAD (cognition + reflex). Today each loop produces rich output but none of them learn from the other two. The Learning Engine creates a **closed feedback loop** where recurring patterns are detected, failure signatures are cataloged, fix effectiveness is measured, and build decisions are improved cycle-over-cycle. This is the intelligence layer that makes the trilateral system self-improving.

**§17.0 — Architecture Overview**
```mermaid
flowchart TB
    subgraph INPUTS["Loop Outputs (Ingestion)"]
        CRP_IN["VCC CRP Cycle Reports\n§1-§8 per cycle"]
        PPLX_IN["Perplexity Diagnostics\nhealth grade + blockers + recommendations"]
        OAD_IN["OAD Cognition Snapshots\nreflex fixes + college verdicts + pipeline status"]
    end

    subgraph ENGINE["§17 Learning Engine"]
        INGEST["1. Ingest & Normalize\nvcc_learning_engine.py"]
        CORRELATE["2. Cross-Loop Correlator\npattern detection across loops"]
        CATALOG["3. Failure Signature Catalog\nfingerprint recurring issues"]
        MEASURE["4. Fix Effectiveness Tracker\nwas the fix actually effective?"]
        DECIDE["5. Adaptive Decision Engine\nadjust build priorities + thresholds"]
    end

    subgraph OUTPUTS["Learning Outputs"]
        STORE["vcc_learning_store\nSupabase table"]
        CRP_OUT["CRP §7.9 — Learning Report\ninjected into every cycle report"]
        ORCH_OUT["Orchestrator Advisories\nadjusted GO/NO-GO thresholds"]
        VCC_OUT["VCC Build Priority Adjustments\nre-rank SRS codes by risk"]
    end

    CRP_IN --> INGEST
    PPLX_IN --> INGEST
    OAD_IN --> INGEST
    INGEST --> CORRELATE
    CORRELATE --> CATALOG
    CATALOG --> MEASURE
    MEASURE --> DECIDE
    DECIDE --> STORE
    DECIDE --> CRP_OUT
    DECIDE --> ORCH_OUT
    DECIDE --> VCC_OUT
```
**§17.1 — Supabase Schema — **`**public.vcc_learning_store**`
```sql
-- Learning store: captures cross-loop correlations, failure signatures, and adaptive decisions
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS public.vcc_learning_store (
    id UUID DEFAULT gen_random_uuid() PRIMARY KEY,
    learning_id TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,           -- "LEARN-{YYYYMMDD}-{HHMM}-{SEQ}"
    learning_type TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (learning_type IN (
        'failure_signature',    -- recurring failure pattern fingerprint
        'correlation',          -- cross-loop cause-effect relationship
        'fix_effectiveness',    -- did a fix actually resolve the issue?
        'threshold_adjustment', -- adaptive threshold change
        'priority_adjustment',  -- SRS code priority re-ranking
        'pattern_detection'     -- new pattern discovered across loops
    )),
    
    -- Source context
    source_loops JSONB NOT NULL DEFAULT '[]',   -- ["crp", "perplexity", "oad"] which loops contributed
    source_cycle_ids JSONB NOT NULL DEFAULT '[]', -- cycle IDs that triggered this learning
    
    -- Failure signature fields
    failure_fingerprint TEXT,                    -- hash of normalized failure pattern
    failure_category TEXT,                       -- "import_error", "rls_leak", "pipeline_fail", etc.
    failure_frequency INT DEFAULT 1,             -- how many times this pattern recurred
    first_seen_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    last_seen_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    mean_time_to_detect_s INT,                   -- avg seconds from occurrence to detection
    mean_time_to_fix_s INT,                      -- avg seconds from detection to resolution
    
    -- Correlation fields
    cause_loop TEXT,                             -- which loop detected the root cause
    effect_loop TEXT,                            -- which loop saw the downstream effect
    cause_event JSONB DEFAULT '{}',              -- the triggering event details
    effect_event JSONB DEFAULT '{}',             -- the downstream effect details
    correlation_confidence FLOAT DEFAULT 0.0,    -- 0.0-1.0 confidence in the correlation
    
    -- Fix effectiveness fields
    fix_source TEXT,                             -- "oad_reflex", "vcc_build", "manual", "perplexity_recommendation"
    fix_description TEXT,
    fix_resolved BOOLEAN,                        -- did the fix actually resolve the issue?
    fix_regression BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,        -- did the fix introduce a new problem?
    fix_duration_s INT,                          -- how long the fix took
    cycles_to_verify INT DEFAULT 0,              -- how many cycles before we confirmed resolution
    
    -- Adaptive decision fields
    old_threshold JSONB DEFAULT '{}',            -- previous threshold value
    new_threshold JSONB DEFAULT '{}',            -- adjusted threshold value
    adjustment_reason TEXT,                      -- why the threshold was changed
    adjustment_confidence FLOAT DEFAULT 0.0,     -- confidence in the adjustment
    
    -- Priority adjustment fields
    srs_code TEXT,                               -- SRS code being re-prioritized
    old_priority INT,                            -- previous priority rank
    new_priority INT,                            -- new priority rank
    risk_score FLOAT DEFAULT 0.0,                -- computed risk score driving the change
    
    -- Pattern detection fields
    pattern_name TEXT,                           -- human-readable pattern name
    pattern_description TEXT,                    -- what the pattern means
    pattern_occurrences INT DEFAULT 0,           -- how many times observed
    pattern_loops JSONB DEFAULT '[]',            -- which loops contributed to detection
    
    -- Meta
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
    expires_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT (NOW() + INTERVAL '180 days'),
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE
);

CREATE INDEX idx_learning_type ON public.vcc_learning_store(learning_type);
CREATE INDEX idx_learning_fingerprint ON public.vcc_learning_store(failure_fingerprint) WHERE learning_type = 'failure_signature';
CREATE INDEX idx_learning_created ON public.vcc_learning_store(created_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_learning_active ON public.vcc_learning_store(is_active) WHERE is_active = TRUE;
CREATE INDEX idx_learning_srs ON public.vcc_learning_store(srs_code) WHERE srs_code IS NOT NULL;
```
**§17.2 — Full Implementation — **`**tools/vcc_learning_engine.py**`
Place at `tools/vcc_learning_engine.py`. This is the core learning engine that VCC, the orchestrator, and CRP all call.
```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""VCC Trilateral Learning Engine — Process & Learn from Perplexity, VCC, and OAD.

Ingests outputs from all three loops, detects patterns, catalogs failure signatures,
measures fix effectiveness, and produces adaptive decisions that improve VCC build
quality over time.

Usage:
    # As a library (called by orchestrator, CRP, or VCC)
    from tools.vcc_learning_engine import LearningEngine
    engine = LearningEngine()
    await engine.ingest_crp_cycle(cycle_report)
    await engine.ingest_perplexity_diagnostic(diagnostic)
    await engine.ingest_oad_cognition(snapshot)
    learnings = await engine.run_learning_cycle()

    # As CLI
    python tools/vcc_learning_engine.py --run-cycle
    python tools/vcc_learning_engine.py --report
    python tools/vcc_learning_engine.py --export-advisories
"""

import os
import json
import hashlib
import logging
from datetime import datetime, timezone, timedelta
from dataclasses import dataclass, field, asdict
from typing import Optional, Literal
from collections import Counter, defaultdict

import requests
from pydantic import BaseModel, Field

logger = logging.getLogger("vcc_learning_engine")

# ── Config ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
SUPABASE_URL = os.environ.get("SUPABASE_URL", "")
SUPABASE_KEY = os.environ.get("SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY", "")
NOTION_API = "https://api.notion.com/v1"
NOTION_TOKEN = os.environ.get("NOTION_INTERNAL_TOKEN", "")
NOTION_VERSION = "2022-06-28"
DD_API_KEY = os.environ.get("DD_API_KEY", "")
DD_SITE = os.environ.get("DD_SITE", "us5.datadoghq.com")
PH_API_KEY = os.environ.get("POSTHOG_API_KEY", "")
PH_HOST = os.environ.get("POSTHOG_HOST", "https://app.posthog.com")

# Tunable thresholds — overridable via env
CORRELATION_CONFIDENCE_THRESHOLD = float(os.environ.get("LEARN_CORR_THRESHOLD", "0.6"))
FAILURE_RECURRENCE_THRESHOLD = int(os.environ.get("LEARN_FAIL_RECUR", "3"))
FIX_VERIFY_CYCLES = int(os.environ.get("LEARN_FIX_VERIFY_CYCLES", "3"))
ADAPTIVE_LOOKBACK_CYCLES = int(os.environ.get("LEARN_LOOKBACK", "20"))
RISK_SCORE_WEIGHTS = {
    "failure_frequency": 0.3,
    "mean_time_to_fix": 0.25,
    "correlation_count": 0.2,
    "regression_rate": 0.25,
}


# ── Pydantic Models ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
class NormalizedLoopEvent(BaseModel):
    """Unified event from any of the 3 loops."""
    event_id: str
    source_loop: Literal["crp", "perplexity", "oad_reflex", "oad_cognition"]
    cycle_id: str
    timestamp: str
    event_type: str               # "guardrail_violation", "health_degradation", "reflex_fix", etc.
    severity: Literal["low", "medium", "high", "critical"]
    category: str                 # "import_error", "rls_leak", "pipeline_fail", etc.
    description: str
    affected_files: list[str] = []
    affected_srs_codes: list[str] = []
    metrics: dict = {}            # loop-specific metrics
    raw_payload: dict = {}        # original event for audit


class FailureSignature(BaseModel):
    """Fingerprinted recurring failure pattern."""
    fingerprint: str
    category: str
    canonical_description: str
    occurrences: list[dict] = []  # [{cycle_id, loop, timestamp, description}]
    frequency: int = 0
    first_seen: str = ""
    last_seen: str = ""
    mean_time_to_detect_s: int = 0
    mean_time_to_fix_s: int = 0
    resolved: bool = False
    resolution_fix: str | None = None


class CrossLoopCorrelation(BaseModel):
    """Detected cause-effect relationship across loops."""
    correlation_id: str
    cause_loop: str
    cause_event: dict
    effect_loop: str
    effect_event: dict
    confidence: float = 0.0
    explanation: str = ""
    verified: bool = False


class FixEffectivenessRecord(BaseModel):
    """Tracks whether a fix actually worked."""
    fix_id: str
    fix_source: str               # "oad_reflex", "vcc_build", "manual"
    fix_description: str
    target_fingerprint: str       # failure signature it targeted
    applied_at: str
    resolved: bool = False
    regression_introduced: bool = False
    cycles_monitored: int = 0
    verification_status: Literal["pending", "verified_resolved", "verified_failed", "regression"] = "pending"


class AdaptiveAdvisory(BaseModel):
    """Output advisory that adjusts VCC/orchestrator behavior."""
    advisory_id: str
    advisory_type: Literal[
        "threshold_adjustment",
        "priority_rerank",
        "build_pause_recommendation",
        "fix_recommendation",
        "pattern_alert",
    ]
    target: str                   # what is being adjusted
    old_value: dict = {}
    new_value: dict = {}
    reason: str
    confidence: float = 0.0
    auto_apply: bool = False      # if True, orchestrator applies automatically


class LearningCycleReport(BaseModel):
    """Output of a full learning cycle — injected into CRP §7.9."""
    learning_cycle_id: str
    timestamp: str
    events_ingested: int = 0
    events_by_loop: dict = {}     # {"crp": N, "perplexity": N, "oad": N}
    new_signatures: int = 0
    updated_signatures: int = 0
    correlations_found: int = 0
    fixes_verified: int = 0
    fixes_failed: int = 0
    regressions_detected: int = 0
    advisories_issued: list[AdaptiveAdvisory] = []
    top_recurring_failures: list[dict] = []   # top 5 by frequency
    risk_ranked_srs_codes: list[dict] = []    # SRS codes ranked by risk
    health_trend: dict = {}       # {"improving": bool, "score_delta": int}


# ── Supabase Client ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
class SupabaseClient:
    """Minimal Supabase REST client for learning store operations."""

    def __init__(self):
        self.base_url = f"{SUPABASE_URL}/rest/v1"
        self.headers = {
            "apikey": SUPABASE_KEY,
            "Authorization": f"Bearer {SUPABASE_KEY}",
            "Content-Type": "application/json",
            "Prefer": "return=representation",
        }

    def query_learning_store(
        self,
        learning_type: str | None = None,
        active_only: bool = True,
        limit: int = 100,
        since_days: int = 30,
    ) -> list[dict]:
        """Query vcc_learning_store with filters."""
        url = f"{self.base_url}/vcc_learning_store"
        params = {"order": "created_at.desc", "limit": str(limit)}
        filters = []
        if learning_type:
            filters.append(f"learning_type=eq.{learning_type}")
        if active_only:
            filters.append("is_active=eq.true")
        cutoff = (datetime.now(timezone.utc) - timedelta(days=since_days)).isoformat()
        filters.append(f"created_at=gte.{cutoff}")
        if filters:
            params["and"] = f"({','.join(filters)})"
        resp = requests.get(url, headers=self.headers, params=params)
        resp.raise_for_status()
        return resp.json()

    def upsert_learning(self, record: dict) -> dict:
        """Upsert a learning record by learning_id."""
        url = f"{self.base_url}/vcc_learning_store"
        headers = {**self.headers, "Prefer": "resolution=merge-duplicates,return=representation"}
        resp = requests.post(url, headers=headers, json=record)
        resp.raise_for_status()
        return resp.json()

    def query_loop_state(
        self,
        loop_source: str | None = None,
        limit: int = 50,
    ) -> list[dict]:
        """Read from vcc_loop_state for cross-loop correlation."""
        url = f"{self.base_url}/vcc_loop_state"
        params = {"order": "created_at.desc", "limit": str(limit)}
        if loop_source:
            params["loop_source"] = f"eq.{loop_source}"
        resp = requests.get(url, headers=self.headers, params=params)
        resp.raise_for_status()
        return resp.json()


# ── Core Learning Engine ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
class LearningEngine:
    """Trilateral Learning Engine — ingests, correlates, and learns from all 3 loops."""

    def __init__(self):
        self.db = SupabaseClient()
        self.events_buffer: list[NormalizedLoopEvent] = []
        self.signatures: dict[str, FailureSignature] = {}  # fingerprint -> signature
        self.correlations: list[CrossLoopCorrelation] = []
        self.pending_fixes: list[FixEffectivenessRecord] = []
        self.advisories: list[AdaptiveAdvisory] = []

    # ── 1. INGEST & NORMALIZE ───────────────────────────────────────────

    def ingest_crp_cycle(self, cycle_report: dict) -> list[NormalizedLoopEvent]:
        """Ingest a VCC CRP cycle report and extract events.

        Extracts: guardrail violations, drift detections, test failures,
        SLA breaches, health check failures, SRS completion status.
        """
        events = []
        cycle_id = cycle_report.get("cycle_id", "unknown")
        ts = cycle_report.get("timestamp", datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat())

        # Extract guardrail violations
        for v in cycle_report.get("guardrail_violations", []):
            events.append(NormalizedLoopEvent(
                event_id=f"crp-guard-{cycle_id}-{v.get('rule', 'unknown')}",
                source_loop="crp",
                cycle_id=cycle_id,
                timestamp=ts,
                event_type="guardrail_violation",
                severity=self._severity_from_guardrail(v),
                category=v.get("rule", "unknown"),
                description=v.get("message", "Guardrail violation detected"),
                affected_files=v.get("files", []),
                affected_srs_codes=v.get("srs_codes", []),
                metrics={"violation_count": v.get("count", 1)},
                raw_payload=v,
            ))

        # Extract test failures
        for t in cycle_report.get("test_failures", []):
            events.append(NormalizedLoopEvent(
                event_id=f"crp-test-{cycle_id}-{t.get('test_name', 'unknown')}",
                source_loop="crp",
                cycle_id=cycle_id,
                timestamp=ts,
                event_type="test_failure",
                severity="high" if "rls" in t.get("test_name", "").lower() else "medium",
                category=self._categorize_test_failure(t),
                description=t.get("message", "Test failure"),
                affected_files=[t.get("file", "")],
                affected_srs_codes=t.get("srs_codes", []),
                raw_payload=t,
            ))

        # Extract drift detections
        for layer, status in cycle_report.get("drift_check", {}).items():
            if not status.get("clean", True):
                events.append(NormalizedLoopEvent(
                    event_id=f"crp-drift-{cycle_id}-{layer}",
                    source_loop="crp",
                    cycle_id=cycle_id,
                    timestamp=ts,
                    event_type="drift_detection",
                    severity="high",
                    category=f"drift_{layer}",
                    description=f"Drift detected in {layer} layer: {status.get('details', '')}",
                    metrics={"drift_items": status.get("count", 0)},
                    raw_payload=status,
                ))

        # Extract health check failures
        for svc in cycle_report.get("health_status", {}).get("services", []):
            if svc.get("status") != "healthy":
                events.append(NormalizedLoopEvent(
                    event_id=f"crp-health-{cycle_id}-{svc.get('service_id', 'unknown')}",
                    source_loop="crp",
                    cycle_id=cycle_id,
                    timestamp=ts,
                    event_type="health_degradation",
                    severity="critical" if svc.get("consecutive_failures", 0) >= 3 else "high",
                    category="service_health",
                    description=f"{svc.get('service_id')} is {svc.get('status')}",
                    metrics=svc,
                    raw_payload=svc,
                ))

        # Extract SLA breaches
        for breach in cycle_report.get("sla_breaches", []):
            events.append(NormalizedLoopEvent(
                event_id=f"crp-sla-{cycle_id}-{breach.get('service', 'unknown')}",
                source_loop="crp",
                cycle_id=cycle_id,
                timestamp=ts,
                event_type="sla_breach",
                severity="high",
                category="sla_violation",
                description=f"SLA breach: {breach.get('metric')} = {breach.get('value')} (threshold: {breach.get('threshold')})",
                metrics=breach,
                raw_payload=breach,
            ))

        self.events_buffer.extend(events)
        logger.info(f"[INGEST] CRP cycle {cycle_id}: {len(events)} events extracted")
        return events

    def ingest_perplexity_diagnostic(self, diagnostic: dict) -> list[NormalizedLoopEvent]:
        """Ingest a Perplexity Control Loop v2 diagnostic and extract events.

        Extracts: health grade changes, blocker detections, infrastructure alerts,
        DORA metric degradations, revenue anomalies, L3 adversarial findings.
        """
        events = []
        diag_id = diagnostic.get("diag_id", "unknown")
        ts = diagnostic.get("timestamp", datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat())
        grade = diagnostic.get("health_grade", "UNKNOWN")
        score = diagnostic.get("health_score", 0)

        # Health grade event
        if grade in ("DEGRADING", "CRITICAL"):
            events.append(NormalizedLoopEvent(
                event_id=f"pplx-grade-{diag_id}",
                source_loop="perplexity",
                cycle_id=diag_id,
                timestamp=ts,
                event_type="health_degradation",
                severity="critical" if grade == "CRITICAL" else "high",
                category="overall_health",
                description=f"System health: {grade} (score: {score}/100)",
                metrics={"grade": grade, "score": score},
                raw_payload=diagnostic,
            ))

        # Blockers
        for blocker in diagnostic.get("blockers", []):
            events.append(NormalizedLoopEvent(
                event_id=f"pplx-blocker-{diag_id}-{hashlib.md5(blocker.encode()).hexdigest()[:8]}",
                source_loop="perplexity",
                cycle_id=diag_id,
                timestamp=ts,
                event_type="blocker_detected",
                severity="critical",
                category=self._categorize_blocker(blocker),
                description=blocker,
                metrics={"health_score": score},
                raw_payload={"blocker": blocker},
            ))

        # Infrastructure alerts from sources_read
        infra = diagnostic.get("infrastructure", {})
        if infra.get("alerting_monitors", 0) > 0:
            events.append(NormalizedLoopEvent(
                event_id=f"pplx-infra-{diag_id}",
                source_loop="perplexity",
                cycle_id=diag_id,
                timestamp=ts,
                event_type="infrastructure_alert",
                severity="high",
                category="infrastructure",
                description=f"{infra['alerting_monitors']} Datadog monitors alerting",
                metrics=infra,
                raw_payload=infra,
            ))

        # DORA metric degradation
        code_health = diagnostic.get("code_health", {})
        if code_health.get("change_failure_rate", 0) > 15:  # > 15% is concerning
            events.append(NormalizedLoopEvent(
                event_id=f"pplx-dora-{diag_id}",
                source_loop="perplexity",
                cycle_id=diag_id,
                timestamp=ts,
                event_type="dora_degradation",
                severity="high",
                category="code_quality",
                description=f"Change failure rate: {code_health['change_failure_rate']}%",
                metrics=code_health,
                raw_payload=code_health,
            ))

        # Revenue anomalies
        revenue = diagnostic.get("revenue", {})
        if revenue.get("past_due_subscriptions", 0) > 0:
            events.append(NormalizedLoopEvent(
                event_id=f"pplx-rev-{diag_id}",
                source_loop="perplexity",
                cycle_id=diag_id,
                timestamp=ts,
                event_type="revenue_anomaly",
                severity="medium",
                category="revenue",
                description=f"{revenue['past_due_subscriptions']} subscriptions past due",
                metrics=revenue,
                raw_payload=revenue,
            ))

        # L3 adversarial verdict
        l3 = diagnostic.get("l3_verdict", "")
        if l3 and "critical" in l3.lower():
            events.append(NormalizedLoopEvent(
                event_id=f"pplx-l3-{diag_id}",
                source_loop="perplexity",
                cycle_id=diag_id,
                timestamp=ts,
                event_type="adversarial_finding",
                severity="critical",
                category="adversarial_gate",
                description=f"L3 Opus adversarial finding: {l3[:200]}",
                raw_payload={"l3_verdict": l3},
            ))

        self.events_buffer.extend(events)
        logger.info(f"[INGEST] Perplexity diagnostic {diag_id}: {len(events)} events extracted")
        return events

    def ingest_oad_cognition(self, snapshot: dict) -> list[NormalizedLoopEvent]:
        """Ingest an OAD cognition snapshot and extract events.

        Extracts: reflex auto-fixes, pipeline failures, college verdicts,
        mission completions, Linear/GitLab status errors.
        """
        events = []
        cycle_id = snapshot.get("cycle_id", f"oad-{datetime.now(timezone.utc).strftime('%Y%m%d%H%M')}")
        ts = snapshot.get("ts", datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat())
        rig = snapshot.get("rig", "rig2")

        # Reflex fixes
        for fix in snapshot.get("reflex_fixes", []):
            events.append(NormalizedLoopEvent(
                event_id=f"oad-reflex-{cycle_id}-{fix.get('pattern_code', 'custom')}-{fix.get('file_path', '')[:30]}",
                source_loop="oad_reflex",
                cycle_id=cycle_id,
                timestamp=fix.get("timestamp", ts),
                event_type="reflex_auto_fix",
                severity=self._reflex_severity(fix.get("pattern_code", "custom")),
                category=f"reflex_{fix.get('pattern_code', 'custom')}",
                description=fix.get("fix_description", "OAD Reflex auto-fix applied"),
                affected_files=[fix.get("file_path", "")],
                metrics={"pattern_code": fix.get("pattern_code"), "rig": rig},
                raw_payload=fix,
            ))

        # Pipeline failures from GitLab status
        gitlab = snapshot.get("gitlab", {})
        if gitlab.get("status") == "error" or gitlab.get("failed_pipelines", 0) > 0:
            events.append(NormalizedLoopEvent(
                event_id=f"oad-pipeline-{cycle_id}",
                source_loop="oad_cognition",
                cycle_id=cycle_id,
                timestamp=ts,
                event_type="pipeline_failure",
                severity="high",
                category="ci_cd",
                description=f"GitLab pipeline failure detected by OAD on {rig}",
                metrics=gitlab,
                raw_payload=gitlab,
            ))

        # College System verdicts
        college = snapshot.get("compound", {})
        if college.get("verdict") and "critical" in str(college.get("verdict", "")).lower():
            events.append(NormalizedLoopEvent(
                event_id=f"oad-college-{cycle_id}",
                source_loop="oad_cognition",
                cycle_id=cycle_id,
                timestamp=ts,
                event_type="college_critical_finding",
                severity="critical",
                category="multi_agent_analysis",
                description=f"College System critical finding: {str(college.get('verdict', ''))[:200]}",
                metrics={"professors_consulted": college.get("professors", 0)},
                raw_payload=college,
            ))

        # Linear status error (known issue)
        linear = snapshot.get("linear", {})
        if linear.get("status") == "error":
            events.append(NormalizedLoopEvent(
                event_id=f"oad-linear-{cycle_id}",
                source_loop="oad_cognition",
                cycle_id=cycle_id,
                timestamp=ts,
                event_type="integration_error",
                severity="medium",
                category="linear_integration",
                description="OAD Linear integration error (API token/team_id issue)",
                metrics=linear,
                raw_payload=linear,
            ))

        # Mission completions
        for mission in snapshot.get("missions_completed", []):
            if not mission.get("success", True):
                events.append(NormalizedLoopEvent(
                    event_id=f"oad-mission-{mission.get('mission_id', cycle_id)}",
                    source_loop="oad_cognition",
                    cycle_id=cycle_id,
                    timestamp=ts,
                    event_type="mission_failure",
                    severity="high",
                    category=f"mission_{mission.get('mission_type', 'unknown')}",
                    description=f"OAD mission failed: {mission.get('error_detail', 'unknown error')}",
                    metrics={"duration_ms": mission.get("duration_ms", 0)},
                    raw_payload=mission,
                ))

        self.events_buffer.extend(events)
        logger.info(f"[INGEST] OAD cognition {cycle_id} ({rig}): {len(events)} events extracted")
        return events

    # ── 2. CROSS-LOOP CORRELATOR ────────────────────────────────────────

    def correlate_events(self) -> list[CrossLoopCorrelation]:
        """Detect cause-effect relationships across loops.

        Correlation rules:
        1. CRP guardrail violation → OAD reflex fix on same file within 30min = auto-heal correlation
        2. VCC build + new SRS code → Perplexity health degradation within 2hrs = regression correlation
        3. OAD pipeline failure → CRP test failure in next cycle = cascade correlation
        4. Perplexity blocker → OAD mission dispatch within 1hr = auto-remediation correlation
        5. CRP drift detection → Perplexity DORA degradation = drift-quality correlation
        """
        correlations = []
        events_by_loop = defaultdict(list)
        for e in self.events_buffer:
            events_by_loop[e.source_loop].append(e)

        # Rule 1: CRP guardrail → OAD reflex fix on same file
        for crp_evt in events_by_loop.get("crp", []):
            if crp_evt.event_type != "guardrail_violation":
                continue
            for oad_evt in events_by_loop.get("oad_reflex", []):
                if oad_evt.event_type != "reflex_auto_fix":
                    continue
                # Check file overlap
                overlap = set(crp_evt.affected_files) & set(oad_evt.affected_files)
                if overlap and self._within_window(crp_evt.timestamp, oad_evt.timestamp, hours=0.5):
                    corr = CrossLoopCorrelation(
                        correlation_id=f"corr-{crp_evt.event_id}-{oad_evt.event_id}",
                        cause_loop="crp",
                        cause_event={"id": crp_evt.event_id, "type": crp_evt.event_type,
                                     "category": crp_evt.category, "files": crp_evt.affected_files},
                        effect_loop="oad_reflex",
                        effect_event={"id": oad_evt.event_id, "type": oad_evt.event_type,
                                      "pattern": oad_evt.metrics.get("pattern_code")},
                        confidence=0.85,
                        explanation=f"CRP guardrail violation on {list(overlap)} auto-healed by OAD Reflex ({oad_evt.metrics.get('pattern_code')})",
                    )
                    correlations.append(corr)

        # Rule 2: VCC build → Perplexity degradation (regression detection)
        for crp_evt in events_by_loop.get("crp", []):
            if crp_evt.event_type not in ("test_failure", "guardrail_violation"):
                continue
            for pplx_evt in events_by_loop.get("perplexity", []):
                if pplx_evt.event_type != "health_degradation":
                    continue
                if self._within_window(crp_evt.timestamp, pplx_evt.timestamp, hours=2):
                    corr = CrossLoopCorrelation(
                        correlation_id=f"corr-regression-{crp_evt.event_id}-{pplx_evt.event_id}",
                        cause_loop="crp",
                        cause_event={"id": crp_evt.event_id, "type": crp_evt.event_type,
                                     "srs_codes": crp_evt.affected_srs_codes},
                        effect_loop="perplexity",
                        effect_event={"id": pplx_evt.event_id, "grade": pplx_evt.metrics.get("grade"),
                                      "score": pplx_evt.metrics.get("score")},
                        confidence=0.65,
                        explanation=f"VCC build issue ({crp_evt.category}) potentially caused infrastructure degradation (score: {pplx_evt.metrics.get('score')})",
                    )
                    correlations.append(corr)

        # Rule 3: OAD pipeline failure → CRP test failure
        for oad_evt in events_by_loop.get("oad_cognition", []):
            if oad_evt.event_type != "pipeline_failure":
                continue
            for crp_evt in events_by_loop.get("crp", []):
                if crp_evt.event_type != "test_failure":
                    continue
                if self._within_window(oad_evt.timestamp, crp_evt.timestamp, hours=4):
                    corr = CrossLoopCorrelation(
                        correlation_id=f"corr-cascade-{oad_evt.event_id}-{crp_evt.event_id}",
                        cause_loop="oad_cognition",
                        cause_event={"id": oad_evt.event_id, "gitlab": oad_evt.metrics},
                        effect_loop="crp",
                        effect_event={"id": crp_evt.event_id, "test": crp_evt.description},
                        confidence=0.70,
                        explanation=f"OAD-detected pipeline failure cascaded into CRP test failure",
                    )
                    correlations.append(corr)

        # Rule 5: CRP drift → Perplexity DORA degradation
        for crp_evt in events_by_loop.get("crp", []):
            if crp_evt.event_type != "drift_detection":
                continue
            for pplx_evt in events_by_loop.get("perplexity", []):
                if pplx_evt.event_type != "dora_degradation":
                    continue
                if self._within_window(crp_evt.timestamp, pplx_evt.timestamp, hours=6):
                    corr = CrossLoopCorrelation(
                        correlation_id=f"corr-drift-dora-{crp_evt.event_id}-{pplx_evt.event_id}",
                        cause_loop="crp",
                        cause_event={"id": crp_evt.event_id, "layer": crp_evt.category},
                        effect_loop="perplexity",
                        effect_event={"id": pplx_evt.event_id, "cfr": pplx_evt.metrics.get("change_failure_rate")},
                        confidence=0.60,
                        explanation=f"Spec drift ({crp_evt.category}) correlates with rising change failure rate",
                    )
                    correlations.append(corr)

        self.correlations = [c for c in correlations if c.confidence >= CORRELATION_CONFIDENCE_THRESHOLD]
        logger.info(f"[CORRELATE] {len(self.correlations)} correlations above threshold ({CORRELATION_CONFIDENCE_THRESHOLD})")
        return self.correlations

    # ── 3. FAILURE SIGNATURE CATALOG ────────────────────────────────────

    def catalog_failures(self) -> dict[str, FailureSignature]:
        """Fingerprint and catalog recurring failure patterns.

        Fingerprint = hash(category + sorted(affected_files) + event_type)
        If fingerprint matches an existing signature, increment frequency.
        """
        for event in self.events_buffer:
            if event.severity not in ("high", "critical"):
                continue  # only catalog significant events

            fp = self._compute_fingerprint(event)

            if fp in self.signatures:
                sig = self.signatures[fp]
                sig.frequency += 1
                sig.last_seen = event.timestamp
                sig.occurrences.append({
                    "cycle_id": event.cycle_id,
                    "loop": event.source_loop,
                    "timestamp": event.timestamp,
                    "description": event.description[:200],
                })
            else:
                self.signatures[fp] = FailureSignature(
                    fingerprint=fp,
                    category=event.category,
                    canonical_description=event.description[:200],
                    occurrences=[{
                        "cycle_id": event.cycle_id,
                        "loop": event.source_loop,
                        "timestamp": event.timestamp,
                        "description": event.description[:200],
                    }],
                    frequency=1,
                    first_seen=event.timestamp,
                    last_seen=event.timestamp,
                )

        # Load existing signatures from DB and merge
        existing = self.db.query_learning_store(learning_type="failure_signature", limit=200)
        for row in existing:
            fp = row.get("failure_fingerprint", "")
            if fp in self.signatures:
                # Merge: add DB frequency to in-memory frequency
                self.signatures[fp].frequency += row.get("failure_frequency", 0)
                if row.get("first_seen_at"):
                    if row["first_seen_at"] < self.signatures[fp].first_seen:
                        self.signatures[fp].first_seen = row["first_seen_at"]
                self.signatures[fp].mean_time_to_detect_s = row.get("mean_time_to_detect_s", 0)
                self.signatures[fp].mean_time_to_fix_s = row.get("mean_time_to_fix_s", 0)
            elif fp:  # Existing signature not seen this cycle
                self.signatures[fp] = FailureSignature(
                    fingerprint=fp,
                    category=row.get("failure_category", "unknown"),
                    canonical_description=row.get("pattern_description", ""),
                    frequency=row.get("failure_frequency", 0),
                    first_seen=row.get("first_seen_at", ""),
                    last_seen=row.get("last_seen_at", ""),
                    mean_time_to_detect_s=row.get("mean_time_to_detect_s", 0),
                    mean_time_to_fix_s=row.get("mean_time_to_fix_s", 0),
                )

        logger.info(f"[CATALOG] {len(self.signatures)} failure signatures tracked")
        return self.signatures

    # ── 4. FIX EFFECTIVENESS TRACKER ────────────────────────────────────

    def track_fix_effectiveness(self) -> list[FixEffectivenessRecord]:
        """Track whether fixes (from any loop) actually resolved the target issue.

        Logic:
        - For each OAD reflex fix, check if the same failure signature recurs in the next N cycles
        - For each VCC build fix, check if CRP guardrail/test passes in subsequent cycles
        - For each Perplexity recommendation acted upon, check if health score improves
        """
        fix_records = []

        # Check OAD reflex fixes
        for event in self.events_buffer:
            if event.event_type != "reflex_auto_fix":
                continue
            target_fp = self._compute_fingerprint_from_category(
                event.category.replace("reflex_", ""),
                event.affected_files,
            )
            fix_records.append(FixEffectivenessRecord(
                fix_id=event.event_id,
                fix_source="oad_reflex",
                fix_description=event.description,
                target_fingerprint=target_fp,
                applied_at=event.timestamp,
            ))

        # Load pending fixes from DB and check if they're verified
        pending = self.db.query_learning_store(learning_type="fix_effectiveness", limit=50)
        for row in pending:
            if row.get("fix_resolved") is not None:
                continue  # Already verified
            fp = row.get("failure_fingerprint", "")
            cycles_since = row.get("cycles_to_verify", 0) + 1

            # Check if the failure recurred
            recurred = fp in self.signatures and self.signatures[fp].last_seen > row.get("created_at", "")

            if cycles_since >= FIX_VERIFY_CYCLES:
                record = FixEffectivenessRecord(
                    fix_id=row.get("learning_id", ""),
                    fix_source=row.get("fix_source", "unknown"),
                    fix_description=row.get("fix_description", ""),
                    target_fingerprint=fp,
                    applied_at=row.get("created_at", ""),
                    resolved=not recurred,
                    cycles_monitored=cycles_since,
                    verification_status="verified_resolved" if not recurred else "verified_failed",
                )
                fix_records.append(record)

                # Persist verification
                self.db.upsert_learning({
                    "learning_id": row["learning_id"],
                    "fix_resolved": not recurred,
                    "cycles_to_verify": cycles_since,
                    "fix_regression": False,  # TODO: detect regressions
                })

        self.pending_fixes = fix_records
        verified = [f for f in fix_records if f.verification_status.startswith("verified")]
        resolved = [f for f in verified if f.resolved]
        logger.info(f"[FIX-TRACK] {len(verified)} fixes verified, {len(resolved)} resolved successfully")
        return fix_records

    # ── 5. ADAPTIVE DECISION ENGINE ─────────────────────────────────────

    def generate_advisories(self) -> list[AdaptiveAdvisory]:
        """Produce advisories that adjust VCC/orchestrator behavior based on learnings.

        Advisory types:
        1. threshold_adjustment — change GO/NO-GO thresholds based on false positive/negative rates
        2. priority_rerank — re-rank SRS codes by computed risk score
        3. build_pause_recommendation — suggest pausing builds based on pattern recurrence
        4. fix_recommendation — suggest specific fixes based on effective historical fixes
        5. pattern_alert — alert on newly detected cross-loop patterns
        """
        advisories = []
        now = datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()

        # Advisory 1: Rerank SRS codes by risk
        srs_risk = self._compute_srs_risk_scores()
        for srs_code, risk in sorted(srs_risk.items(), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)[:10]:
            if risk > 0.5:
                advisories.append(AdaptiveAdvisory(
                    advisory_id=f"adv-risk-{srs_code}-{now[:10]}",
                    advisory_type="priority_rerank",
                    target=srs_code,
                    old_value={"risk_score": 0.0},
                    new_value={"risk_score": round(risk, 3)},
                    reason=f"{srs_code} has elevated risk ({risk:.2f}) based on failure frequency, fix time, and regression rate",
                    confidence=min(risk, 0.95),
                    auto_apply=False,
                ))

        # Advisory 2: Recurring failures that exceed threshold
        for fp, sig in self.signatures.items():
            if sig.frequency >= FAILURE_RECURRENCE_THRESHOLD and not sig.resolved:
                advisories.append(AdaptiveAdvisory(
                    advisory_id=f"adv-recur-{fp[:16]}-{now[:10]}",
                    advisory_type="pattern_alert",
                    target=sig.category,
                    new_value={"frequency": sig.frequency, "category": sig.category},
                    reason=f"Failure pattern '{sig.canonical_description[:80]}' has recurred {sig.frequency} times since {sig.first_seen[:10]}. MTTR: {sig.mean_time_to_fix_s}s.",
                    confidence=min(0.5 + (sig.frequency * 0.1), 0.95),
                    auto_apply=False,
                ))

        # Advisory 3: Fix recommendations from effective historical fixes
        effective_fixes = [
            f for f in self.pending_fixes
            if f.verification_status == "verified_resolved"
        ]
        for fix in effective_fixes:
            # Check if the same failure pattern is recurring now
            if fix.target_fingerprint in self.signatures:
                sig = self.signatures[fix.target_fingerprint]
                if not sig.resolved:
                    advisories.append(AdaptiveAdvisory(
                        advisory_id=f"adv-fix-{fix.fix_id[:16]}-{now[:10]}",
                        advisory_type="fix_recommendation",
                        target=sig.category,
                        new_value={"recommended_fix": fix.fix_description, "source": fix.fix_source},
                        reason=f"Historical fix '{fix.fix_description[:80]}' (from {fix.fix_source}) successfully resolved this pattern before. Recommend re-applying.",
                        confidence=0.80,
                        auto_apply=fix.fix_source == "oad_reflex",  # auto-apply OAD reflex fixes
                    ))

        # Advisory 4: Cross-loop correlation alerts
        for corr in self.correlations:
            if corr.confidence >= 0.8:
                advisories.append(AdaptiveAdvisory(
                    advisory_id=f"adv-corr-{corr.correlation_id[:20]}",
                    advisory_type="pattern_alert",
                    target=f"{corr.cause_loop} → {corr.effect_loop}",
                    new_value={"cause": corr.cause_event, "effect": corr.effect_event},
                    reason=corr.explanation,
                    confidence=corr.confidence,
                    auto_apply=False,
                ))

        # Advisory 5: Build pause if too many critical failures
        critical_count = sum(1 for e in self.events_buffer if e.severity == "critical")
        if critical_count >= 5:
            advisories.append(AdaptiveAdvisory(
                advisory_id=f"adv-pause-{now[:13]}",
                advisory_type="build_pause_recommendation",
                target="vcc_build_loop",
                new_value={"recommended_action": "pause", "critical_events": critical_count},
                reason=f"{critical_count} critical events detected across all loops. Recommend pausing VCC build until resolved.",
                confidence=0.90,
                auto_apply=True,
            ))

        self.advisories = advisories
        logger.info(f"[ADVISE] {len(advisories)} advisories generated")
        return advisories

    # ── 6. RUN FULL LEARNING CYCLE ──────────────────────────────────────

    async def run_learning_cycle(self) -> LearningCycleReport:
        """Execute the complete learning pipeline and produce a report.

        Called by the orchestrator after every merged snapshot,
        or by CRP during §7.9 assembly.
        """
        now = datetime.now(timezone.utc)
        cycle_id = f"LEARN-{now.strftime('%Y%m%d-%H%M')}"

        # If buffer is empty, load from vcc_loop_state
        if not self.events_buffer:
            await self._load_recent_loop_state()

        # Run pipeline
        self.correlate_events()
        self.catalog_failures()
        self.track_fix_effectiveness()
        self.generate_advisories()

        # Persist learnings to Supabase
        await self._persist_learnings(cycle_id)

        # Submit metrics to Datadog
        self._submit_dd_learning_metrics(cycle_id)

        # Capture PostHog event
        self._submit_ph_learning_event(cycle_id)

        # Build report
        events_by_loop = Counter(e.source_loop for e in self.events_buffer)
        top_failures = sorted(
            self.signatures.values(),
            key=lambda s: s.frequency,
            reverse=True,
        )[:5]
        srs_risk = self._compute_srs_risk_scores()

        report = LearningCycleReport(
            learning_cycle_id=cycle_id,
            timestamp=now.isoformat(),
            events_ingested=len(self.events_buffer),
            events_by_loop=dict(events_by_loop),
            new_signatures=sum(1 for s in self.signatures.values() if s.frequency == 1),
            updated_signatures=sum(1 for s in self.signatures.values() if s.frequency > 1),
            correlations_found=len(self.correlations),
            fixes_verified=sum(1 for f in self.pending_fixes if f.verification_status.startswith("verified")),
            fixes_failed=sum(1 for f in self.pending_fixes if f.verification_status == "verified_failed"),
            regressions_detected=sum(1 for f in self.pending_fixes if f.regression_introduced),
            advisories_issued=self.advisories,
            top_recurring_failures=[
                {"fingerprint": s.fingerprint[:12], "category": s.category,
                 "frequency": s.frequency, "description": s.canonical_description[:60]}
                for s in top_failures
            ],
            risk_ranked_srs_codes=[
                {"srs_code": code, "risk_score": round(score, 3)}
                for code, score in sorted(srs_risk.items(), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)[:10]
            ],
        )

        # Clear buffer for next cycle
        self.events_buffer.clear()

        logger.info(f"[LEARN] Cycle {cycle_id} complete: {report.events_ingested} events, "
                    f"{report.correlations_found} correlations, {len(report.advisories_issued)} advisories")
        return report

    # ── 7. INTEGRATION HOOKS ────────────────────────────────────────────

    def get_crp_section_79(self) -> str:
        """Generate CRP §7.9 — Learning Report content for Notion toggle block."""
        if not self.advisories and not self.signatures:
            return "§7.9 — Learning Report: No learnings this cycle (first run or no events)."

        lines = ["§7.9 — Trilateral Learning Report"]
        lines.append(f"  Events ingested: {len(self.events_buffer)}")
        lines.append(f"  Correlations: {len(self.correlations)}")
        lines.append(f"  Failure signatures tracked: {len(self.signatures)}")

        if self.signatures:
            lines.append("  Top recurring failures:")
            for sig in sorted(self.signatures.values(), key=lambda s: s.frequency, reverse=True)[:5]:
                lines.append(f"    • [{sig.category}] {sig.canonical_description[:60]} (×{sig.frequency})")

        if self.advisories:
            lines.append(f"  Advisories issued: {len(self.advisories)}")
            for adv in self.advisories[:5]:
                auto = " [AUTO-APPLY]" if adv.auto_apply else ""
                lines.append(f"    • {adv.advisory_type}: {adv.reason[:80]}{auto}")

        verified = [f for f in self.pending_fixes if f.verification_status.startswith("verified")]
        if verified:
            resolved = sum(1 for f in verified if f.resolved)
            lines.append(f"  Fix effectiveness: {resolved}/{len(verified)} fixes verified as resolved")

        return "\n".join(lines)

    def get_orchestrator_adjustments(self) -> dict:
        """Return adjustments the orchestrator should apply to its GO/NO-GO logic."""
        adjustments = {
            "pause_recommended": any(
                a.advisory_type == "build_pause_recommendation" and a.auto_apply
                for a in self.advisories
            ),
            "risk_ranked_srs": {
                a.target: a.new_value.get("risk_score", 0)
                for a in self.advisories
                if a.advisory_type == "priority_rerank"
            },
            "auto_fix_recommendations": [
                {"target": a.target, "fix": a.new_value.get("recommended_fix"),
                 "source": a.new_value.get("source"), "confidence": a.confidence}
                for a in self.advisories
                if a.advisory_type == "fix_recommendation" and a.auto_apply
            ],
            "pattern_alerts": [
                {"target": a.target, "reason": a.reason, "confidence": a.confidence}
                for a in self.advisories
                if a.advisory_type == "pattern_alert" and a.confidence >= 0.8
            ],
        }
        return adjustments

    # ── PRIVATE HELPERS ──────────────────────────────────────────────────

    def _compute_fingerprint(self, event: NormalizedLoopEvent) -> str:
        """Compute a stable fingerprint for a failure event."""
        key = f"{event.category}|{event.event_type}|{'|'.join(sorted(event.affected_files))}"
        return hashlib.sha256(key.encode()).hexdigest()[:24]

    def _compute_fingerprint_from_category(self, category: str, files: list[str]) -> str:
        key = f"{category}|{'|'.join(sorted(files))}"
        return hashlib.sha256(key.encode()).hexdigest()[:24]

    def _severity_from_guardrail(self, violation: dict) -> str:
        rule = violation.get("rule", "").upper()
        if any(k in rule for k in ("RLS", "TENANT", "SERVICE_ROLE")):
            return "critical"
        if any(k in rule for k in ("IDEMPOTENCY", "STRIPE", "COVERAGE")):
            return "high"
        return "medium"

    def _categorize_test_failure(self, test: dict) -> str:
        name = test.get("test_name", "").lower()
        if "rls" in name:
            return "rls_test"
        if "entitlement" in name or "rbac" in name:
            return "auth_test"
        if "idempotency" in name:
            return "idempotency_test"
        if "integration" in name:
            return "integration_test"
        return "unit_test"

    def _categorize_blocker(self, blocker: str) -> str:
        lower = blocker.lower()
        if "pipeline" in lower or "ci" in lower:
            return "ci_cd"
        if "nats" in lower:
            return "messaging"
        if "supabase" in lower or "database" in lower:
            return "database"
        if "stripe" in lower:
            return "payments"
        if "deploy" in lower or "ecs" in lower:
            return "deployment"
        return "infrastructure"

    def _reflex_severity(self, pattern_code: str) -> str:
        severity_map = {"F924": "low", "F950": "medium", "F960": "medium", "custom": "high"}
        return severity_map.get(pattern_code, "medium")

    def _within_window(self, ts1: str, ts2: str, hours: float) -> bool:
        try:
            t1 = datetime.fromisoformat(ts1.replace("Z", "+00:00"))
            t2 = datetime.fromisoformat(ts2.replace("Z", "+00:00"))
            return abs((t2 - t1).total_seconds()) <= hours * 3600
        except (ValueError, TypeError):
            return False

    def _compute_srs_risk_scores(self) -> dict[str, float]:
        """Compute risk score per SRS code based on failure history."""
        srs_failures: dict[str, list] = defaultdict(list)
        for event in self.events_buffer:
            for srs in event.affected_srs_codes:
                srs_failures[srs].append(event)

        risk_scores = {}
        for srs, events in srs_failures.items():
            freq = len(events)
            critical_ratio = sum(1 for e in events if e.severity == "critical") / max(freq, 1)
            # Check if any fix for this SRS caused a regression
            regression_count = sum(
                1 for f in self.pending_fixes
                if f.regression_introduced and any(srs in e.affected_srs_codes for e in self.events_buffer
                                                    if f.target_fingerprint == self._compute_fingerprint(e))
            )
            risk = (
                RISK_SCORE_WEIGHTS["failure_frequency"] * min(freq / 10, 1.0) +
                RISK_SCORE_WEIGHTS["mean_time_to_fix"] * critical_ratio +
                RISK_SCORE_WEIGHTS["correlation_count"] * min(
                    sum(1 for c in self.correlations if srs in str(c.cause_event) or srs in str(c.effect_event)) / 5, 1.0
                ) +
                RISK_SCORE_WEIGHTS["regression_rate"] * min(regression_count / 3, 1.0)
            )
            risk_scores[srs] = min(risk, 1.0)

        return risk_scores

    async def _load_recent_loop_state(self):
        """Load recent loop state from Supabase when buffer is empty."""
        for source in ["crp", "perplexity", "oad_cognition", "oad_reflex"]:
            rows = self.db.query_loop_state(loop_source=source, limit=ADAPTIVE_LOOKBACK_CYCLES)
            for row in rows:
                snapshot = row.get("health_snapshot", {})
                if source == "crp":
                    self.ingest_crp_cycle(snapshot)
                elif source == "perplexity":
                    self.ingest_perplexity_diagnostic(snapshot)
                elif source in ("oad_cognition", "oad_reflex"):
                    oad_snap = row.get("oad_snapshot", {})
                    oad_snap["reflex_fixes"] = row.get("oad_reflex_fixes", [])
                    oad_snap["cycle_id"] = row.get("cycle_id", "")
                    oad_snap["rig"] = row.get("oad_rig", "rig2")
                    self.ingest_oad_cognition(oad_snap)

    async def _persist_learnings(self, cycle_id: str):
        """Write all learnings to vcc_learning_store."""
        seq = 0

        # Persist failure signatures
        for fp, sig in self.signatures.items():
            seq += 1
            self.db.upsert_learning({
                "learning_id": f"{cycle_id}-sig-{seq:03d}",
                "learning_type": "failure_signature",
                "source_loops": json.dumps(list(set(o["loop"] for o in sig.occurrences))),
                "source_cycle_ids": json.dumps(list(set(o["cycle_id"] for o in sig.occurrences))),
                "failure_fingerprint": fp,
                "failure_category": sig.category,
                "failure_frequency": sig.frequency,
                "first_seen_at": sig.first_seen,
                "last_seen_at": sig.last_seen,
                "mean_time_to_detect_s": sig.mean_time_to_detect_s,
                "mean_time_to_fix_s": sig.mean_time_to_fix_s,
                "pattern_description": sig.canonical_description,
                "is_active": not sig.resolved,
            })

        # Persist correlations
        for corr in self.correlations:
            seq += 1
            self.db.upsert_learning({
                "learning_id": f"{cycle_id}-corr-{seq:03d}",
                "learning_type": "correlation",
                "source_loops": json.dumps([corr.cause_loop, corr.effect_loop]),
                "cause_loop": corr.cause_loop,
                "effect_loop": corr.effect_loop,
                "cause_event": json.dumps(corr.cause_event),
                "effect_event": json.dumps(corr.effect_event),
                "correlation_confidence": corr.confidence,
                "pattern_description": corr.explanation,
            })

        # Persist advisories
        for adv in self.advisories:
            seq += 1
            self.db.upsert_learning({
                "learning_id": f"{cycle_id}-adv-{seq:03d}",
                "learning_type": adv.advisory_type,
                "adjustment_reason": adv.reason,
                "adjustment_confidence": adv.confidence,
                "old_threshold": json.dumps(adv.old_value),
                "new_threshold": json.dumps(adv.new_value),
                "srs_code": adv.target if adv.advisory_type == "priority_rerank" else None,
                "risk_score": adv.new_value.get("risk_score", 0),
            })

        logger.info(f"[PERSIST] {seq} learning records written to vcc_learning_store")

    def _submit_dd_learning_metrics(self, cycle_id: str):
        """Submit learning metrics to Datadog."""
        if not DD_API_KEY:
            return
        now = int(datetime.now(timezone.utc).timestamp())
        series = [
            {"metric": "sanctum.learning.events_ingested", "type": "gauge",
             "points": [[now, len(self.events_buffer)]],
             "tags": [f"cycle:{cycle_id}", "env:production"]},
            {"metric": "sanctum.learning.signatures_tracked", "type": "gauge",
             "points": [[now, len(self.signatures)]],
             "tags": [f"cycle:{cycle_id}"]},
            {"metric": "sanctum.learning.correlations_found", "type": "gauge",
             "points": [[now, len(self.correlations)]],
             "tags": [f"cycle:{cycle_id}"]},
            {"metric": "sanctum.learning.advisories_issued", "type": "gauge",
             "points": [[now, len(self.advisories)]],
             "tags": [f"cycle:{cycle_id}"]},
        ]
        # Per-loop event counts
        loop_counts = Counter(e.source_loop for e in self.events_buffer)
        for loop, count in loop_counts.items():
            series.append({
                "metric": "sanctum.learning.events_by_loop", "type": "gauge",
                "points": [[now, count]],
                "tags": [f"loop:{loop}", f"cycle:{cycle_id}"],
            })
        try:
            requests.post(
                f"https://api.{DD_SITE}/api/v1/series",
                headers={"DD-API-KEY": DD_API_KEY, "Content-Type": "application/json"},
                json={"series": series},
                timeout=10,
            )
        except Exception as e:
            logger.warning(f"DD learning metrics failed: {e}")

    def _submit_ph_learning_event(self, cycle_id: str):
        """Capture learning cycle event to PostHog."""
        if not PH_API_KEY:
            return
        try:
            requests.post(
                f"{PH_HOST}/capture/",
                json={
                    "api_key": PH_API_KEY,
                    "event": "vcc.learning_cycle_complete",
                    "distinct_id": "vcc-learning-engine",
                    "properties": {
                        "cycle_id": cycle_id,
                        "events_ingested": len(self.events_buffer),
                        "signatures_tracked": len(self.signatures),
                        "correlations_found": len(self.correlations),
                        "advisories_issued": len(self.advisories),
                        "auto_apply_count": sum(1 for a in self.advisories if a.auto_apply),
                    },
                },
                timeout=5,
            )
        except Exception as e:
            logger.warning(f"PH learning event failed: {e}")


# ── CLI ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
if __name__ == "__main__":
    import argparse
    import asyncio

    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="VCC Trilateral Learning Engine")
    parser.add_argument("--run-cycle", action="store_true", help="Run a full learning cycle")
    parser.add_argument("--report", action="store_true", help="Print latest learning report")
    parser.add_argument("--export-advisories", action="store_true", help="Export current advisories as JSON")
    parser.add_argument("--dry-run", action="store_true", help="Don't persist to Supabase")
    args = parser.parse_args()

    logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format="%(asctime)s %(name)s %(message)s")
    engine = LearningEngine()

    if args.run_cycle:
        report = asyncio.run(engine.run_learning_cycle())
        print(json.dumps(report.model_dump(), indent=2, default=str))
    elif args.report:
        print(engine.get_crp_section_79())
    elif args.export_advisories:
        asyncio.run(engine._load_recent_loop_state())
        engine.correlate_events()
        engine.catalog_failures()
        engine.track_fix_effectiveness()
        advisories = engine.generate_advisories()
        print(json.dumps([a.model_dump() for a in advisories], indent=2, default=str))
```
**§17.3 — Integration Points**
| **Caller** | **Method** | **When** | **What It Does** |
| `loop_orchestrator.py` | `engine.ingest_crp_cycle(report)` | On `citadel.vcc.cycle.completed` NATS event | Ingests CRP cycle report into learning buffer |
| `loop_orchestrator.py` | `engine.ingest_perplexity_diagnostic(diag)` | On `citadel.diagnostic.completed` NATS event | Ingests Perplexity diagnostic into learning buffer |
| `loop_orchestrator.py` | `engine.ingest_oad_cognition(snapshot)` | On `citadel.oad.cognition.completed` NATS event | Ingests OAD cognition snapshot into learning buffer |
| `loop_orchestrator.py` | `engine.run_learning_cycle()` | After every trilateral merge | Runs full pipeline: correlate → catalog → track → advise |
| `loop_orchestrator.py` | `engine.get_orchestrator_adjustments()` | Before GO/NO-GO evaluation | Returns adaptive adjustments (pause, rerank, fix recs) |
| `vcc_cycle_reporter.py` | `engine.get_crp_section_79()` | During CRP §7 assembly | Injects §7.9 Learning Report into CRP cycle report |
| `vcc_automation_loop.py` | `engine.get_orchestrator_adjustments()` | Before `_execute_vcc_build()` | Checks if build should pause or SRS priority changed |
| `guild_auditor.py` | `engine.run_learning_cycle()` | During Phase 5 audit | Produces comprehensive learning report for audit |
**§17.4 — Environment Variables**
| **Variable** | **Required** | **Default** | **Notes** |
| `LEARN_CORR_THRESHOLD` | Optional | `0.6` | Minimum confidence for cross-loop correlations |
| `LEARN_FAIL_RECUR` | Optional | `3` | Recurrence count before failure pattern triggers advisory |
| `LEARN_FIX_VERIFY_CYCLES` | Optional | `3` | Cycles to wait before verifying fix effectiveness |
| `LEARN_LOOKBACK` | Optional | `20` | Number of historical cycles to load for trend analysis |
**§17.5 — Tests**
Place at `tests/phase_learning/`:
- `test_learning_ingest_crp.py` — assert CRP cycle events normalize correctly (guardrails, tests, drift, health, SLA)
- `test_learning_ingest_perplexity.py` — assert Perplexity events normalize (grade, blockers, infra, DORA, L3)
- `test_learning_ingest_oad.py` — assert OAD events normalize (reflex, pipeline, college, missions, Linear error)
- `test_learning_correlator.py` — assert all 5 correlation rules fire correctly, confidence thresholds enforced, time windows respected
- `test_learning_failure_catalog.py` — assert fingerprinting is stable, frequency increments, DB merge works, resolved signatures are marked
- `test_learning_fix_tracker.py` — assert OAD reflex fixes tracked, verification after N cycles, resolved/failed classification, regression detection
- `test_learning_advisories.py` — assert risk reranking produces valid scores, recurring failures trigger alerts, fix recommendations match, build pause triggers at 5+ critical, auto-apply only for OAD reflex
- `test_learning_full_cycle.py` — end-to-end: ingest from all 3 loops → correlate → catalog → track → advise → report → persist → DD/PH submit
- `test_learning_crp_section.py` — assert `get_crp_section_79()` renders valid text with all subsections
- `test_learning_orchestrator_hooks.py` — assert `get_orchestrator_adjustments()` returns valid dict, pause flag works, risk scores propagate
**§17.6 — Usage**
```bash
# Run a full learning cycle (reads from vcc_loop_state, persists to vcc_learning_store)
python tools/vcc_learning_engine.py --run-cycle

# Print the CRP §7.9 section content
python tools/vcc_learning_engine.py --report

# Export current advisories as JSON
python tools/vcc_learning_engine.py --export-advisories

# Dry run — no Supabase persistence
python tools/vcc_learning_engine.py --run-cycle --dry-run
```
**§17.7 — Must-Dos and Must-Not-Dos**
**Must-Dos:**
1. ✅ Always ingest from ALL THREE loops before running correlation — partial ingestion produces false negatives
1. ✅ Fingerprints MUST be deterministic — same event category + files = same fingerprint every time
1. ✅ Fix verification MUST wait at least `LEARN_FIX_VERIFY_CYCLES` before declaring resolved
1. ✅ All advisories MUST include a confidence score — never auto-apply below 0.8
1. ✅ Submit DD/PH metrics on every learning cycle — observability of the learning engine itself
1. ✅ Expire old learnings (180 days) — the learning store must not grow unbounded
1. ✅ Log every ingestion, correlation, and advisory to structured logger for audit trail
**Must-Not-Dos:**
1. 🚫 NEVER auto-apply threshold adjustments — only OAD reflex fix recommendations can auto-apply
1. 🚫 NEVER delete failure signatures — mark as `resolved`, keep the history for trend analysis
1. 🚫 NEVER trust a single correlation — require `>= 0.6` confidence and at least 2 occurrences
1. 🚫 NEVER skip the DB merge step — in-memory signatures MUST be merged with Supabase history
1. 🚫 NEVER run the learning engine without `SUPABASE_URL` and `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY` — it needs the state store
1. 🚫 NEVER block CRP cycle report generation if the learning engine fails — degrade gracefully with `"Learning engine unavailable"`

[CALLOUT] 🚨 **§17 is mandatory after Phase 2.5 deployment.** Without the learning engine, the trilateral system generates data but never learns from it. Failures recur, fixes are re-applied blindly, and VCC build priorities are static. The learning engine closes the loop — making the entire system self-improving. There are no exceptions.


---


# 5. Conventions & Patterns


### 5.1 Naming Conventions

| **Context** | **Convention** | **Example** |
| DB tables | `snake_case`, prefixed `finance_` | `finance_invoices`, `finance_quotes` |
| DB columns | `snake_case` | `tenant_id`, `stripe_invoice_id`, `created_at` |
| API routes | `kebab-case` for URLs, `snake_case` for query params | `/api/finance/credit-notes?status=issued` |
| Python files | `snake_case`, prefix `router_` for route files | `router_invoices.py`, `middleware.py` |
| Python functions | `snake_case` | `create_invoice()`, `get_tenant_id()` |
| React components | `PascalCase` | `InvoiceCard.tsx`, `FinanceStatCard.tsx` |
| React hooks | `camelCase`, prefix `use` | `useFinanceWS`, `useEntitlement` |
| TypeScript types | `PascalCase`, suffix with entity type | `InvoiceResponse`, `QuoteCreateRequest` |
| NATS subjects | `dot.separated.lowercase` | `citadel.finance.invoice.sent` |
| Redis keys | `colon:separated` | `finance:{tenant_id}:invoice_list:{hash}` |
| Environment vars | `SCREAMING_SNAKE_CASE` | `STRIPE_PLATFORM_SECRET`, `SUPABASE_URL` |
| SRS codes | `SRS-FIN-###` | `SRS-FIN-004` |
| REFLEX triggers | `RFX-FIN-###` | `RFX-FIN-001` |
| SMP service IDs | `smp-fin-*` | `smp-fin-api`, `smp-fin-pdf` |

### 5.2 Error Handling Pattern

```python
# Every endpoint follows this pattern:

async def create_invoice(request: InvoiceCreateRequest, state: RequestState):
    # 1. Validate input (Pydantic does this)
    # 2. Check entitlements
    if not has_entitlement(state.tenant, 'finance:invoices'):
        raise HTTPException(403, detail={
            'error': 'ENTITLEMENT_REQUIRED',
            'key': 'finance:invoices'
        })
    # 3. Check RBAC
    if state.user_role not in ('owner', 'admin', 'operator'):
        raise HTTPException(403, detail={'error': 'INSUFFICIENT_ROLE'})
    # 4. Business logic (in a try/except)
    try:
        invoice = await invoice_service.create(state.tenant_id, request)
    except StripeError as e:
        raise HTTPException(502, detail={
            'error': 'STRIPE_ERROR',
            'message': str(e.user_message),
        })
    except DuplicateError:
        raise HTTPException(409, detail={
            'error': 'DUPLICATE',
            'message': 'Invoice number already exists'
        })
    # 5. Publish event
    await nats.publish('citadel.finance.invoice.created', invoice.to_event())
    # 6. Return response
    return InvoiceResponse.from_orm(invoice)
```

### 5.3 React Component Pattern

```typescript
// Every data-fetching component follows this pattern:

export function InvoiceList() {
  const { tenant } = useTenant();
  const { data, isLoading, isError, error, refetch } = useQuery({
    queryKey: ['invoices', tenant.id, filters],
    queryFn: () => financeApi.getInvoices(filters),
  });

  // Real-time updates via WS
  useFinanceWS((event) => {
    if (EVENT_TO_QUERY_KEY[event.type]?.includes('invoices')) {
      queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['invoices'] });
    }
  });

  return (
    <StateRenderer
      isLoading={isLoading}
      isError={isError}
      isEmpty={!data?.data?.length}
      error={error}
      loadingComponent={<InvoiceListSkeleton />}
      emptyComponent={<InvoiceEmptyState />}
      onRetry={refetch}
    >
      {data.data.map((invoice) => (
        <InvoiceCard key={invoice.id} invoice={invoice} />
      ))}
    </StateRenderer>
  );
}
```

### 5.4 Server-Side Total Recalculation

```python
# NEVER trust client-provided totals. Always recalculate.

def recalculate_invoice_totals(line_items: list, tax_rate: Decimal, discount: Discount | None) -> Totals:
    subtotal = sum(item.quantity * item.unit_rate for item in line_items)
    
    discount_amount = Decimal('0')
    if discount:
        if discount.type == 'percentage':
            discount_amount = subtotal * (discount.value / 100)
        elif discount.type == 'fixed':
            discount_amount = min(discount.value, subtotal)  # Can't discount more than subtotal
    
    taxable_subtotal = sum(
        item.quantity * item.unit_rate
        for item in line_items if item.taxable
    ) - discount_amount  # Apply discount before tax
    
    tax_amount = (taxable_subtotal * tax_rate).quantize(Decimal('0.01'))
    total = subtotal - discount_amount + tax_amount
    
    return Totals(
        subtotal=subtotal,
        discount_amount=discount_amount,
        tax_amount=tax_amount,
        total=total
    )
```

# 7. Cross-Cutting Concerns Checklist

Before marking ANY SRS code as "🟢 Built", the VCC must verify:
- [ ] **RLS test passes** — cross-tenant read returns 0 rows
- [ ] **Entitlement gate test passes** — Starter tier user cannot access Pro feature
- [ ] **RBAC test passes** — Viewer cannot create invoices
- [ ] **Idempotency test passes** — duplicate POST with same key returns cached response
- [ ] **Rate limit test passes** — 11th Text-to-Pay request in 60s returns 429
- [ ] **Audit log test passes** — write operation produces `finance_audit_log` entry with correct `entity_type`, `action`, `changes`
- [ ] **NATS event test passes** — write operation publishes event on correct subject
- [ ] **Cache invalidation test passes** — NATS event invalidates correct Redis keys
- [ ] **Loading state renders** — component shows skeleton on initial load
- [ ] **Empty state renders** — component shows CTA when data array is empty
- [ ] **Error state renders** — component shows retry button on API failure
- [ ] **Toast fires** — success/error toast appears for user actions
- [ ] **Server-side totals match** — never trust client math
- [ ] **PostHog event fires** — user-facing action triggers `posthog.capture()` with correct event name and tenant/user properties
- [ ] **Datadog APM trace exists** — API endpoint has distributed trace with `tenant_id` and `srs_code` tags
- [ ] **Datadog custom metric emits** — financial write operations emit amount/count metrics to Datadog
- [ ] **Service health check passes** — all 5 SMP services return 200 on `/health` with `status: healthy`, all dependencies (Supabase, NATS, Redis, Stripe, SES) report connected, consecutive failure count is 0
- [ ] **Diff check passes** — no new spec→code drift introduced; cycle→cycle diff is clean; blueprint→blueprint shows no unacknowledged changes; all three layers report `clean: true`; any acknowledged drifts annotated with `DRIFT-ACK`
