# 8. LLM-Specific Instructions

These are instructions for the LLM (VCC) itself, not for the code it generates.

### 8.1 Code Generation Rules


[CALLOUT] 🚨 **MANDATORY CODEBASE SCAN — RULE ZERO**

  Before generating ANY new file, the VCC MUST scan the existing codebase. This is non-negotiable. Skipping this step produces duplicate classes, broken imports, and orphaned code. Every file generation task begins with a scan — no exceptions.
**Rule 0 — Codebase Scan Before File Creation**
Before writing a single line of code for ANY new file, the VCC MUST:
1. **Scan **`**src/api/finance/**`** for existing files** — run `ls -R src/api/finance/` and `ls -R src/components/finance/` to know what already exists
1. **Scan for existing base classes and shared modules** — specifically check:
  - `src/api/finance/schemas/__init__.py` or any `schemas/*.py` for existing `FinanceBase`, shared enums, common response models
  - `src/api/deps.py` for `get_supabase`, `TenantContext`, `get_tenant_context`, `check_rbac`, and any other shared dependencies
  - `src/api/finance/middleware.py` for existing middleware stack
  - `src/api/finance/services/` for existing business logic modules
  - `src/hooks/` for existing React hooks (`useFinanceWS`, `useEntitlement`, etc.)
  - `src/types/finance.ts` for existing TypeScript types
1. **Import from existing modules — NEVER recreate** — if `FinanceBase` already exists in `schemas/base.py` or `schemas/__init__.py`, import it: `from src.api.finance.schemas.base import FinanceBase`. Do NOT define a new `FinanceBase` class in your new file.
1. **Verify import paths against actual file structure** — before writing `from src.api.deps import get_supabase`, confirm `src/api/deps.py` exists and exports `get_supabase`. If it doesn't, flag with `# VCC-QUESTION: deps.py does not export get_supabase — need to add it or use alternative`.
1. **Check git log for recently committed files** — run `git log --oneline --name-only -20` to see what was committed in recent cycles. Do NOT rebuild files that already exist in the repo.
1. **Output scan results as a preamble** — before generating code, output a brief scan summary:
```javascript
[SCAN] Existing files in src/api/finance/:
  - router_integrations.py (committed, 180 lines)
  - router_customers.py (committed, 220 lines)
  - schemas/base.py (committed, FinanceBase defined here)
  - deps.py exports: get_supabase, TenantContext, get_tenant_context, check_rbac
[SCAN] Will import from: schemas.base.FinanceBase, deps.get_supabase
[SCAN] Will create: router_dashboard.py, schemas/dashboard.py
```
**What happens if you skip the scan:**
- 🚫 You recreate `FinanceBase` in every schema file instead of importing the shared one → code duplication, divergent behavior
- 🚫 You write `from src.api.deps import X` without checking if X exists → import errors at runtime
- 🚫 You create `router_dashboard.py` when it was already committed 2 cycles ago → file overwrite, lost work
- 🚫 You report `Routers: 0/9` when 6 are already committed → broken progress tracking, operator confusion

---

- **Generate complete files** — no `// ... rest of the code` or `# TODO: implement`. Every file must be production-ready.
- **Include all imports** — never assume an import exists. Every file starts with its full import block. **Imports MUST reference actual existing modules found during the codebase scan.**
- **Include TypeScript types** — every function parameter, every return type, every state variable must be explicitly typed. No `any`.
- **Include error handling** — every `try` needs a `catch`. Every API call needs a failure path.
- **Include comments** — but only for _why_, never for _what_. `// Recalculate to prevent client-side tampering` is good. `// Create invoice` is useless.
- **Generate tests alongside code** — when you generate `router_invoices.py`, also generate `test_router_invoices.py`.
- **NEVER define a class that already exists in the codebase** — if the scan finds `FinanceBase`, `TenantContext`, `StateRenderer`, or ANY shared utility, you MUST import it. Defining a duplicate is a guardrail violation.

### 8.2 When You're Unsure

- If the spec doesn't cover something, **do not improvise**. Output a `# VCC-QUESTION: [describe what's missing]` comment and move on.
- If two sections of the spec appear to contradict each other, **flag it** with `# VCC-CONFLICT: Section X says A, Section Y says B` and use the more restrictive interpretation.
- If a feature requires an external service not in the stack (e.g., Twilio, SendGrid), **do not add it**. Use the existing services: AWS SNS for SMS, AWS SES for email, Bedrock for AI.

### 8.3 What to Output Per Task

When given a build task (e.g., "Build SRS-FIN-004"), output in this order:
1. **Codebase scan** (MANDATORY FIRST STEP — see Rule 0 in §8.1). Output scan summary before any code.
1. **Migration file** (if new tables/columns/indexes needed)
1. **Backend route file** (FastAPI router)
1. **Backend service file** (business logic, separated from route handler)
1. **Backend test file** (pytest)
1. **TypeScript types** (additions to `finance.ts`)
1. **React components** (one file per component)
1. **React hooks** (if needed)
1. **Frontend test files** (vitest)

### 8.4 Referencing the Spec

- Section numbers (Section 1–22) refer to the parent page: _Finance Guild — UI Layout & Dashboard Spec_
- SRS codes (`SRS-FIN-001` through `SRS-FIN-035`) are in Section 19
- REFLEX triggers (`RFX-FIN-001` through `RFX-FIN-010`) are in Section 20
- SMP services are in Section 21
- The fg__ raw DDL is in the sibling page: _Finance Guild — fg__ Schema & RLS Policies_

# 9. Common Pitfalls — Avoid These


[CALLOUT] ⚠️ **Pitfall 1: Forgetting **`**Stripe-Account**`** header**

  Every Stripe API call for a tenant MUST include `stripe_account=tenant.stripe_account_id`. Without this, the call hits the platform account and creates data in the wrong place. This is the #1 cause of multi-tenant financial data leaks.

[CALLOUT] ⚠️ **Pitfall 2: RLS policy on child tables**

  Tables like `finance_quote_line_items` don't have `tenant_id` directly. Their RLS policy MUST join through the parent table: `quote_id IN (SELECT id FROM finance_quotes WHERE tenant_id = ...)`. Forgetting this means line items leak across tenants.

[CALLOUT] ⚠️ **Pitfall 3: Floating point money**

  JavaScript `number` type is IEEE 754 float. `0.1 + 0.2 !== 0.3`. All money math on the frontend MUST be display-only. All calculations happen server-side with `NUMERIC(12,2)` (Python `Decimal`).

[CALLOUT] ⚠️ **Pitfall 4: Race condition on invoice status**

  Stripe webhooks and user actions can race. Use the idempotency layer + optimistic locking (`updated_at` check) to prevent: user voids invoice while Stripe webhook marks it paid.

[CALLOUT] ⚠️ **Pitfall 5: Forgetting to invalidate cache**

  Every NATS event handler in `smp-fin-worker` MUST call `invalidate_cache()` for the affected resources (Section 16.2 `INVALIDATION_MAP`). Stale dashboard stats are a top user complaint.

[CALLOUT] ⚠️ **Pitfall 6: Sending SMS without rate-limit check**

  Text-to-Pay sends real SMS via AWS SNS. Each SMS costs money. The 10/min rate limit is a cost control measure. Bypassing it can result in runaway SMS bills.

---


# 10. Definition of Done

A feature is **Done** when:
1. ✅ All code files are generated (migration, routes, services, components, hooks, types, tests)
1. ✅ All tests pass (RLS, entitlement, RBAC, idempotency, rate limit, audit, NATS, cache, UI states)
1. ✅ The corresponding SRS code status can be changed from 🔵 Spec'd → 🟢 Built
1. ✅ No `VCC-QUESTION` or `VCC-CONFLICT` comments remain unresolved
1. ✅ The feature works end-to-end: UI → API → DB → NATS event → WS → UI update
1. ✅ Skeleton, empty, and error states all render correctly
1. ✅ Audit log captures all write operations
1. ✅ Cross-tenant isolation verified

# 12. Game Room (RPG) Integration Blueprint


[CALLOUT] 🎮 **Purpose:** The Game Room is the third room type in the Citadel Entertainment Guild triad — alongside **Deal Rooms** (business) and **Studio Rooms** (creative). Game Room = RPG Campaign System. It adds a full RPG session engine, living world state, SaaS monetization layer, creator marketplace, and a bridge to the Book Maker pipeline. The VCC MUST understand how Game Room integrates with the existing Finance Guild stack (shared Stripe Connect, shared Supabase, shared NATS bus) and where the boundaries lie.


---


## 12.1 Game Room Architecture Overview


### Service Identity

| **Component** | **Stack** | **Port** | **NATS Namespace** |
| RPG Session Engine | FastAPI (Python) | :8400 | `citadel.rpg.*` |
| Entertainment Gateway | FastAPI (Python) | :8401 | `citadel.ent.*` |
| Book Maker Bridge | FastAPI (Python) | :8402 | `citadel.writer.*` |

### Room Type Triad — Shared Layer

All three room types share a common infrastructure layer. The VCC builds Finance Guild services that **connect to** this shared layer — it does NOT build the shared layer itself.
| **Shared Layer** | **What It Does** | **Finance Guild Touchpoint** |
| NATS Event Mesh | Cross-room event routing | Finance publishes `citadel.finance.*`, subscribes to `citadel.rpg.session.completed` for creator payouts |
| Supabase + RLS | Shared PostgreSQL with tenant isolation | Finance `fg_*` tables coexist with `rpg_*` tables — same Supabase project, separate schemas |
| ElevenLabs Voice | Guild Master voice agent + RPG narrator | Finance Guild Master widget calls ElevenLabs for voice interactions; RPG narrator uses same API |
| FATE/XP Economy | Cross-room XP and progression | Finance commissions can award XP; RPG sessions earn XP redeemable in marketplace |
| Guardian Audit | Cross-room security and audit trail | Both `finance_audit_log` and `rpg_events` feed into Guardian |
| Stripe Connect | Cross-room payments | **Same Stripe Connect accounts** — creator payouts from marketplace use the same `stripe_account_id` as Finance invoices |

---


## 12.2 Game Room Supabase Schema


### 12.2.1 Core RPG Tables (7 tables)

These tables are owned by the Entertainment Guild RPG engine. The VCC does **not** create these tables — they are provisioned by the RPG Session Engine build. The VCC MUST know they exist for cross-guild queries and NATS event payloads.
| **Table** | **Purpose** | **Key Columns** | **RLS** |
| `rpg_campaigns` | Campaign containers (worlds) | `id`, `tenant_id`, `title`, `world_seed`, `gm_user_id`, `status`, `tier` | ✅ tenant_id |
| `rpg_characters` | Player characters | `id`, `campaign_id`, `user_id`, `name`, `class`, `level`, `xp`, `stats JSONB`, `inventory JSONB` | ✅ via campaign |
| `rpg_sessions` | Individual play sessions | `id`, `campaign_id`, `started_at`, `ended_at`, `summary`, `xp_awarded`, `loot_dropped JSONB` | ✅ via campaign |
| `rpg_events` | In-session event log (combat, dialogue, rolls) | `id`, `session_id`, `event_type`, `payload JSONB`, `timestamp` | ✅ via session→campaign |
| `rpg_lore_fragments` | AI-generated world lore | `id`, `campaign_id`, `fragment_type`, `content TEXT`, `embedding vector(1536)`, `canonical BOOLEAN` | ✅ via campaign |
| `rpg_world_state` | Living world state (factions, locations, NPCs) | `id`, `campaign_id`, `state_key`, `state_value JSONB`, `last_mutated_by`, `version INT` | ✅ via campaign |
| `rpg_chapters` | Narrative chapters for Book Maker bridge | `id`, `campaign_id`, `chapter_number`, `title`, `prose TEXT`, `lore_fragment_ids JSONB`, `published BOOLEAN` | ✅ via campaign |

### 12.2.2 SaaS Extension Tables (10 tables)

These tables power the RPG Add-On SaaS monetization layer. **The VCC MUST integrate with these** for Stripe Connect creator payouts and marketplace commission processing.
| **Table** | **Purpose** | **Finance Guild Integration** |
| `rpg_subscriptions` | RPG tier subscriptions (Free → Guildmaster) | **Stripe Connect** — uses same `stripe_account_id` as Finance invoices |
| `rpg_session_usage` | Per-session metering for tier enforcement | Usage data feeds into Finance billing reports |
| `rpg_marketplace_listings` | Creator content listings (campaigns, assets, modules) | Listings have `price NUMERIC(12,2)` — same money type as Finance |
| `rpg_marketplace_purchases` | Purchase records | **70/30 split** via Stripe Connect `transfer_data` |
| `rpg_creator_payouts` | Creator payout ledger | **Finance commission engine** processes payouts — `citadel.rpg.payout.requested` → `smp-fin-worker` |
| `rpg_creator_profiles` | Creator identity and Stripe Connect status | Links to same `finance_integrations` Stripe Connect account |
| `rpg_usage_metering` | AI token usage, storage, session hours | Metering data → Finance recurring billing engine |
| `rpg_revenue_ledger` | Immutable revenue entries | Mirrors `finance_payments` pattern — same `NUMERIC(12,2)`, same audit trail |
| `rpg_agreements` | DocuSign creator agreements | Uses same DocuSign integration as Finance contracts (Phase 4) |
| `rpg_content_rights` | IP and content licensing rights | Rights enforcement gates marketplace listings |

---


## 12.3 NATS Subjects — Game Room

The VCC MUST subscribe to these subjects where Finance Guild integration is required. The VCC MUST NOT publish to `citadel.rpg.*` or `citadel.ent.*` — those namespaces are owned by the Entertainment Guild.

### Subjects VCC Subscribes To (read-only)

| **Subject** | **Payload** | **Finance Guild Action** |
| `citadel.rpg.payout.requested` | `{creator_id, amount, currency, stripe_account_id, campaign_id}` | `smp-fin-worker` processes payout via Stripe Connect transfer |
| `citadel.rpg.subscription.created` | `{user_id, tier, stripe_subscription_id, tenant_id}` | Log to `finance_audit_log`, update entitlement cache |
| `citadel.rpg.subscription.cancelled` | `{user_id, tier, stripe_subscription_id, reason}` | Log to `finance_audit_log`, revoke entitlements |
| `citadel.rpg.marketplace.purchased` | `{buyer_id, listing_id, amount, creator_id, split_amount}` | Process 70/30 split, log revenue to `rpg_revenue_ledger` |
| `citadel.rpg.session.completed` | `{session_id, campaign_id, xp_awarded, duration_minutes}` | Update usage metering for billing, award XP to FATE economy |
| `citadel.ent.room.created` | `{room_id, room_type, tenant_id, created_by}` | If `room_type = 'game_room'`, provision RPG entitlements for tenant |
| `citadel.ent.room.joined` | `{room_id, user_id, role}` | Log participant join for billing/metering |

### Subjects VCC Publishes (Finance → RPG)

| **Subject** | **Payload** | **When** |
| `citadel.finance.payout.completed` | `{payout_id, creator_id, amount, stripe_transfer_id, status}` | After `smp-fin-worker` completes a creator payout |
| `citadel.finance.subscription.payment_failed` | `{subscription_id, user_id, retry_count, next_retry_at}` | When Stripe webhook reports RPG subscription payment failure |
| `citadel.finance.entitlement.changed` | `{tenant_id, user_id, entitlements[], reason}` | When RPG tier change affects feature access |

## 12.4 RPG SaaS Tier Model

The VCC's Stripe Connect and entitlement systems MUST enforce these tiers:
| **Tier** | **Price** | **Stripe Product** | **Entitlements** |
| Free | $0/mo | — | 1 campaign, 3 players, 2 sessions/week, no marketplace, no Book Maker |
| Adventurer | $9.99/mo | `prod_rpg_adventurer` | 3 campaigns, 6 players, unlimited sessions, marketplace browse, basic lore export |
| Storyteller | $24.99/mo | `prod_rpg_storyteller` | 10 campaigns, 12 players, AI narrator, marketplace sell, Book Maker bridge, custom world seeds |
| Guildmaster | $49.99/mo | `prod_rpg_guildmaster` | Unlimited campaigns, unlimited players, priority AI, marketplace featured, full Book Maker pipeline, white-label |
| One-Shot | $4.99 (one-time) | `prod_rpg_oneshot` | Single pre-built campaign, 6 players, 1 session, no marketplace |
**VCC Entitlement Gate Rules:**
- ✅ `EntitlementGateMiddleware` MUST check `rpg:tier` before processing any marketplace or Book Maker request routed through Finance
- ✅ Free tier users MUST NOT trigger creator payouts or marketplace purchases
- ✅ Tier downgrades MUST NOT delete campaigns — they become read-only until re-upgraded
- ✅ One-Shot purchases use Stripe Checkout (one-time), not Stripe Subscriptions

## 12.5 Marketplace — 70/30 Revenue Split

The RPG marketplace uses Stripe Connect Express for creator payouts. **This shares the same Stripe Connect infrastructure as Finance Guild invoicing.** The VCC MUST handle marketplace transactions in `smp-fin-worker`.

### Split Logic

```python
# Marketplace revenue split — processed by smp-fin-worker
# on NATS event: citadel.rpg.marketplace.purchased

async def process_marketplace_purchase(event: MarketplacePurchaseEvent):
    """
    70/30 split: 70% to creator, 30% platform fee.
    Uses Stripe Connect transfer_data for automatic splitting.
    """
    CREATOR_SHARE = Decimal("0.70")
    PLATFORM_FEE = Decimal("0.30")
    
    listing = await get_marketplace_listing(event.listing_id)
    creator = await get_creator_profile(event.creator_id)
    
    if not creator.stripe_account_id:
        raise PayoutError(
            code="CREATOR_NOT_CONNECTED",
            message="Creator has not completed Stripe Connect onboarding"
        )
    
    amount_cents = int(event.amount * 100)
    creator_amount_cents = int(event.amount * CREATOR_SHARE * 100)
    
    # Create Stripe PaymentIntent with automatic transfer
    intent = stripe.PaymentIntent.create(
        amount=amount_cents,
        currency=event.currency or "usd",
        payment_method=event.payment_method_id,
        confirm=True,
        transfer_data={
            "destination": creator.stripe_account_id,
            "amount": creator_amount_cents,  # 70% to creator
        },
        metadata={
            "type": "rpg_marketplace",
            "listing_id": str(event.listing_id),
            "buyer_id": str(event.buyer_id),
            "creator_id": str(event.creator_id),
        },
        idempotency_key=f"mkt-{event.listing_id}-{event.buyer_id}-{event.timestamp}",
    )
    
    # Log to rpg_revenue_ledger (immutable)
    await insert_revenue_ledger_entry(
        listing_id=event.listing_id,
        buyer_id=event.buyer_id,
        creator_id=event.creator_id,
        gross_amount=event.amount,
        creator_share=event.amount * CREATOR_SHARE,
        platform_fee=event.amount * PLATFORM_FEE,
        stripe_payment_intent_id=intent.id,
        stripe_transfer_id=intent.transfer_data["destination"],
    )
    
    # Publish completion event
    await nats.publish("citadel.finance.payout.completed", {
        "payout_id": str(uuid4()),
        "creator_id": str(event.creator_id),
        "amount": float(event.amount * CREATOR_SHARE),
        "stripe_transfer_id": intent.latest_charge.transfer,
        "status": "completed",
    })
    
    # Log to finance_audit_log
    await audit_log(
        entity_type="rpg_marketplace_purchase",
        entity_id=str(event.listing_id),
        action="marketplace_purchase_processed",
        changes={"gross": float(event.amount), "creator_share": float(event.amount * CREATOR_SHARE)},
    )
```

---


## 12.6 Book Maker Bridge

The Book Maker bridge converts RPG campaign lore into publishable books/audiobooks via the 33-professor College pipeline. **Finance Guild handles the monetization side** — marketplace listing, pricing, creator payouts, and revenue tracking.

### Bridge Flow

```mermaid
flowchart LR
    RPG["Game Room\nRPG Session"] --> LORE["rpg_lore_fragments\n+ rpg_chapters"]
    LORE --> BRIDGE["Book Maker Bridge\n:8402"]
    BRIDGE --> COLLEGE["College Pipeline\n33 Professors"]
    COLLEGE --> BOOK["Published Book\n+ Audiobook"]
    BOOK --> MKT["RPG Marketplace\nListing"]
    MKT --> FIN["Finance Guild\nStripe 70/30 split"]
    FIN --> CREATOR["Creator Payout\nvia Stripe Connect"]
```
**VCC Integration Points:**
1. `smp-fin-worker` subscribes to `citadel.writer.book.published` → auto-creates marketplace listing with pricing from creator profile
1. `smp-fin-api` exposes `/api/finance/marketplace/listings` for RPG marketplace CRUD (read-only for non-Storyteller/Guildmaster tiers)
1. `smp-fin-api` exposes `/api/finance/marketplace/purchases` for purchase history and revenue reports
1. Creator payouts from book sales follow the same 70/30 split as direct marketplace purchases
**VCC MUST NOT:**
- 🚫 Build the Book Maker pipeline itself (owned by College/Entertainment Guild)
- 🚫 Build the 33-professor system (owned by College Guild)
- 🚫 Modify `rpg_lore_fragments` or `rpg_chapters` tables
- 🚫 Publish to `citadel.writer.*` namespace — only subscribe

## 12.7 Room Crossover Events

| **Crossover** | **Trigger** | **Finance Guild Action** |
| Game Room → Book Maker → Marketplace | RPG campaign lore exported as book | Auto-create marketplace listing, process purchases, pay creator 70% |
| Game Room → Studio Room | RPG session needs custom soundtrack/art | Log Studio Room commission request to `finance_commissions` if paid service |
| Deal Room → Game Room | Sales team gamifies client onboarding | Track gamification XP spend as marketing cost in Finance reports |
| Game Room → Finance Reports | RPG subscription/marketplace revenue | Aggregate RPG revenue into Finance dashboard stats (new revenue source category) |

## 12.9 Game Room Guardrails

**Additional guardrail rules for Game Room integration** — these supplement the 20+ rules in Section 3:
- 🚫 **NEVER modify **`**rpg_***`** tables directly** — Finance Guild reads from them but NEVER writes. All writes go through the RPG Session Engine on :8400
- 🚫 **NEVER publish to **`**citadel.rpg.***`** or **`**citadel.ent.***`** NATS namespaces** — Finance ONLY subscribes to these. Publishing is owned by Entertainment Guild.
- 🚫 **NEVER process a marketplace purchase without verifying the creator has an active Stripe Connect account** — check `rpg_creator_profiles.stripe_account_id IS NOT NULL`
- 🚫 **NEVER allow Free tier users to trigger marketplace purchases or creator payouts** — check `rpg_subscriptions.tier != 'free'` before processing
- 🚫 **NEVER use **`**FLOAT**`** for marketplace amounts** — same `NUMERIC(12,2)` rule as all Finance money columns
- 🚫 **NEVER split marketplace revenue without using Stripe Connect **`**transfer_data**` — manual transfers are error-prone and break reconciliation
- 🚫 **NEVER skip the **`**rpg_revenue_ledger**`** entry** — every marketplace transaction MUST have an immutable ledger row
- ✅ **ALWAYS use the same **`**Idempotency-Key**`** pattern for marketplace purchases** as for Finance invoices
- ✅ **ALWAYS log RPG-originated transactions to **`**finance_audit_log**` with `entity_type = 'rpg_marketplace_purchase'` or `'rpg_creator_payout'`
- ✅ **ALWAYS include **`**rpg_tier**`** in PostHog event properties** for marketplace/payout events — enables tier-segmented analytics

---


## 12.10 Game Room Health Checks

The VCC MUST extend the existing service health check to verify RPG integration connectivity:
```python
# Add to smp-fin-worker /health endpoint

async def check_rpg_integration_health() -> dict:
    """Verify RPG integration dependencies are reachable."""
    checks = {}
    
    # 1. NATS subscription active for RPG subjects
    try:
        sub_info = await nats_client.subscription_info("citadel.rpg.>")
        checks["nats_rpg_subscription"] = "connected" if sub_info.active else "disconnected"
    except Exception:
        checks["nats_rpg_subscription"] = "disconnected"
    
    # 2. RPG tables accessible (read-only)
    try:
        result = await supabase.table("rpg_marketplace_listings").select("id").limit(1).execute()
        checks["rpg_tables"] = "accessible"
    except Exception:
        checks["rpg_tables"] = "inaccessible"
    
    # 3. RPG Session Engine reachable
    try:
        resp = await httpx.get("http://localhost:8400/health", timeout=5)
        checks["rpg_engine"] = "healthy" if resp.status_code == 200 else "unhealthy"
    except Exception:
        checks["rpg_engine"] = "unreachable"
    
    return {
        "rpg_integration": checks,
        "rpg_integration_status": "healthy" if all(
            v in ("connected", "accessible", "healthy") for v in checks.values()
        ) else "degraded",
    }
```

[CALLOUT] 🚨 **Game Room integration health is a Phase 3+ dependency.** The RPG health check MUST pass before any marketplace or payout endpoints are enabled. If `rpg_engine` is unreachable, marketplace endpoints MUST return `503 {"error": "RPG_ENGINE_UNAVAILABLE"}` — not silently fail.

# 13. Music Pipeline (C.R.E.W.) Integration Blueprint


[CALLOUT] 🎵 **Purpose:** The Music Pipeline adds a full music reel player + AI song generation system to the C.R.E.W. engagement layer. It uses ElevenLabs Music Gen API for AI-generated tracks, S3+CloudFront for audio delivery, and NATS for real-time playback analytics. The VCC MUST understand how this integrates with the existing platform (shared Supabase, shared NATS bus, shared CDN) and where the boundaries lie.


---


## 13.1 Music Pipeline Architecture Overview


### Service Identity

| **Component** | **Stack** | **Location** | **NATS Namespace** |
| Music API Routes | FastAPI (Python) | `src/api/music/music_routes.py` | `citadel.music.*` |
| Music Reel Player | React 18 + Framer Motion | `src/components/music/MusicReelPlayer.tsx` | — |
| Song Gen Form | React 18 | `src/components/music/SongGenForm.tsx` | — |
| Audio CDN | S3 + CloudFront | Bucket: `citadel-audio` | — |
| AI Music Gen | ElevenLabs API | External service | `citadel.music.generate.*` |

---


## 13.2 Music Pipeline Supabase Schema


### 3 Core Tables

| **Table** | **Purpose** | **Key Columns** | **RLS** |
| `music_tracks` | Track metadata + CDN URLs | `id`, `tenant_id`, `title`, `artist`, `genre`, `duration_ms`, `s3_key`, `cdn_url`, `cover_art_url`, `bpm`, `mood`, `is_ai_generated`, `created_at` | ✅ tenant_id |
| `music_play_events` | Playback analytics (plays, skips, completes) | `id`, `track_id`, `visitor_id`, `event_type` (play|pause|skip|complete|mute|unmute|dismiss), `timestamp`, `duration_listened_ms`, `source_page` | ✅ via track→tenant |
| `music_gen_requests` | AI song generation jobs | `id`, `visitor_id`, `prompt`, `genre`, `mood`, `duration_target_ms`, `status` (pending|processing|completed|failed), `result_track_id`, `elevenlabs_job_id`, `error_message`, `created_at`, `completed_at` | ✅ visitor_id scoped |
**Migration:** `20260227_music_pipeline.sql` — idempotent, all tables use `gen_random_uuid()`, all timestamps are `TIMESTAMPTZ`, RLS enabled on all tables.

---


## 13.3 Music Pipeline FastAPI Endpoints

All routes live in `src/api/music/music_routes.py` — 5 endpoints:
| **Method** | **Path** | **Purpose** | **Auth** | **NATS Event** |
| GET | `/music/reel` | Fetch paginated music reel (cursor-based) | Public (visitor_id cookie) | — |
| POST | `/music/event` | Log playback event (play, pause, skip, etc.) | Public (visitor_id cookie) | `citadel.music.{event_type}` |
| POST | `/music/generate` | Submit AI song generation request | Authenticated (JWT) | `citadel.music.generate.requested` |
| GET | `/music/status/{id}` | Poll generation job status | Authenticated (JWT) | — |
| GET | `/music/my-songs/{visitor_id}` | List user's generated songs | Authenticated (JWT) | — |

## 13.4 Music Pipeline NATS Subjects

10 subjects under `citadel.music.*`:
| **Subject** | **Payload** | **Publisher** |
| `citadel.music.play` | `{track_id, visitor_id, timestamp}` | Music API on play event |
| `citadel.music.pause` | `{track_id, visitor_id, position_ms}` | Music API on pause |
| `citadel.music.skip` | `{track_id, visitor_id, skipped_at_ms}` | Music API on skip |
| `citadel.music.mute` | `{track_id, visitor_id}` | Music API on mute |
| `citadel.music.unmute` | `{track_id, visitor_id}` | Music API on unmute |
| `citadel.music.complete` | `{track_id, visitor_id, duration_ms}` | Music API on track complete |
| `citadel.music.dismiss` | `{track_id, visitor_id}` | Music API on reel dismiss |
| `citadel.music.generate.requested` | `{request_id, visitor_id, prompt, genre, mood}` | Music API on gen submit |
| `citadel.music.generate.completed` | `{request_id, track_id, cdn_url, duration_ms}` | Worker on gen complete |
| `citadel.music.generate.failed` | `{request_id, error_code, error_message}` | Worker on gen failure |

---


## 13.5 ElevenLabs Music Gen Integration

**API Flow:**
1. User submits prompt via `/music/generate` → row inserted into `music_gen_requests` with `status: pending`
1. Worker picks up request → calls ElevenLabs Music Generation API with prompt, genre, mood, duration
1. On success → ElevenLabs returns audio file → worker uploads to S3 bucket `citadel-audio` → creates `music_tracks` row with CDN URL → updates `music_gen_requests.status = completed`
1. On failure → updates `music_gen_requests.status = failed` with error message → publishes `citadel.music.generate.failed`
**VCC MUST NOT:**
- 🚫 Call ElevenLabs API directly from the frontend — always proxy through FastAPI
- 🚫 Store ElevenLabs API key in client code — backend env var only
- 🚫 Allow unlimited generation requests — rate limit: 5 requests/hour per visitor
- 🚫 Serve audio files directly from S3 — always use CloudFront CDN URL

---


## 13.6 Frontend Components


### `MusicReelPlayer.tsx` — Persistent Player

- Renders as a persistent bottom bar (similar to Spotify mini-player)
- Framer Motion `layoutId` transitions between mini and expanded states
- Auto-advances through reel tracks
- Controls: play/pause, skip, mute/unmute, dismiss
- Each interaction fires POST `/music/event` → NATS event
- Uses `useFinanceWS` pattern for real-time track additions

### `SongGenForm.tsx` — AI Song Generator

- Route: `/crew/make-your-song`
- Form fields: prompt (text), genre (select), mood (select), duration (slider 30s–180s)
- Debounced submit with loading state
- Polls `/music/status/{id}` every 3s until completed/failed
- On completion, auto-plays generated track in `MusicReelPlayer`
- Requires authentication (JWT)

| **Workflow** | **Trigger** | **Action** |

| SES Follow-Up | `citadel.music.generate.completed` | Send email to user with download link + share CTA |
| Lead Capture | `citadel.music.play` (first play by visitor) | Capture visitor as lead in CRM pipeline |
| Daily Digest | Cron (daily 9am) | Aggregate play stats → post to #analytics Slack channel |
| Conversion Tracker | `citadel.music.generate.requested` | Track visitor→user conversion funnel in PostHog |

# 14. Social Engagement Pipeline (C.R.E.W.) Integration Blueprint


[CALLOUT] 📱 **Purpose:** The Social Engagement Pipeline is the 60-second content delivery and community engagement system for C.R.E.W. It distributes content across 8 channels (Instagram, TikTok, YouTube, X, LinkedIn, Reddit, Blog, Direct DM/Email/SMS), provides a real-time social feed with WebSocket support, and includes polls, bookmarks, drafts, content moderation, push notifications, and a full search engine. This is a **massive subsystem** — 15+ Supabase tables, 11 FastAPI route files, WebSocket layer, 14 SRS codes.


---


## 14.1 Social Engagement Architecture Overview


### Service Identity

| **Component** | **Stack** | **Location** | **NATS Namespace** |
| Social API (11 route files) | FastAPI (Python) | `src/api/social/` | `citadel.social.*` |
| Social WebSocket | FastAPI WebSocket | `src/ws/social.py` | `citadel.social.presence.*` |
| Social Feed UI | React 18 | `src/components/social/` | — |
| 8-Channel Distributor | n8n + platform APIs | n8n workflows | `citadel.social.content.distributed` |

### 8-Channel Distribution Matrix

| **Channel** | **API** | **Content Types** | **Delivery SLA** |
| Instagram | Graph API | Reels, Stories, Posts | ≤ 60s |
| TikTok | Content Posting API | Short-form video | ≤ 60s |
| YouTube | Data API v3 | Shorts, Videos | ≤ 120s |
| X (Twitter) | v2 API | Tweets, Threads | ≤ 30s |
| LinkedIn | Marketing API | Posts, Articles | ≤ 60s |
| Reddit | API | Posts, Comments | ≤ 60s |
| Blog | Internal CMS | Long-form articles | ≤ 120s |
| Direct (DM/Email/SMS) | SES + SNS + WS | Personalized messages | ≤ 30s |

## 14.2 Social Engagement Supabase Schema


### 15+ Tables

| **Table** | **Purpose** | **Key Columns** |
| `crew_social_requests` | Content creation requests from operators | `id`, `tenant_id`, `requester_id`, `content_type`, `prompt`, `channels[]`, `status`, `scheduled_at` |
| `crew_social_content` | Generated content pieces | `id`, `request_id`, `body`, `media_urls[]`, `format`, `channel_variants JSONB`, `ai_confidence_score` |
| `crew_social_deliveries` | Per-channel delivery tracking | `id`, `content_id`, `channel`, `platform_post_id`, `status`, `delivered_at`, `error_message` |
| `crew_social_engagement` | Engagement metrics per delivery | `id`, `delivery_id`, `likes`, `comments`, `shares`, `views`, `clicks`, `snapshot_at` |
| `crew_social_polls` | Community polls | `id`, `tenant_id`, `question`, `options JSONB`, `expires_at`, `is_anonymous`, `created_by` |
| `crew_social_poll_votes` | Poll vote records | `id`, `poll_id`, `voter_id`, `option_index`, `voted_at` |
| `crew_social_bookmarks` | User content bookmarks | `id`, `user_id`, `content_id`, `created_at` |
| `crew_social_drafts` | Saved content drafts | `id`, `user_id`, `tenant_id`, `body`, `media_urls[]`, `channels[]`, `last_edited_at` |
| `crew_push_tokens` | Device push notification tokens | `id`, `user_id`, `token`, `platform` (ios|android|web), `created_at` |
| `crew_push_log` | Push notification delivery log | `id`, `user_id`, `title`, `body`, `status`, `sent_at` |
| `crew_social_reports` | Content moderation reports | `id`, `reporter_id`, `content_id`, `reason`, `status` (pending|reviewed|actioned|dismissed), `reviewed_by` |
| `crew_social_appeals` | Moderation action appeals | `id`, `report_id`, `appellant_id`, `reason`, `status`, `reviewed_by`, `resolved_at` |
| `crew_social_preferences` | User notification/feed preferences | `id`, `user_id`, `email_digest`, `push_enabled`, `channels_visible[]`, `feed_algorithm` |
| `crew_social_hashtags` | Hashtag registry | `id`, `tag`, `usage_count`, `trending_score`, `created_at` |
| `crew_social_content_hashtags` | Content ↔ hashtag junction | `content_id`, `hashtag_id` |
**Migration:** `20260227_social_engagement.sql` — idempotent, all tables use `gen_random_uuid()`, all timestamps `TIMESTAMPTZ`, RLS on all tables, `pg_trgm` extension enabled for search.

## 14.4 Social Engagement WebSocket Layer

`src/ws/social.py` — Real-time social feed updates using NATS JetStream fan-out:
```python
# WebSocket connection pattern for social feed
# Each connected client subscribes to their tenant's social events
# NATS JetStream provides durable delivery + replay on reconnect

async def social_ws_handler(websocket: WebSocket, tenant_id: str, user_id: str):
    await websocket.accept()
    
    # Subscribe to tenant-scoped social events via NATS
    subjects = [
        f"citadel.social.content.{tenant_id}",
        f"citadel.social.poll.{tenant_id}",
        f"citadel.social.presence.{tenant_id}",
    ]
    
    async for msg in nats_subscribe(subjects):
        event = json.loads(msg.data)
        # Filter based on user preferences
        if should_deliver(event, user_id):
            await websocket.send_json(event)
```

| `citadel.social.content.*` | `.created`, `.updated`, `.deleted`, `.published`, `.distributed`, `.scheduled` |
| `citadel.social.poll.*` | `.created`, `.voted`, `.closed`, `.results` |
| `citadel.social.report.*` | `.submitted`, `.reviewed`, `.actioned`, `.dismissed` |
| `citadel.social.appeal.*` | `.submitted`, `.reviewed`, `.resolved` |
| `citadel.social.push.*` | `.sent`, `.delivered`, `.failed`, `.clicked` |
| `citadel.social.presence.*` | `.online`, `.offline`, `.typing` |
| `citadel.social.spam.*` | `.detected`, `.blocked`, `.false_positive` |

---


## 14.6 Social Engagement — Search, Rate Limiting & Spam


### Search Engine

- Uses PostgreSQL `pg_trgm` extension for fuzzy text search
- Indexed columns: `crew_social_content.body`, `crew_social_hashtags.tag`
- Supports: keyword search, hashtag search (`#tag`), user search (`@user`)
- Cursor-based pagination on all search results

### Rate Limiting

- Content creation: 10 posts/hour per user
- Poll creation: 3 polls/day per user
- Report submission: 5 reports/hour per user
- Push notifications: 50/day per user
- All limits enforced via Upstash Redis sliding window

### Spam Detection

- Pre-publish content scan for known spam patterns
- Duplicate content detection (Jaccard similarity threshold: 0.8)
- New account velocity check (accounts < 24h old: 2 posts/day max)
- Flagged content auto-held for moderation review
- NATS events: `citadel.social.spam.detected` → moderation queue

### Social Engagement Guardrails

- 🚫 **NEVER publish to external channels without operator approval** — drafts must be explicitly published
- 🚫 **NEVER store platform API keys in client code** — all channel APIs proxied through backend
- 🚫 **NEVER skip spam detection on content creation** — every post passes through spam filter
- 🚫 **NEVER allow anonymous poll creation** — require authenticated user
- 🚫 **NEVER send push notifications without user opt-in** — check `crew_social_preferences.push_enabled`
- 🚫 **NEVER expose moderation reporter identity to content author** — reports are anonymous
- 🚫 **NEVER use offset-based pagination on feeds** — cursor-based only (high-volume table)
- 🚫 **NEVER allow direct WebSocket writes to NATS** — WS is read-only fan-out, all writes go through REST
- ✅ **ALWAYS enforce rate limits via Upstash Redis** — sliding window pattern
- ✅ **ALWAYS log content moderation actions to audit trail** — compliance requirement
- ✅ **ALWAYS include **`**tenant_id**`** + **`**channel**`** in PostHog events** — enables per-channel analytics
- ✅ **ALWAYS use **`**pg_trgm**`** GIN indexes for search** — never `LIKE '%term%'` sequential scans

# 15. Nemesis Defense System Integration Blueprint


[CALLOUT] 🛡️ **Purpose:** Nemesis is the Citadel platform's **6-layer defense + Red Team** security system. It covers everything from perimeter firewall (nftables/CrowdSec) to AI-powered threat detection, honeypots, ML classifiers, infrastructure hardening (Ansible/NATS TLS/Helm), compliance scanning (SAST/DAST/WAF/Terraform), and an automated Red Team with 7 attack scanners. The VCC MUST integrate with Nemesis for security event logging, Datadog metric publishing, PostHog feature flags, and diagnostic endpoints.


---


## 15.1 Nemesis Architecture — 6 Layers + Red Team

| **Layer** | **Name** | **Components** | **Key Files** |
| **L1** | Perimeter | nftables firewall, CrowdSec, GeoIP blocking, IP reputation | `nemesis/layer1/nftables_rules.sh`, `crowdsec_config.yaml`, `geoip_filter.py` |
| **L2** | Inspector | AI firewall middleware, request fingerprinting, anomaly detection | `nemesis/layer2/inspector_middleware.py`, `request_fingerprint.py`, `anomaly_detector.py` |
| **L3** | Hunter | Honeypots, decoy endpoints, trap databases, attacker profiling | `nemesis/layer3/honeypot_routes.py`, `decoy_db.py`, `attacker_profiler.py` |
| **L4** | Oracle | ML threat classifier, geo-risk scoring, model retraining pipeline | `nemesis/layer4/oracle_classifier.py`, `geo_risk.py`, `retrain_pipeline.py` |
| **L5** | Shield | Ansible hardening playbooks, NATS TLS rotation, Helm chart security | `nemesis/layer5/ansible/`, `nats_tls_rotator.py`, `helm_security_values.yaml` |
| **L6** | Compliance | SAST scanner, DAST runner, WAF rules, Terraform security policies | `nemesis/layer6/sast_scanner.py`, `dast_runner.py`, `waf_rules.yaml`, `terraform_policies/` |
| **RT** | Red Team | 7 automated attack scanners + campaign manager | `nemesis/redteam/scanner_*.py`, `campaign_manager.py` |

### Red Team Scanners (7)

| **Scanner** | **File** | **What It Tests** |
| Injection Scanner | `scanner_inject.py` | SQL injection, XSS, command injection, LDAP injection |
| LLM Scanner | `scanner_llm.py` | Prompt injection, jailbreak attempts, data exfiltration via AI |
| Recon Scanner | `scanner_recon.py` | Port scanning, service enumeration, DNS zone transfer |
| Auth Scanner | `scanner_auth.py` | Brute force, credential stuffing, token replay, session fixation |
| Honeypot Scanner | `scanner_honey.py` | Tests that honeypots (L3) correctly detect and log attacker behavior |
| Exfil Scanner | `scanner_exfil.py` | Data exfiltration via DNS tunneling, steganography, side-channels |
| Campaign Manager | `campaign_manager.py` | Orchestrates multi-scanner campaigns, produces consolidated Red Team report |

---


## 15.2 Nemesis Install Script

`scripts/nemesis_full_install.sh` — 10-phase installation with flags:
```bash
# Full install
bash scripts/nemesis_full_install.sh

# Dry run (no changes)
bash scripts/nemesis_full_install.sh --dry-run

# Skip database migrations
bash scripts/nemesis_full_install.sh --skip-migrations

# Install specific layers only
bash scripts/nemesis_full_install.sh --layer L1,L2,L4

# Install Red Team only
bash scripts/nemesis_full_install.sh --layer RT
```
**10 Install Phases:**
1. Validate environment variables
1. Run Supabase migrations (4 migration files)
1. Deploy L1 Perimeter (nftables + CrowdSec)
1. Deploy L2 Inspector (AI middleware)
1. Deploy L3 Hunter (honeypots)
1. Deploy L4 Oracle (ML classifier)
1. Deploy L5 Shield (Ansible + NATS TLS)
1. Deploy L6 Compliance (SAST/DAST/WAF)
1. Deploy Red Team scanners
1. Run diagnostic health check on all layers

---

| `20260226_nemesis.sql` | `nemesis_events`, `nemesis_threats`, `nemesis_blocked_ips`, `nemesis_fingerprints` | Core threat detection and event storage |
| `20260226_shield.sql` | `nemesis_shield_runs`, `nemesis_tls_certs`, `nemesis_hardening_log` | Infrastructure hardening audit trail |
| `20260226_compliance.sql` | `nemesis_sast_results`, `nemesis_dast_results`, `nemesis_waf_events`, `nemesis_policy_violations` | Compliance scanning results |
| `20260226_redteam.sql` | `nemesis_rt_campaigns`, `nemesis_rt_findings`, `nemesis_rt_reports` | Red Team campaign tracking and findings |

## 15.4 Nemesis NATS Streams

3 JetStream streams:
| **Stream** | **Subjects** | **Retention** | **Purpose** |
| `CITADEL_NEMESIS` | `citadel.nemesis.event.*`, `citadel.nemesis.threat.*`, `citadel.nemesis.block.*` | Limits, 30 days | Core security events, threat detections, IP blocks |
| `CITADEL_NEMESIS_ALERTS` | `citadel.nemesis.alert.*`, `citadel.nemesis.escalation.*` | Limits, 90 days | High-priority alerts, escalation to operators |
| `CITADEL_RED_TEAM` | `citadel.nemesis.redteam.scan.*`, `citadel.nemesis.redteam.campaign.*`, `citadel.nemesis.redteam.finding.*` | Limits, 90 days | Red Team scan results, campaign status, findings |

## 15.5 Nemesis Datadog Integration

`nemesis_datadog.py` — **25+ metric functions** for real-time security observability:

### Key Metrics

- `nemesis.threats.detected` (counter) — per layer, per threat type
- `nemesis.threats.blocked` (counter) — successful blocks
- `nemesis.threats.missed` (counter) — threats that evaded detection (found by Red Team)
- `nemesis.layer.latency` (histogram) — per-layer processing time
- `nemesis.honeypot.visits` (counter) — honeypot interaction count
- `nemesis.oracle.confidence` (gauge) — ML classifier confidence score
- `nemesis.oracle.retrain.count` (counter) — model retrain events
- `nemesis.firewall.rules.active` (gauge) — active nftables rules
- `nemesis.crowdsec.decisions` (counter) — CrowdSec ban/captcha decisions
- `nemesis.tls.cert.expiry_days` (gauge) — days until TLS cert expiry
- `nemesis.compliance.sast.findings` (counter) — SAST vulnerability findings by severity
- `nemesis.compliance.dast.findings` (counter) — DAST vulnerability findings
- `nemesis.redteam.findings` (counter) — Red Team findings by severity
- `nemesis.redteam.campaign.duration` (histogram) — campaign execution time

### Dashboard: `datadog_nemesis_dashboard.json`

- 12 widgets covering all 6 layers + Red Team
- 6 monitors with Terraform provisioning (`datadog_monitors.tf`)

### Terraform Monitors (`datadog_monitors.tf` — 5 monitors)

1. **Threat Spike** — alert if `nemesis.threats.detected` > 100/min
1. **Layer Down** — alert if any layer health check fails for > 5min
1. **Oracle Drift** — alert if ML classifier confidence drops below 0.7 for > 15min
1. **TLS Expiry** — warn at 30 days, critical at 7 days before cert expiry
1. **Red Team Critical** — alert on any critical-severity Red Team finding

---


## 15.6 Nemesis PostHog Integration

`nemesis_posthog.py` — Feature flags, session replay hooks, and security events:

### Feature Flags

- `nemesis-l2-inspector-enabled` — toggle AI inspector middleware (per-tenant)
- `nemesis-l3-honeypots-enabled` — toggle honeypot layer
- `nemesis-l4-oracle-enabled` — toggle ML classifier
- `nemesis-redteam-enabled` — toggle automated Red Team scans
- `nemesis-strict-mode` — enable maximum security (blocks borderline threats)

### Session Replay Hooks

- Tag sessions with `security_risk_score` for replay filtering
- Mark sessions that triggered security events for analyst review
- Capture blocked request metadata (without PII) for debugging

### Events

- `nemesis.threat_detected` — properties: `layer`, `threat_type`, `severity`, `action_taken`
- `nemesis.ip_blocked` — properties: `ip_hash`, `reason`, `duration`, `layer`
- `nemesis.redteam_finding` — properties: `scanner`, `severity`, `category`, `remediation`

---


## 15.7 Nemesis Diagnostics

`nemesis_diagnostics.py` + `nemesis_diagnostics_api.py` at `/api/nemesis/diagnostics/*`:

### Endpoints

- `GET /api/nemesis/diagnostics/health` — all-layer health check (L1–L6 + RT)
- `GET /api/nemesis/diagnostics/status` — current threat level, active blocks, recent events
- `GET /api/nemesis/diagnostics/layers/{layer}` — per-layer deep diagnostic
- `GET /api/nemesis/diagnostics/redteam/latest` — latest Red Team campaign results
- `POST /api/nemesis/diagnostics/test` — trigger diagnostic self-test (admin only)
**All diagnostic endpoints require **`**NEMESIS_ADMIN_TOKEN**`** in the Authorization header.**

### Nemesis Guardrails

- 🚫 **NEVER disable Nemesis in production** — `NEMESIS_ENABLED=false` is for dev/staging ONLY
- 🚫 **NEVER log raw PII in threat events** — encrypt with `PII_ENCRYPTION_KEY` before storage
- 🚫 **NEVER expose diagnostic endpoints without **`**NEMESIS_ADMIN_TOKEN**` — these reveal internal security posture
- 🚫 **NEVER run Red Team scanners against production without operator approval** — use `--dry-run` flag
- 🚫 **NEVER trust client-provided IP addresses** — always use `X-Forwarded-For` with trusted proxy validation
- 🚫 **NEVER skip L2 Inspector middleware on any public endpoint** — it is the first line of AI defense
- 🚫 **NEVER store MaxMind GeoIP database in the repo** — download at runtime via license key
- 🚫 **NEVER publish security findings to public NATS subjects** — use `CITADEL_NEMESIS_ALERTS` stream (restricted consumers)
- ✅ **ALWAYS rotate **`**NEMESIS_ADMIN_TOKEN**`** every 90 days** — via Vault or ECS Secrets Manager
- ✅ **ALWAYS include **`**layer**`**, **`**threat_type**`**, and **`**severity**`** in all Datadog metrics** — enables per-layer dashboards
- ✅ **ALWAYS run diagnostic self-test after any Nemesis config change** — `POST /api/nemesis/diagnostics/test`
- ✅ **ALWAYS tag PostHog sessions with **`**security_risk_score**` — enables analyst filtering

[CALLOUT] 🚨 **Nemesis is a Phase 2 hard dependency.** No guild module proceeds to Phase 3 without Nemesis L1–L4 active and passing health checks. Red Team (L5–L6 + RT) deploys in Phase 3. The full install script MUST pass `--dry-run` before any real deployment.

# 16. Safe Auto-Build Pipeline — `_execute_vcc_build()` Implementation Requirements


[CALLOUT] 🚨 **CRITICAL GAP:** The current `_execute_vcc_build()` in `tools/vcc_automation_loop.py` is a **7-line placeholder** that returns `{"success": True}` without doing anything. The telemetry assessment (READ + THINK + DD/PH) works, but **the actual build execution is empty**. This section defines the 14 gaps that must be filled to enable safe, auditable, automatic build-out from blueprint.


## 16.1 Gap Audit — Current vs Required

| **#** | **Gap** | **What's Missing** | **Severity** | **SRS Code** |

## 16.2 Required Build Pipeline — `_execute_vcc_build()` Implementation


[CALLOUT] 🔧 **This is the 12-step pipeline that **`**_execute_vcc_build(phase)**`** MUST execute.** Each step has a pass/fail gate. If any CRITICAL gate fails, the pipeline halts and publishes a NO-GO to `citadel.vcc.build.failed`. The cycle report is still generated (documenting the failure).

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    A["1. Pre-flight: Load crp_config.yaml"] --> B["2. Diff Check L1: Spec to Code"]
    B --> C["3. Code Generation: write_codegen via Bedrock"]
    C --> D["4. Blueprint Storage: write_code_blueprints to Notion"]
    D --> E["5. Diff Check L2: Cycle to Cycle git diff"]
    E --> F["6. Test Suite: pytest --cov >= 80%"]
    F --> G["7. Quality Gates: lint + CAPS + guardrails"]
    G --> H["8. Governance Audit: 8 scopes"]
    H --> I["9. Diff Check L3: Blueprint to Blueprint"]
    I --> J["10. Cycle Report: 8-section Notion page"]
    J --> K["11. DD/PH metrics for build cycle"]
    K --> L["12. Rollback checkpoint: save SHA"]
```

### Step 1 — Pre-flight: Load SRS Registry

- Load `config/crp_config.yaml` containing all 35+ SRS codes with their expected artifacts (route file, service file, test file, component, types)
- Resolve current phase from `.vcc_state.json` cross-referenced with filesystem scan (Rule Zero)
- Determine which SRS codes are in scope for the current phase
- **Gate:** `crp_config.yaml` must exist and parse without errors → CRITICAL

### Step 2 — Diff Check Layer 1: Spec → Code

- Run `vcc_diff_checker.py --layer spec-to-code --phase {phase}`
- For each in-scope SRS code, check if the expected artifact files exist on disk
- Output: list of missing artifacts, list of existing artifacts, coverage percentage
- **Gate:** Coverage must be ≥ previous cycle's coverage (no regression) → HIGH

### Step 3 — Code Generation

- Import `write_codegen()` from `perplexity_control_loop_v2.py`
- For each missing artifact from Step 2, generate code via Bedrock Claude
- Generated code MUST pass Rule Zero codebase scan before writing to disk
- All generated files saved to `build/staging/` first (NOT directly to `src/`)
- **Gate:** All generated files must pass syntax check (`python -m py_compile` / `tsc --noEmit`) → CRITICAL

### Step 4 — Blueprint Storage

- Import `write_code_blueprints()` from `perplexity_control_loop_v2.py`
- Push generated code blueprints to Notion for audit trail
- Each blueprint page includes: SRS code, file path, code content, generation model, timestamp
- **Gate:** Notion API returns 200 for all blueprint posts → LOW (non-blocking)

### Step 5 — Diff Check Layer 2: Cycle → Cycle

- Run `git diff --stat HEAD~1..HEAD` (or between last CRP cycle SHA and current)
- Compute: files changed, insertions, deletions, net change
- Flag any unexpected changes outside `src/api/finance/`, `src/components/finance/`, `tests/`
- **Gate:** No changes outside allowed directories without `DRIFT-ACK` annotation → HIGH

### Step 6 — Test Suite

- Run full test suite: `pytest tests/ --cov=src/api/finance --cov-report=json -v`
- Parse coverage report: must be ≥ 80% line coverage
- Run targeted tests: `pytest tests/ -k "rls"` (RLS isolation), `pytest tests/ -k "entitlement"` (entitlement gates), `pytest tests/ -k "rbac"` (role-based access)
- **Gate:** Coverage ≥ 80% AND 0 test failures → CRITICAL

### Step 7 — Quality Gates

- **Lint:** `ruff check src/api/finance/ --select E,W,F,I` + `eslint src/components/finance/` + `sqlfluff lint supabase/migrations/`
- **CAPS Score:** Run AIMB pipeline on all 5 SMP services → all must score ≥ B (70)
- **Guardrails:** Full-repo scan using 20+ guardrail rules from `crp_config.yaml` → 0 critical violations
- **Gate:** All three sub-gates pass → CRITICAL

### Step 8 — Governance Audit

- Run `guild_auditor.py --phase {phase} --services smp-fin-api,smp-fin-ws,smp-fin-worker,smp-fin-pdf,smp-fin-ai`
- 8 audit scopes: Schema Compliance, RLS Coverage, SRS Coverage Matrix, CAPS Scorecard, Guardrails Report, Entitlement Matrix, Observability Checklist, Diff Summary
- **Gate:** All 8 scopes pass with 0 blocking failures → HIGH

### Step 9 — Diff Check Layer 3: Blueprint → Blueprint

- Run `vcc_diff_checker.py --layer blueprint-to-blueprint`
- Compare current Notion blueprint snapshot against previous cycle's snapshot
- Flag any unacknowledged blueprint drift (spec changes without corresponding code changes)
- **Gate:** All layers report `clean: true` or changes are `DRIFT-ACK` annotated → MEDIUM

### Step 10 — Cycle Report

- Generate 8-section CRP cycle report and post to Notion:
  - §1 — Cycle ID + Phase + Timestamp
  - §2 — SRS Status Matrix (code × artifact type)
  - §3 — Git Commits (files changed, insertions, deletions)
  - §4 — Diff Check Results (3 layers)
  - §5 — Test Results (passed, failed, coverage %)
  - §6 — Quality Gate Results (lint, CAPS, guardrails)
  - §7 — Health Metrics (Perplexity diagnostic, OAD status, bridge status, SLA compliance, trends)
  - §8 — Next Cycle Intent (what VCC plans to build next)
- **Gate:** Report must validate against CRP schema (all 8 sections present) → HIGH

### Step 11 — DD/PH Build Metrics

- Submit build cycle metrics to Datadog: `vcc.build.duration`, `vcc.build.files_generated`, `vcc.build.test_coverage`, `vcc.build.guardrail_violations`, `vcc.build.caps_composite`
- Capture `vcc.build_cycle_complete` event to PostHog with phase, SRS codes touched, GO/NO-GO
- Publish `citadel.vcc.cycle.completed` NATS event (triggers Perplexity via Phase 2.1 bridge)
- **Gate:** At least DD OR PH submission succeeds → LOW (non-blocking, uses `analytics_retry` backoff)

### Step 12 — Rollback Checkpoint

- Save current `git rev-parse HEAD` as the rollback SHA in `.vcc_state.json` and `vcc_loop_state`
- Verify DOWN migrations exist for any new UP migrations created in this cycle
- Record feature flag state for any new Phase 3+ features
- **Gate:** SHA saved successfully → MEDIUM

## 16.4 GitLab CI Quality Gates (G0–G10)


[CALLOUT] 🔒 **These 11 CI stages run on every push to **`**main**`** or **`**develop**`**.** The VCC automation loop's Step 7 mirrors these gates locally before committing. The CI pipeline is the second line of defense — it catches anything the local gates missed.

| **Gate** | **Stage Name** | **What It Does** | **Pass Criteria** | **Blocking?** |
| G0 | `notify-notion-commit` | Mirror commit to Notion via `tools/notify_notion_commit.py` | Notion API 200 | No |
| G1 | `lint` | Python (`ruff`), Frontend (`eslint`), SQL (`sqlfluff`) | 0 errors | Yes |
| G2 | `test:backend` | `pytest tests/ --cov` with coverage report | Coverage ≥ 80%, 0 failures | Yes |
| G3 | `test:rls + test:entitlements` | Cross-tenant RLS probes + entitlement gate tests | 0 leaks, all gates enforced | Yes |
| G4 | `build` | Build all 5 SMP microservices + frontend bundle | All builds succeed | Yes |
| G5 | `caps-score` | AIMB CAPS scoring on all SMP profiles | All services ≥ B (70) | Yes |
| G6 | `guardrails` | Full-repo scan against 20+ guardrail rules | 0 critical violations | Yes |
| G7 | `guild-audit` | Run `guild_auditor.py` on 8 audit scopes | All scopes pass | Yes |
| G8 | `smoke-test` | Health probe on staging after deploy | All `/health` endpoints return 200 | Yes |
| G9 | `deploy:prod` | Manual approval gate → ECS stagger deploy | Operator approval | Yes (manual) |
| G10 | `vcc-cycle-report` | Post CRP cycle report to Notion + DD deploy event | Report posted + DD event sent | No |

## 16.5 Implementation Priority Order


[CALLOUT] 📋 **VCC must implement these gaps in this exact order.** Each step depends on the previous. Do not skip ahead. Post a CRP cycle report after completing each priority tier.


### Tier 1 — Foundation (Must exist before any auto-build)

1. **SRS Registry** (`config/crp_config.yaml`) — without this, nothing can be tracked
1. **3-Layer Diff Checker** (`tools/vcc_diff_checker.py`) — without this, no audit trail
1. **Test Harness** (`tests/conftest.py` + 10 test files) — without this, no safety net

### Tier 2 — Build Execution (Core pipeline)

1. **Build Execution Engine** — implement full 12-step `_execute_vcc_build()` in `vcc_automation_loop.py`
1. **Codegen Integration** — wire `write_codegen()` + `write_code_blueprints()` into Steps 3-4
1. **Cycle Report** (`tools/vcc_cycle_reporter.py`) — 8-section CRP report per cycle

### Tier 3 — Quality & Governance (Gates before deploy)

1. **GitLab CI Pipeline** (`.gitlab-ci.yml`) — 11-stage G0–G10 pipeline
1. **Governance Audit** (`tools/guild_auditor.py`) — 8-scope audit system
1. **Datadog Backend** (`dd_bootstrap.py`, `dd_middleware.py`, `dd_metrics.py`)
1. **PostHog Frontend** (`PostHogProvider.tsx`, `useFinanceCapture.ts`)

### Tier 4 — Hardening (Safety nets)

1. **Rollback Integration** — wire `rollback_agent.py` + DOWN migrations
1. **Idempotency Enforcement** — `x-idempotency-key` on all financial writes
1. **NATS Event Publishing** — all write ops → `citadel.finance.*`
1. **Artifact Storage** — `build/diffs/`, `build/reports/` with naming convention

## 16.6 `_execute_vcc_build()` — Implementation Skeleton

```python
async def _execute_vcc_build(self, phase: Optional[str]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """Execute the full VCC build pipeline.
    
    12-step pipeline with pass/fail gates at each step.
    If any CRITICAL gate fails, pipeline halts and publishes NO-GO.
    Cycle report is always generated (even on failure).
    """
    from tools.perplexity_control_loop_v2 import write_codegen, write_code_blueprints
    
    pipeline = BuildPipeline(phase=phase)
    
    # Step 1: Pre-flight — Load SRS registry
    config = pipeline.load_crp_config("config/crp_config.yaml")
    if not config:
        return pipeline.fail("crp_config.yaml not found or invalid")
    
    # Step 2: Diff Check L1 — Spec→Code
    spec_diff = pipeline.run_diff_check(layer="spec-to-code", phase=phase)
    missing_artifacts = spec_diff.get("missing", [])
    
    # Step 3: Code Generation
    if missing_artifacts:
        # Rule Zero: scan codebase FIRST
        scan_result = pipeline.scan_codebase()
        generated = []
        for artifact in missing_artifacts:
            code = await write_codegen(
                srs_code=artifact["srs_code"],
                artifact_type=artifact["type"],
                context=scan_result,
                model="bedrock-claude-haiku"
            )
            # Write to staging, NOT src/ directly
            pipeline.write_to_staging(artifact["path"], code)
            generated.append(artifact)
        
        # Syntax check all generated files
        syntax_ok = pipeline.syntax_check("build/staging/")
        if not syntax_ok:
            return pipeline.fail("Generated code has syntax errors")
    
    # Step 4: Blueprint Storage
    await write_code_blueprints(generated, notion_token=os.getenv("NOTION_INTERNAL_TOKEN"))
    
    # Step 5: Diff Check L2 — Cycle→Cycle
    cycle_diff = pipeline.run_diff_check(layer="cycle-to-cycle")
    if cycle_diff.get("unexpected_changes"):
        pipeline.warn(f"Changes outside allowed dirs: {cycle_diff['unexpected_changes']}")
    
    # Step 6: Test Suite
    test_result = pipeline.run_tests(coverage_threshold=80)
    if not test_result["passed"]:
        return pipeline.fail(f"Tests failed: {test_result['failures']} failures, {test_result['coverage']}% coverage")
    
    # Step 7: Quality Gates
    lint_ok = pipeline.run_lint()
    caps_ok = pipeline.run_caps_score(threshold=70)
    guardrails_ok = pipeline.run_guardrails(max_critical=0)
    if not all([lint_ok, caps_ok, guardrails_ok]):
        return pipeline.fail("Quality gates failed")
    
    # Step 8: Governance Audit
    audit = pipeline.run_guild_audit(phase=phase)
    if audit.get("blocking_failures"):
        return pipeline.fail(f"Governance audit NO-GO: {audit['blocking_reasons']}")
    
    # Step 9: Diff Check L3 — Blueprint→Blueprint
    bp_diff = pipeline.run_diff_check(layer="blueprint-to-blueprint")
    
    # Step 10: Cycle Report
    report = pipeline.generate_cycle_report(
        spec_diff=spec_diff, cycle_diff=cycle_diff, bp_diff=bp_diff,
        test_result=test_result, audit=audit, generated=generated
    )
    await pipeline.post_cycle_report_to_notion(report)
    
    # Step 11: DD/PH Build Metrics
    await pipeline.submit_build_metrics(report)
    await pipeline.publish_nats_event("citadel.vcc.cycle.completed", report.to_event())
    
    # Step 12: Rollback Checkpoint
    pipeline.save_rollback_checkpoint()
    
    return {
        "success": True,
        "phase": phase,
        "generated_files": len(generated),
        "test_coverage": test_result["coverage"],
        "caps_composite": caps_ok.get("composite", 0),
        "guardrail_violations": 0,
        "cycle_report_id": report.cycle_id,
        "go_no_go": "GO"
    }
```

## 16.7 Environment Variables for Auto-Build

| **Variable** | **Used By** | **Required** | **Notes** |
| `CRP_CONFIG_PATH` | Build pipeline Step 1 | Optional | Default: `config/crp_config.yaml` |
| `VCC_BUILD_STAGING_DIR` | Build pipeline Step 3 | Optional | Default: `build/staging/` |
| `VCC_COVERAGE_THRESHOLD` | Build pipeline Step 6 | Optional | Default: `80` (percent) |
| `VCC_CAPS_THRESHOLD` | Build pipeline Step 7 | Optional | Default: `70` (composite score) |
| `VCC_MAX_GUARDRAIL_VIOLATIONS` | Build pipeline Step 7 | Optional | Default: `0` (zero tolerance for critical) |
| `VCC_ROLLBACK_ENABLED` | Build pipeline Step 12 | Optional | Default: `true` |

## 16.8 Guardrails for Auto-Build


### Must-Dos ✅

- ✅ **Every auto-generated file MUST pass syntax check** before moving from `build/staging/` to `src/`
- ✅ **Every build cycle MUST produce a CRP cycle report** — even on failure
- ✅ **Every build cycle MUST save a rollback SHA** before committing
- ✅ **Rule Zero codebase scan MUST run** before any code generation
- ✅ **3-layer diff check MUST run** — no silent drift allowed
- ✅ **Test coverage MUST be ≥ 80%** — no exceptions
- ✅ **CAPS score MUST be ≥ B (70)** for all 5 SMP services
- ✅ **0 critical guardrail violations** — period
- ✅ **All financial writes MUST have **`**x-idempotency-key**` enforcement
- ✅ **All write operations MUST publish NATS events** — no silent writes

### Must-Not-Dos 🚫

- 🚫 **NEVER commit generated code directly to **`**src/**` — always stage in `build/staging/` first
- 🚫 **NEVER skip the test suite** — even for "small" changes
- 🚫 **NEVER skip the diff check** — drift is the #1 cause of production incidents
- 🚫 **NEVER deploy without a passing governance audit** — Phase 5 audit is mandatory
- 🚫 **NEVER auto-deploy to production** — G9 is always a manual approval gate
- 🚫 **NEVER overwrite existing files** without first checking `git log` for recent changes
- 🚫 **NEVER generate code without the SRS registry loaded** — untracked code is ungoverned code
- 🚫 **NEVER suppress test failures** — fix the code, not the tests
- 🚫 **NEVER commit without a cycle report** — every commit must be auditable
- 🚫 **NEVER bypass the rollback checkpoint** — if you can't roll back, you can't deploy
