# 17. Software Module Profile (SMP) Protocols

> **Source of truth:** College System Blueprint (CAPS/Nemesis/USO), VS Code Extension SMP Pipeline, AIMB Enhancer Pipeline.
> **SMP = Software Module Profile** — the identity card, scoring envelope, and governance binding for every deployable module in the Citadel stack.

## 17.1 What SMP Is

Every micro-service, worker, and executable in Finance Guild is a **Software Module Profile (SMP)** entity. An SMP is a `.sake.yaml` manifest that declares:
- **Identity** — `module_id`, human name, SRS code, ICP component ID
- **Lineage** — `lid` (Lineage ID) tracing build ancestry via F977
- **CAPS Scores** — Complexity, Archetype Alignment, Performance, Sovereignty (0-100 each)
- **Fingerprint** — SHA-256 of source at build time
- **Capabilities** — what the module can do (enum list)
- **Dependencies** — other SMP modules it requires
- **Status** — `scaffold | poc | active | stable | deprecated`
The SMP pipeline (F941 → F977 → F992 → F999) builds, traces, validates, and tests each profile before it can be promoted.

## 17.2 Finance Guild SMP Registry

The five Finance Guild micro-services and their SMP archetype mappings:
| **Module ID** | **Service** | **Port** | **SRS Code** | **CAPS Archetype** | **ICP Component ID** |
| `smp-fin-api` | Finance API Gateway | :8093 | FG-API-001 | Service_Gateway | `icp.fg.api` |
| `smp-fin-ws` | Finance WebSocket | :8094 | FG-WS-001 | Realtime_Relay | `icp.fg.ws` |
| `smp-fin-worker` | Finance Background Worker | — | FG-WRK-001 | Async_Processor | `icp.fg.worker` |
| `smp-fin-pdf` | PDF Generation Service | :8095 | FG-PDF-001 | Content_Generator | `icp.fg.pdf` |
| `smp-fin-ai` | Finance AI Service | :8096 | FG-AI-001 | Intelligence_Agent | `icp.fg.ai` |

## 17.3 CAPS Scoring — Axis Weights per Archetype

CAPS uses four axes weighted per archetype. Default weights sum to 1.0:
```yaml
# CAPS axis weights per Finance Guild archetype
caps_archetype_weights:
  Service_Gateway:       # smp-fin-api
    w_C: 0.25            # Complexity — moderate (route fan-out, middleware chain)
    w_A: 0.25            # Archetype Alignment — high (must match API contract exactly)
    w_P: 0.30            # Performance — critical (latency, throughput, error rate)
    w_S: 0.20            # Sovereignty — standard (self-healing, audit compliance)

  Realtime_Relay:        # smp-fin-ws
    w_C: 0.20
    w_A: 0.20
    w_P: 0.35            # Performance dominant — sub-100ms delivery required
    w_S: 0.25            # Sovereignty higher — must self-heal dropped connections

  Async_Processor:       # smp-fin-worker
    w_C: 0.30            # Complexity higher — NATS consumer, retry logic, dead-letter
    w_A: 0.20
    w_P: 0.25
    w_S: 0.25            # Sovereignty higher — must survive crashes, resume from checkpoint

  Content_Generator:     # smp-fin-pdf
    w_C: 0.35            # Complexity dominant — template rendering, layout engine
    w_A: 0.20
    w_P: 0.25
    w_S: 0.20

  Intelligence_Agent:    # smp-fin-ai
    w_C: 0.30
    w_A: 0.25            # Archetype Alignment higher — must match AI guardrails
    w_P: 0.25
    w_S: 0.20
```
**Grade thresholds** (from College System):
| Grade | Score Range | Meaning |
| S | 90-100 | Sovereign (elite) |
| A | 80-89 | Excellent |
| B | 70-79 | Good |
| C | 55-69 | Adequate |
| D | 40-54 | Marginal |
| F | 0-39 | Failing |
| X | — | Quarantine (suspended) |
**Minimum CAPS for Finance Guild promotion to production: B (70)**. Services scoring below 70 MUST NOT be deployed.

## 17.4 SMP `.sake.yaml` Template

VCC MUST generate a `.sake.yaml` profile for each Finance Guild service during build:
```yaml
# Template: smp-fin-api.sake.yaml
module_id: smp-fin-api
name: Finance API Gateway
srs_code: FG-API-001
icp_component_id: icp.fg.api
caps_archetype: Service_Gateway
layer: service
ecosystem: finance-guild
version: "0.1.0"
status: scaffold
fingerprint: ""  # SHA-256, computed by F941 at build time

capabilities:
  - INVOICE_CRUD
  - QUOTE_CRUD
  - CONTRACT_CRUD
  - PAYMENT_PROCESSING
  - STRIPE_CONNECT
  - XERO_SYNC
  - MERCURY_BANKING
  - CURSOR_PAGINATION
  - IDEMPOTENCY
  - RATE_LIMITING
  - AUDIT_LOGGING

dependencies:
  - supabase-auth
  - nats-jetstream
  - upstash-redis
  - stripe-connect
  - smp-fin-worker
  - smp-fin-pdf

icp_policy:
  allowed_enums:
    - INVOICE_CREATED
    - INVOICE_SENT
    - INVOICE_PAID
    - QUOTE_ACCEPTED
    - CONTRACT_SIGNED
    - PAYMENT_RECEIVED
    - WEBHOOK_PROCESSED
  forbidden_enums:
    - MODIFY_OWN_CAPS_POLICY
    - BYPASS_RLS
    - DISABLE_AUDIT
  max_severity: HIGH
  allowed_environments:
    - development
    - staging
    - production

caps_scores:  # Updated by F992 Validate + AIMB pipeline
  C: 0
  A: 0
  P: 0
  S: 0
  composite: 0
  grade: "F"
  last_scored: null

lineage:
  lid: ""          # Computed by F977
  parent: null
  build_chain: []
```

## 17.5 AIMB Enhancer Pipeline Integration

The **AI Module Blueprint (AIMB) Enhancer Pipeline** runs CAPS evaluation on each SMP. VCC MUST wire Finance Guild services into this pipeline:
```python
# aimb_finance_evaluator.py
# Integrates Finance Guild SMPs with the AIMB pipeline

from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Dict, Optional
from datetime import datetime, timezone
import hashlib
import json

@dataclass
class CAPSAxes:
    C: float = 0.0  # Complexity
    A: float = 0.0  # Archetype Alignment
    P: float = 0.0  # Performance
    S: float = 0.0  # Sovereignty

@dataclass
class SmpProfile:
    module_id: str
    srs_code: str
    icp_component_id: str
    caps_archetype: str
    version: str
    status: str
    fingerprint: str
    caps: CAPSAxes
    grade: str = "F"
    composite: float = 0.0

CAPS_WEIGHTS: Dict[str, Dict[str, float]] = {
    "Service_Gateway":    {"w_C": 0.25, "w_A": 0.25, "w_P": 0.30, "w_S": 0.20},
    "Realtime_Relay":     {"w_C": 0.20, "w_A": 0.20, "w_P": 0.35, "w_S": 0.25},
    "Async_Processor":    {"w_C": 0.30, "w_A": 0.20, "w_P": 0.25, "w_S": 0.25},
    "Content_Generator":  {"w_C": 0.35, "w_A": 0.20, "w_P": 0.25, "w_S": 0.20},
    "Intelligence_Agent": {"w_C": 0.30, "w_A": 0.25, "w_P": 0.25, "w_S": 0.20},
}

GRADE_MAP = [
    (90, "S"), (80, "A"), (70, "B"),
    (55, "C"), (40, "D"), (0, "F"),
]

def score_to_grade(score: float) -> str:
    for threshold, grade in GRADE_MAP:
        if score >= threshold:
            return grade
    return "F"

def compute_caps_composite(axes: CAPSAxes, archetype: str) -> float:
    w = CAPS_WEIGHTS.get(archetype, CAPS_WEIGHTS["Service_Gateway"])
    return (
        w["w_C"] * axes.C +
        w["w_A"] * axes.A +
        w["w_P"] * axes.P +
        w["w_S"] * axes.S
    )

def evaluate_complexity(module_id: str, source_stats: dict) -> float:
    """Score C axis: cyclomatic complexity, function density, async/IO mix."""
    cc = source_stats.get("avg_cyclomatic_complexity", 10)
    fn_density = source_stats.get("functions_per_file", 5)
    async_ratio = source_stats.get("async_ratio", 0.5)
    # Lower complexity = higher score (inverse relationship)
    cc_score = max(0, 100 - (cc - 1) * 8)          # cc=1 → 100, cc=13 → 4
    fn_score = min(100, fn_density * 10)             # 10 fn/file → 100
    async_score = async_ratio * 100                  # 1.0 → 100
    return round((cc_score * 0.5) + (fn_score * 0.25) + (async_score * 0.25), 1)

def evaluate_archetype_alignment(module_id: str, profile: dict) -> float:
    """Score A axis: mission compliance, ENUM adherence, contract match."""
    checks = [
        profile.get("has_rls_enforcement", False),
        profile.get("has_tenant_middleware", False),
        profile.get("has_idempotency", False),
        profile.get("has_audit_logging", False),
        profile.get("has_error_catalog", False),
        profile.get("has_pydantic_schemas", False),
        profile.get("has_cursor_pagination", False),
        profile.get("has_nats_events", False),
        profile.get("matches_spec_routes", False),
        profile.get("has_test_coverage", False),
    ]
    return round((sum(checks) / len(checks)) * 100, 1)

def evaluate_performance(module_id: str, metrics: dict) -> float:
    """Score P axis: success rate, latency, resource usage."""
    success_rate = metrics.get("success_rate", 0.95)       # 0-1
    p95_latency_ms = metrics.get("p95_latency_ms", 200)    # target < 500ms
    memory_mb = metrics.get("memory_mb", 256)               # target < 512
    sr_score = success_rate * 100
    lat_score = max(0, 100 - (p95_latency_ms / 5))         # 500ms → 0
    mem_score = max(0, 100 - (memory_mb / 5.12))           # 512MB → 0
    return round((sr_score * 0.5) + (lat_score * 0.3) + (mem_score * 0.2), 1)

def evaluate_sovereignty(module_id: str, ops: dict) -> float:
    """Score S axis: self-healing, audit pass rate, maintainability."""
    has_health_check = ops.get("has_health_endpoint", False)
    has_graceful_shutdown = ops.get("has_graceful_shutdown", False)
    has_retry_logic = ops.get("has_retry_logic", False)
    has_dead_letter = ops.get("has_dead_letter_queue", False)
    has_circuit_breaker = ops.get("has_circuit_breaker", False)
    audit_pass_rate = ops.get("audit_pass_rate", 0.8)       # 0-1
    feature_flags = [
        has_health_check, has_graceful_shutdown,
        has_retry_logic, has_dead_letter, has_circuit_breaker,
    ]
    feature_score = (sum(feature_flags) / len(feature_flags)) * 100
    audit_score = audit_pass_rate * 100
    return round((feature_score * 0.6) + (audit_score * 0.4), 1)

def run_aimb_evaluation(profile: SmpProfile, source_stats: dict,
                        alignment: dict, metrics: dict, ops: dict) -> SmpProfile:
    """Full AIMB pipeline: evaluate all four CAPS axes and compute composite."""
    profile.caps.C = evaluate_complexity(profile.module_id, source_stats)
    profile.caps.A = evaluate_archetype_alignment(profile.module_id, alignment)
    profile.caps.P = evaluate_performance(profile.module_id, metrics)
    profile.caps.S = evaluate_sovereignty(profile.module_id, ops)
    profile.composite = compute_caps_composite(profile.caps, profile.caps_archetype)
    profile.grade = score_to_grade(profile.composite)
    return profile
```

## 17.6 ICP (Identity / Component / Policy) Contracts

Every Finance Guild SMP MUST declare its ICP binding per the College System safety framework:
```yaml
# ICP contract for smp-fin-api
icp_contract:
  component_id: icp.fg.api
  human_owner: mr.nobody
  srs_code: FG-API-001
  caps_archetype: Service_Gateway

  policy_profile:
    allowed_enums:
      - INVOICE_CREATED
      - INVOICE_UPDATED
      - INVOICE_SENT
      - INVOICE_VOIDED
      - INVOICE_PAID
      - QUOTE_CREATED
      - QUOTE_SENT
      - QUOTE_ACCEPTED
      - QUOTE_REJECTED
      - CONTRACT_CREATED
      - CONTRACT_SIGNED
      - PAYMENT_INTENT_CREATED
      - PAYMENT_RECEIVED
      - WEBHOOK_STRIPE_PROCESSED
      - WEBHOOK_XERO_PROCESSED
      - XERO_SYNC_COMPLETED
      - MERCURY_BALANCE_FETCHED
    forbidden_enums:
      - MODIFY_OWN_CAPS_POLICY
      - BYPASS_NEMESIS
      - DISABLE_RLS
      - DISABLE_AUDIT_TRAIL
      - MODIFY_REFLEX_GRAPH
      - UPDATE_MIRAS_WEIGHTS
    max_severity: HIGH
    allowed_environments:
      - development
      - staging
      - production

  invariants:
    - "MUST NOT write outside finance schema (fg_*) tables"
    - "MUST NOT bypass RLS on any query"
    - "MUST NOT skip Nemesis on CAPS violations"
    - "MUST NOT modify own ICP policy profile"
    - "MUST NOT process Stripe webhooks without signature verification"
    - "MUST NOT expose tenant data across tenant boundaries"
    - "MUST log all write operations to finance_audit_log"
```

## 17.7 VCC Build Rules for SMP

**VCC MUST:**
- ✅ Generate a `.sake.yaml` profile for each of the 5 Finance Guild services during initial scaffold
- ✅ Set `status: scaffold` on initial creation, advance to `poc` → `active` → `stable` as tests pass
- ✅ Run `F992_reflex_validator.py` on every generated profile before committing
- ✅ Compute fingerprint (SHA-256 of all source files in the service) on every build
- ✅ Include ICP invariants in every service's health check endpoint
- ✅ Declare all NATS event subjects as `allowed_enums` in the ICP policy
- ✅ Map archetype weights to the service's role (see §17.3 table)
- ✅ Target CAPS grade **B (70+)** minimum before any service is flagged as `active`
- ✅ Sync SMP profiles to Notion via `smp_notion_sync.py` after every successful pipeline run
**VCC MUST NOT:**
- 🚫 Deploy any service with CAPS grade below B (70) to production
- 🚫 Skip the AIMB evaluation pipeline on any build
- 🚫 Hardcode CAPS scores — they MUST be computed by the pipeline
- 🚫 Allow any service to declare `MODIFY_OWN_CAPS_POLICY` in allowed_enums
- 🚫 Omit ICP invariants from the `.sake.yaml` manifest
- 🚫 Bypass F992 validation for "speed" — validation is non-optional

## 17.8 SMP Lifecycle — Finance Guild

```mermaid
flowchart LR
    SCAFFOLD["scaffold\n(VCC generates code)"] --> BUILD["F941 Build\n(compute fingerprint)"]
    BUILD --> LINEAGE["F977 Lineage\n(trace ancestry)"]
    LINEAGE --> VALIDATE["F992 Validate\n(check ICP + policy)"]
    VALIDATE --> TEST["F999 Test\n(run test suite)"]
    TEST --> AIMB["AIMB Pipeline\n(CAPS scoring)"]
    AIMB --> CHECK{"Grade >= B?"}
    CHECK -->|Yes| PROMOTE["status: active\nSync to Notion"]
    CHECK -->|No| FIX["Fix violations\nRe-enter pipeline"]
    FIX --> BUILD
    PROMOTE --> STABLE["Passes 14-day window\nstatus: stable"]
    STABLE --> PROD["Deploy to production"]
```

---


# 11. Cycle Report Protocol (CRP)

**This is mandatory.** Every VCC build cycle MUST end with a structured Cycle Report posted to the VCC Build Instructions page (this page) via the Notion API. Raw git commit dumps are **prohibited** — they are noisy, unstructured, and break the feedback loop. The VCC MUST use the `vcc_cycle_reporter.py` module defined below.

## 11.1 Protocol Rules

- ✅ **One report per build cycle** — a "cycle" is a continuous VCC session that produces one or more commits
- ✅ **Report MUST be posted as a single toggle heading block** — not raw text, not multiple blocks
- ✅ **Report MUST be posted AFTER all commits are pushed** — never mid-cycle
- ✅ **Report MUST cross-reference SRS codes** from Section 19 of the parent spec
- ✅ **Report MUST include a guardrails compliance scan** — automated grep for violations
- ✅ **Report MUST include a drift report** — delta between spec and actual codebase
- ✅ **Report MUST include next cycle intent** — so the operator can redirect before the next build
- 🚫 **NEVER dump raw **`**git log**`** output** — always parse into structured format
- 🚫 **NEVER post more than one report per cycle** — consolidate, don't spam
- 🚫 **NEVER skip the guardrails scan** — even if "nothing changed" (prove it)
- 🚫 **NEVER leave **`**VCC-QUESTION**`** or **`**VCC-CONFLICT**`** flags buried in code** — surface them in Section 4 of the report

## 11.2 Report Schema

Every Cycle Report MUST contain these 7 sections in this exact order:
| **Section** | **Name** | **Contents** | **Required** |
| §1 | Cycle Header | Cycle ID, timestamps, author chain (which Claude models), git commit range, total files/lines | ✅ Always |
| §2 | What Was Built | SRS codes touched + new status (🔵→🟢), files created/modified with line counts, tables migrated, RLS policies added, components scaffolded — grouped by build phase (P0/P1/P2/P3) | ✅ Always |
| §3 | Guardrails Compliance | Automated scan results: ✅ pass / 🚫 violation per guardrail category (RLS, multi-tenancy, money types, auth, hardcoded colors, `SELECT *`, `Any` types, etc.). Each violation includes file:line reference. | ✅ Always |
| §4 | Flags & Questions | All `VCC-QUESTION` and `VCC-CONFLICT` flags found in code, with file:line and context. If none: "No flags raised." | ✅ Always |
| §5 | Drift Report | Delta between Notion blueprint and codebase: spec'd-but-not-built (missing), built-but-not-spec'd (orphaned), stale code that no longer maps to an SRS code | ✅ Always |
| §6 | Next Cycle Intent | What VCC plans to build next: SRS codes, target phase, estimated files. Blockers or dependencies it needs resolved. Questions for the operator (consolidated). | ✅ Always |
| §7 | Health Metrics | Notion sync status, NATS events, migrations applied/pending, build time, bundle size delta, test pass/fail counts. **PostHog:** event capture count, feature flag status, session recording count, distinct user count. **Datadog:** APM p50/p95 latency per service, error rate, active monitor/alert count, cache hit rate, RLS violation count. **Service Health Checks:** per-service `/health` endpoint status (liveness + readiness), response time ms, dependency status (Supabase, NATS, Redis, Stripe, SES), last-checked timestamp, consecutive failure count. Health probe failures with `consecutive_failures >= 3` are **blocking** — cycle report is flagged NO-GO until all services report healthy. | ✅ Always |
| §8 | Diff Check | Three-layer diff: **Spec→Code** (Notion blueprint vs codebase — missing/orphaned/stale per SRS code), **Cycle→Cycle** (unified diff of all files changed this cycle vs previous cycle's end state), **Blueprint→Blueprint** (Notion page version diff — detect mid-build spec changes). Each layer outputs pass/fail + itemized delta. Cycle report is **REJECTED** if diff check is missing. **Diff check is a blocking gate** — any dirty layer with unacknowledged drift causes the cycle to be flagged NO-GO. Acknowledged drifts must be annotated with `# DRIFT-ACK: <reason>` in code or logged in the CRP config `acknowledged_drifts` list. | ✅ Always |

## 11.3 Cycle ID Format

```javascript
VCC-{GUILD}-{YYYYMMDD}-{HHMM}
```
Examples:
- `VCC-FIN-20260227-1930` — Finance Guild cycle on Feb 27 at 19:30 UTC
- `VCC-FIN-20260228-0845` — Finance Guild cycle on Feb 28 at 08:45 UTC

## 11.4 Implementation — `vcc_cycle_reporter.py`

The VCC MUST use this module to generate and post cycle reports. Place in `tools/vcc_cycle_reporter.py`.
```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""VCC Cycle Reporter — Structured build cycle reports to Notion.

Protocol: CRP v1.0 (Cycle Report Protocol)
Target:   Finance Guild — VCC Build Instructions & Guardrails
Usage:    python tools/vcc_cycle_reporter.py --from <commit> --to <commit>
"""

import os
import re
import json
import subprocess
import hashlib
from datetime import datetime, timezone
from dataclasses import dataclass, field, asdict
from typing import Optional
from pathlib import Path

import requests

# ── Configuration ────────────────────────────────────────────────
NOTION_API = "https://api.notion.com/v1"
NOTION_VERSION = "2022-06-28"
NOTION_TOKEN = os.environ["NOTION_INTERNAL_TOKEN"]

# Target page: Finance Guild — VCC Build Instructions & Guardrails
VCC_INSTRUCTIONS_PAGE_ID = os.environ.get(
    "VCC_INSTRUCTIONS_PAGE_ID",
    ""  # Set in .env — the page ID of this document
)

GUILD = "FIN"  # Change per guild
REPO_ROOT = Path(os.environ.get("REPO_ROOT", "."))

# ── SRS Code Registry (from Section 19 of parent spec) ──────────
# VCC should auto-parse these from the spec, but as fallback:
SRS_CODES = {
    "SRS-FIN-001": "Stripe Connect Onboarding",
    "SRS-FIN-002": "Customer CRUD",
    "SRS-FIN-003": "Service Catalog CRUD",
    "SRS-FIN-004": "Invoice CRUD",

# ── Data Models ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
@dataclass
class CommitInfo:
    sha: str
    message: str
    author: str
    timestamp: str
    files_changed: int = 0
    insertions: int = 0
    deletions: int = 0
    co_author: Optional[str] = None


@dataclass
class GuardrailViolation:
    rule: str           # e.g. "NO_FLOAT_MONEY"
    file: str           # e.g. "src/api/finance/router_invoices.py"
    line: int
    snippet: str        # the offending line
    severity: str       # "critical" | "warning"


@dataclass
class DriftItem:
    srs_code: str
    name: str
    status: str         # "missing" | "orphaned" | "stale" | "partial"
    detail: str


@dataclass
class CycleReport:
    cycle_id: str
    guild: str
    started_at: str
    ended_at: str
    author_chain: list[str]
    commit_range: str
    total_commits: int
    total_files_changed: int
    total_insertions: int
    total_deletions: int
    # §2 What Was Built
    srs_codes_touched: dict[str, str]   # SRS code → new status
    files_created: list[str]
    files_modified: list[str]
    tables_migrated: list[str]
    rls_policies_added: list[str]
    components_scaffolded: list[str]
    # §3 Guardrails
    guardrail_violations: list[GuardrailViolation] = field(default_factory=list)
    guardrail_pass: bool = True
    # §4 Flags
    vcc_questions: list[dict] = field(default_factory=list)
    vcc_conflicts: list[dict] = field(default_factory=list)
    # §5 Drift
    drift_items: list[DriftItem] = field(default_factory=list)
    # §6 Next Cycle
    next_srs_codes: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)
    next_phase: str = ""
    blockers: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)
    operator_questions: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)
    # §7 Health
    notion_sync_status: str = "ok"
    nats_events_published: int = 0
    migrations_applied: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)
    migrations_pending: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)
    test_passed: int = 0
    test_failed: int = 0
    build_time_seconds: float = 0.0
    bundle_size_kb: float = 0.0


# ── Git Parsing ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
def parse_commits(from_sha: str, to_sha: str) -> list[CommitInfo]:
    """Parse git log between two commits."""
    fmt = "--format=COMMIT_START%n%H%n%an%n%aI%n%s%n%b%nCOMMIT_END"
    result = subprocess.run(
        ["git", "log", f"{from_sha}..{to_sha}", fmt, "--stat"],
        capture_output=True, encoding="utf-8", errors="replace",
        cwd=REPO_ROOT,
    )
    commits = []
    raw_blocks = result.stdout.split("COMMIT_START")
    for block in raw_blocks:
        if "COMMIT_END" not in block:
            continue
        lines = block.strip().split("\n")
        if len(lines) < 4:
            continue
        sha = lines[0].strip()
        author = lines[1].strip()
        ts = lines[2].strip()
        subject = lines[3].strip()
        body = "\n".join(lines[4:])

        # Extract co-author
        co = None
        co_match = re.search(r"Co-Authored-By:\s*(.+)", body)
        if co_match:
            co = co_match.group(1).strip()

        # Extract stat line
        stat_match = re.search(
            r"(\d+) files? changed(?:, (\d+) insertions?\(\+\))?(?:, (\d+) deletions?\(-\))?",
            body
        )
        fc = int(stat_match.group(1)) if stat_match else 0
        ins = int(stat_match.group(2) or 0) if stat_match else 0
        dels = int(stat_match.group(3) or 0) if stat_match else 0

        commits.append(CommitInfo(
            sha=sha[:7], message=subject, author=author,
            timestamp=ts, files_changed=fc, insertions=ins,
            deletions=dels, co_author=co,
        ))
    return commits


def extract_author_chain(commits: list[CommitInfo]) -> list[str]:
    """Extract unique LLM co-authors from commit chain."""
    authors = []
    seen = set()
    for c in commits:
        if c.co_author and c.co_author not in seen:
            seen.add(c.co_author)
            # Clean to just model name
            model = re.sub(r"<.*>", "", c.co_author).strip()
            authors.append(model)
    return authors or ["Unknown"]


# ── Guardrails Scanner ───────────────────────────────────────────
GUARDRAIL_RULES = [
    {
        "id": "NO_FLOAT_MONEY",
        "pattern": r"\b(FLOAT|DOUBLE PRECISION|REAL)\b",
        "file_glob": "*.sql",
        "severity": "critical",
        "description": "Monetary columns must use NUMERIC(12,2), never FLOAT/DOUBLE/REAL",
    },
    {
        "id": "NO_SELECT_STAR",
        "pattern": r"SELECT\s+\*\s+FROM",
        "file_glob": "*.py",
        "severity": "critical",
        "description": "Never use SELECT * in production queries",
        "exclude_patterns": [r"test_", r"seed_", r"migration"],
    },
    {
        "id": "NO_ANY_TYPE",
        "pattern": r":\s*Any\b|\bAny\]",
        "file_glob": "*.py",
        "severity": "warning",
        "description": "Pydantic models must not use Any type",
        "exclude_patterns": [r"test_"],
    },
    {
        "id": "NO_HARDCODED_HEX",
        "pattern": r"[\"']#[0-9a-fA-F]{6}[\"']",
        "file_glob": "*.tsx",
        "severity": "warning",
        "description": "Use dr.* tokens, never hardcode hex colors",
        "exclude_patterns": [r"StatusBadge", r"statusColors"],
    },
    {
        "id": "NO_TOFIXED_MONEY",
        "pattern": r"\.toFixed\(2\)",
        "file_glob": "*.tsx",
        "severity": "critical",
        "description": "Use Intl.NumberFormat, never toFixed(2) for money",
    },
    {
        "id": "NO_LOCALSTORAGE_SENSITIVE",
        "pattern": r"localStorage\.setItem\([\"'](token|jwt|secret|key|password)",
        "file_glob": "*.tsx",
        "severity": "critical",
        "description": "Never store sensitive data in localStorage",
    },
    {
        "id": "NO_DANGEROUS_HTML",
        "pattern": r"dangerouslySetInnerHTML",
        "file_glob": "*.tsx",
        "severity": "critical",
        "description": "Never use dangerouslySetInnerHTML",
    },
    {
        "id": "RLS_ENABLED",
        "pattern": r"CREATE TABLE(?!.*ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY)",
        "file_glob": "*.sql",
        "severity": "critical",
        "description": "Every CREATE TABLE must have RLS enabled in same migration",
    },
    {
        "id": "NO_SERVICE_ROLE_CLIENT",
        "pattern": r"service_role|SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE",
        "file_glob": "*.tsx",
        "severity": "critical",
        "description": "Never use service_role key in client-side code",
    },
    {
        "id": "NO_OFFSET_PAGINATION",
        "pattern": r"OFFSET\s+\d+|offset=|page_number",
        "file_glob": "*.py",
        "severity": "warning",
        "description": "Use cursor-based pagination, never offset-based",
        "exclude_patterns": [r"test_", r"seed_"],
    },
    {
        "id": "TENANT_ID_REQUIRED",
        "pattern": r"CREATE TABLE\s+finance_\w+\s*\([^)]*\)\s*;",
        "file_glob": "*.sql",
        "severity": "critical",
        "description": "All finance_ tables must include tenant_id column",
    },
    {
        "id": "NO_BARE_TIMESTAMP",
        "pattern": r"\bTIMESTAMP\b(?!TZ| WITH TIME ZONE)",
        "file_glob": "*.sql",
        "severity": "warning",
        "description": "Use TIMESTAMPTZ, never bare TIMESTAMP",
    },
    {
        "id": "STRIPE_ACCOUNT_HEADER",
        "pattern": r"stripe\.(Invoice|PaymentIntent|Charge|Customer)\.create\(",
        "file_glob": "*.py",
        "severity": "critical",
        "description": "Every Stripe API call must include stripe_account header",
    },
    {
        "id": "NO_ALERT_CONFIRM",
        "pattern": r"\b(alert|confirm|prompt)\s*\(",
        "file_glob": "*.tsx",
        "severity": "warning",
        "description": "Use Citadel modal system, never alert()/confirm()/prompt()",
        "exclude_patterns": [r"console\."],
    },
    {
        "id": "NO_UUID_V4",
        "pattern": r"uuid_generate_v4\(\)",
        "file_glob": "*.sql",
        "severity": "warning",
        "description": "Use gen_random_uuid(), never uuid_generate_v4()",
    },
]


def scan_guardrails(changed_files: list[str]) -> list[GuardrailViolation]:
    """Scan changed files against guardrail rules."""
    violations = []
    for fpath in changed_files:
        full_path = REPO_ROOT / fpath
        if not full_path.exists():
            continue
        try:
            content = full_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")
        except Exception:
            continue

        for rule in GUARDRAIL_RULES:
            # Check file glob match
            if not fpath.endswith(rule["file_glob"].replace("*", "")):
                continue
            # Check exclude patterns
            excludes = rule.get("exclude_patterns", [])
            if any(re.search(ex, fpath) for ex in excludes):
                continue
            # Scan each line
            for i, line in enumerate(content.split("\n"), 1):
                if line.strip().startswith("#") or line.strip().startswith("//"):
                    continue  # Skip comments
                if re.search(rule["pattern"], line, re.IGNORECASE):
                    violations.append(GuardrailViolation(
                        rule=rule["id"],
                        file=fpath,
                        line=i,
                        snippet=line.strip()[:120],
                        severity=rule["severity"],
                    ))
    return violations


# ── Flag Scanner ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
def scan_flags(changed_files: list[str]) -> tuple[list[dict], list[dict]]:
    """Scan for VCC-QUESTION and VCC-CONFLICT flags in code."""
    questions, conflicts = [], []
    for fpath in changed_files:
        full_path = REPO_ROOT / fpath
        if not full_path.exists():
            continue
        try:
            content = full_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")
        except Exception:
            continue
        for i, line in enumerate(content.split("\n"), 1):
            if "VCC-QUESTION" in line:
                questions.append({
                    "file": fpath, "line": i,
                    "text": line.strip()[:200]
                })
            if "VCC-CONFLICT" in line:
                conflicts.append({
                    "file": fpath, "line": i,
                    "text": line.strip()[:200]
                })
    return questions, conflicts


# ── Drift Scanner ────────────────────────────────────────────────
def scan_drift() -> list[DriftItem]:
    """Compare SRS codes against actual codebase to find gaps."""
    drift = []
    src_api = REPO_ROOT / "src" / "api" / "finance"
    src_components = REPO_ROOT / "src" / "components" / "finance"
    migrations_dir = REPO_ROOT / "supabase" / "migrations"

    # Check for expected route files per SRS code
    expected_routes = {
        "SRS-FIN-001": "router_integrations.py",
        "SRS-FIN-002": "router_customers.py",
        "SRS-FIN-003": "router_service_catalog.py",
        "SRS-FIN-004": "router_invoices.py",
        "SRS-FIN-005": "router_payments.py",
        "SRS-FIN-006": "router_dashboard.py",
        "SRS-FIN-009": "router_webhooks_stripe.py",
        "SRS-FIN-010": "router_quotes.py",
        "SRS-FIN-019": "router_recurring.py",
        "SRS-FIN-020": "router_credit_notes.py",
        "SRS-FIN-021": "router_commissions.py",
        "SRS-FIN-023": "router_contracts.py",
    }

    for srs_code, route_file in expected_routes.items():
        route_path = src_api / route_file
        if not route_path.exists():
            drift.append(DriftItem(
                srs_code=srs_code,
                name=SRS_CODES.get(srs_code, "Unknown"),
                status="missing",
                detail=f"Expected {route_file} not found in src/api/finance/"
            ))
        elif route_path.stat().st_size < 500:
            drift.append(DriftItem(
                srs_code=srs_code,
                name=SRS_CODES.get(srs_code, "Unknown"),
                status="partial",
                detail=f"{route_file} exists but appears to be a stub ({route_path.stat().st_size} bytes)"
            ))

    # Check for orphaned files (not mapped to any SRS code)
    if src_api.exists():
        known_files = set(expected_routes.values())
        known_files.update(["__init__.py", "middleware.py", "services"])
        for f in src_api.iterdir():
            if f.name.startswith("router_") and f.name not in known_files:
                drift.append(DriftItem(
                    srs_code="NONE",
                    name=f.name,
                    status="orphaned",
                    detail=f"{f.name} exists but is not mapped to any SRS code"
                ))

    return drift


# ── Migration Scanner ────────────────────────────────────────────
def scan_migrations() -> tuple[list[str], list[str]]:
    """Find applied and pending migrations."""
    migrations_dir = REPO_ROOT / "supabase" / "migrations"
    applied, pending = [], []
    if not migrations_dir.exists():
        return applied, pending
    for f in sorted(migrations_dir.glob("*.sql")):
        # Heuristic: if migration file mentions finance_, it's ours
        content = f.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")
        if "finance_" in content or "fg_" in content:
            # Check if it's been applied (look for marker comment or date)
            pending.append(f.name)  # Default to pending; VCC should check Supabase
    return applied, pending


# ── Report Builder ───────────────────────────────────────────────
def build_report(
    from_sha: str,
    to_sha: str,
    next_srs: list[str] | None = None,
    next_phase: str = "",
    blockers: list[str] | None = None,
    operator_questions: list[str] | None = None,
) -> CycleReport:
    """Build a complete cycle report from git range."""
    now = datetime.now(timezone.utc)
    cycle_id = f"VCC-{GUILD}-{now.strftime('%Y%m%d-%H%M')}"

    # Parse commits
    commits = parse_commits(from_sha, to_sha)
    if not commits:
        raise ValueError(f"No commits found in range {from_sha}..{to_sha}")

    author_chain = extract_author_chain(commits)

    # Aggregate stats
    total_files = sum(c.files_changed for c in commits)
    total_ins = sum(c.insertions for c in commits)
    total_dels = sum(c.deletions for c in commits)

    # Get changed files for scanning
    diff_result = subprocess.run(
        ["git", "diff", "--name-only", f"{from_sha}..{to_sha}"],
        capture_output=True, encoding="utf-8", errors="replace",
        cwd=REPO_ROOT,
    )
    changed_files = [f.strip() for f in diff_result.stdout.strip().split("\n") if f.strip()]

    # Categorize files
    created = [f for f in changed_files if not (REPO_ROOT / f).exists()]
    modified = [f for f in changed_files if (REPO_ROOT / f).exists()]

    # Detect tables and RLS from SQL files
    tables_migrated = []
    rls_added = []
    for f in changed_files:
        if f.endswith(".sql"):
            full = REPO_ROOT / f
            if full.exists():
                sql = full.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")
                tables_migrated.extend(re.findall(r"CREATE TABLE\s+(?:IF NOT EXISTS\s+)?(\w+)", sql))
                rls_added.extend(re.findall(r"CREATE POLICY\s+(\w+)", sql))

    # Detect React components
    components = [f for f in changed_files if f.endswith(".tsx") and "/finance/" in f]

    # Detect SRS codes touched (from commit messages)
    srs_touched = {}
    for c in commits:
        for code in re.findall(r"SRS-FIN-\d{3}", c.message):
            srs_touched[code] = "🟡 In Progress"

    # Run scans
    violations = scan_guardrails(changed_files)
    questions, conflicts = scan_flags(changed_files)
    drift = scan_drift()
    applied, pending = scan_migrations()

    return CycleReport(
        cycle_id=cycle_id,
        guild=GUILD,
        started_at=commits[-1].timestamp if commits else now.isoformat(),
        ended_at=commits[0].timestamp if commits else now.isoformat(),
        author_chain=author_chain,
        commit_range=f"{from_sha[:7]}..{to_sha[:7]}",
        total_commits=len(commits),
        total_files_changed=total_files,
        total_insertions=total_ins,
        total_deletions=total_dels,
        srs_codes_touched=srs_touched,
        files_created=[f for f in changed_files if f.endswith((".py", ".tsx", ".ts", ".sql"))],
        files_modified=modified,
        tables_migrated=tables_migrated,
        rls_policies_added=rls_added,
        components_scaffolded=components,
        guardrail_violations=violations,
        guardrail_pass=len([v for v in violations if v.severity == "critical"]) == 0,
        vcc_questions=questions,
        vcc_conflicts=conflicts,
        drift_items=drift,
        next_srs_codes=next_srs or [],
        next_phase=next_phase,
        blockers=blockers or [],
        operator_questions=operator_questions or [],
        notion_sync_status="ok",
        nats_events_published=0,  # VCC fills from runtime
        migrations_applied=applied,
        migrations_pending=pending,
        test_passed=0,   # VCC fills from pytest output
        test_failed=0,
    )


# ── Notion Renderer ──────────────────────────────────────────────
def render_to_notion_blocks(report: CycleReport) -> list[dict]:
    """Convert CycleReport to Notion API block children."""
    blocks = []

    def _h3(text: str) -> dict:
        return {"object": "block", "type": "heading_3", "heading_3": {
            "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": text}}],
        }}

    def _text(text: str, bold: bool = False) -> dict:
        return {"object": "block", "type": "paragraph", "paragraph": {
            "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": text[:2000]},
                           "annotations": {"bold": bold}}],
        }}

    def _bullet(text: str) -> dict:
        return {"object": "block", "type": "bulleted_list_item",
                "bulleted_list_item": {
            "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": text[:2000]}}],
        }}

    def _divider() -> dict:
        return {"object": "block", "type": "divider", "divider": {}}

    def _callout(text: str, icon: str = "📋", color: str = "blue_background") -> dict:
        return {"object": "block", "type": "callout", "callout": {
            "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": text[:2000]}}],
            "icon": {"type": "emoji", "emoji": icon},
            "color": color,
        }}

    # ── §1 Cycle Header ──
    guardrail_icon = "✅" if report.guardrail_pass else "🚫"
    header = (
        f"Cycle {report.cycle_id} | "
        f"{report.total_commits} commits | "
        f"+{report.total_insertions}/-{report.total_deletions} lines | "
        f"Guardrails: {guardrail_icon}"
    )

    # Main toggle heading
    toggle_block = {
        "object": "block",
        "type": "heading_2",
        "heading_2": {
            "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": f"📊 {header}"}}],
            "is_toggleable": True,
            "children": [],  # We'll build children separately
        },
    }

    children = []

    # §1 details
    children.append(_callout(
        f"Range: {report.commit_range}\n"
        f"Started: {report.started_at}\n"
        f"Ended: {report.ended_at}\n"
        f"Authors: {', '.join(report.author_chain)}\n"
        f"Files changed: {report.total_files_changed}",
        icon="🔧", color="gray_background"
    ))

    # §2 What Was Built
    children.append(_h3("§2 What Was Built"))
    if report.srs_codes_touched:
        for code, status in report.srs_codes_touched.items():
            name = SRS_CODES.get(code, "Unknown")
            children.append(_bullet(f"{code} — {name} → {status}"))
    else:
        children.append(_text("No SRS codes explicitly referenced in commits."))

    if report.tables_migrated:
        children.append(_text(f"Tables created/migrated: {', '.join(report.tables_migrated)}"))
    if report.rls_policies_added:
        children.append(_text(f"RLS policies added: {len(report.rls_policies_added)}"))
    if report.components_scaffolded:
        children.append(_text(f"Components: {', '.join(report.components_scaffolded[:10])}"))

    # §3 Guardrails Compliance
    children.append(_h3("§3 Guardrails Compliance"))
    if report.guardrail_pass:
        children.append(_callout("All guardrails passed — no critical violations.",
                                  icon="✅", color="green_background"))
    else:
        crit = [v for v in report.guardrail_violations if v.severity == "critical"]
        warn = [v for v in report.guardrail_violations if v.severity == "warning"]
        children.append(_callout(
            f"VIOLATIONS: {len(crit)} critical, {len(warn)} warnings",
            icon="🚫", color="red_background"
        ))
        for v in report.guardrail_violations[:20]:  # Cap at 20
            children.append(_bullet(
                f"[{v.severity.upper()}] {v.rule} — {v.file}:{v.line} — {v.snippet}"
            ))

    # §4 Flags & Questions
    children.append(_h3("§4 Flags & Questions"))
    if not report.vcc_questions and not report.vcc_conflicts:
        children.append(_text("No flags raised."))
    else:
        for q in report.vcc_questions:
            children.append(_bullet(f"❓ VCC-QUESTION: {q['file']}:{q['line']} — {q['text']}"))
        for c in report.vcc_conflicts:
            children.append(_bullet(f"⚠️ VCC-CONFLICT: {c['file']}:{c['line']} — {c['text']}"))

    # §5 Drift Report
    children.append(_h3("§5 Drift Report"))
    if not report.drift_items:
        children.append(_text("No drift detected — codebase matches spec."))
    else:
        for d in report.drift_items:
            emoji = {"missing": "🔴", "orphaned": "🟡", "stale": "⚪", "partial": "🟠"}[d.status]
            children.append(_bullet(f"{emoji} [{d.status.upper()}] {d.srs_code} {d.name} — {d.detail}"))

    # §6 Next Cycle Intent
    children.append(_h3("§6 Next Cycle Intent"))
    if report.next_srs_codes:
        children.append(_text(f"Target phase: {report.next_phase}"))
        for code in report.next_srs_codes:
            children.append(_bullet(f"{code} — {SRS_CODES.get(code, 'Unknown')}"))
    if report.blockers:
        children.append(_text("Blockers:", bold=True))
        for b in report.blockers:
            children.append(_bullet(f"🛑 {b}"))
    if report.operator_questions:
        children.append(_text("Questions for operator:", bold=True))
        for q in report.operator_questions:
            children.append(_bullet(f"❓ {q}"))

    # §7 Health Metrics
    children.append(_h3("§7 Health Metrics"))
    children.append(_callout(
        f"Notion sync: {report.notion_sync_status}\n"
        f"NATS events: {report.nats_events_published}\n"
        f"Migrations applied: {len(report.migrations_applied)} | "
        f"Pending: {len(report.migrations_pending)}\n"
        f"Tests: {report.test_passed} passed, {report.test_failed} failed\n"
        f"Build time: {report.build_time_seconds:.1f}s | "
        f"Bundle: {report.bundle_size_kb:.0f} KB",
        icon="📈", color="purple_background"
    ))

    # Assemble toggle
    toggle_block["heading_2"]["children"] = children
    blocks.append(_divider())
    blocks.append(toggle_block)

    return blocks


# ── Notion Poster ────────────────────────────────────────────────
def post_to_notion(report: CycleReport) -> str:
    """Post cycle report to the VCC Build Instructions page."""
    blocks = render_to_notion_blocks(report)
    headers = {
        "Authorization": f"Bearer {NOTION_TOKEN}",
        "Notion-Version": NOTION_VERSION,
        "Content-Type": "application/json",
    }

    resp = requests.patch(
        f"{NOTION_API}/blocks/{VCC_INSTRUCTIONS_PAGE_ID}/children",
        headers=headers,
        json={"children": blocks},
    )
    resp.raise_for_status()
    return report.cycle_id


# ── CLI Entry Point ──────────────────────────────────────────────
if __name__ == "__main__":
    import argparse

    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="VCC Cycle Reporter")
    parser.add_argument("--from", dest="from_sha", required=True,
                        help="Start commit SHA")
    parser.add_argument("--to", dest="to_sha", required=True,
                        help="End commit SHA (inclusive)")
    parser.add_argument("--next-phase", default="",
                        help="Next build phase (e.g. P1)")
    parser.add_argument("--next-srs", nargs="*", default=[],
                        help="SRS codes for next cycle")
    parser.add_argument("--blocker", nargs="*", default=[],
                        help="Blockers for next cycle")
    parser.add_argument("--question", nargs="*", default=[],
                        help="Questions for operator")
    parser.add_argument("--dry-run", action="store_true",
                        help="Print report without posting to Notion")

    args = parser.parse_args()

    print(f"Building cycle report: {args.from_sha}..{args.to_sha}")
    report = build_report(
        from_sha=args.from_sha,
        to_sha=args.to_sha,
        next_srs=args.next_srs,
        next_phase=args.next_phase,
        blockers=args.blocker,
        operator_questions=args.question,
    )

    if args.dry_run:
        print(json.dumps(asdict(report), indent=2, default=str))
        print(f"\nGuardrails: {'PASS' if report.guardrail_pass else 'FAIL'}")
        print(f"Violations: {len(report.guardrail_violations)}")
        print(f"Drift items: {len(report.drift_items)}")
        print(f"Questions: {len(report.vcc_questions)}")
        print(f"Conflicts: {len(report.vcc_conflicts)}")
    else:
        cycle_id = post_to_notion(report)
        print(f"✅ Posted cycle report: {cycle_id}")
```

## 11.5 Usage

```bash
# Basic usage — post report for a commit range
python tools/vcc_cycle_reporter.py \\
  --from 551a38 \\
  --to 225ee9e

# With next cycle intent + blockers
python tools/vcc_cycle_reporter.py \\
  --from 551a38 \\
  --to 225ee9e \\
  --next-phase P1 \\
  --next-srs SRS-FIN-010 SRS-FIN-011 SRS-FIN-012 \\
  --blocker "Xero OAuth creds not provisioned" \\
  --question "Should quote PDF use same template as invoice PDF?"

# Dry run — print report without posting
python tools/vcc_cycle_reporter.py \\
  --from 551a38 \\
  --to 225ee9e \\
  --dry-run
```

## 11.6 Integration with `vcc_git_reporter.py`

The existing `vcc_git_reporter.py` MUST be retired or refactored to call `vcc_cycle_reporter.py` internally. Raw commit posting is **no longer allowed** after this protocol takes effect.
```python
# Replace the old vcc_git_reporter.py with:

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""vcc_git_reporter.py — DEPRECATED. Delegates to vcc_cycle_reporter.py"""
import subprocess
import sys

def main():
    # Get last 50 commits range
    result = subprocess.run(
        ["git", "log", "--oneline", "-50", "--format=%H"],
        capture_output=True, encoding="utf-8",
    )
    shas = result.stdout.strip().split("\n")
    if len(shas) < 2:
        print("Not enough commits to build a range.")
        return

    from_sha = shas[-1][:7]  # Oldest
    to_sha = shas[0][:7]     # Newest

    subprocess.run([
        sys.executable, "tools/vcc_cycle_reporter.py",
        "--from", from_sha,
        "--to", to_sha,
    ])

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

## 11.7 Environment Variables

| **Variable** | **Required** | **Notes** |
| `NOTION_INTERNAL_TOKEN` | ✅ | Notion API token with write access to this page |
| `VCC_INSTRUCTIONS_PAGE_ID` | ✅ | Page ID of this document (Finance Guild — VCC Build Instructions & Guardrails) |
| `REPO_ROOT` | Optional | Defaults to current directory. Set if running from a different working dir. |

## 11.8 Enforcement


[CALLOUT] 🚨 **This protocol is enforced.** Any VCC build cycle that ends without a structured Cycle Report — or that dumps raw git commits instead — is considered **incomplete**. The operator WILL reject the output and require a re-run with proper reporting.

The VCC's CI/CD pipeline (`.gitlab-ci.yml`) SHOULD include a post-deploy stage that auto-runs the reporter:
```yaml
# .gitlab-ci.yml — add after deploy stage
vcc-cycle-report:
  stage: post-deploy
  script:
    - |
      PREV_SHA=$(git rev-parse HEAD~${CI_COMMIT_COUNT:-50})
      python tools/vcc_cycle_reporter.py \\
        --from $PREV_SHA \\
        --to $CI_COMMIT_SHA
  rules:
    - if: $CI_COMMIT_BRANCH == "main"
  allow_failure: true  # Don't block deploy if Notion is down
```

## 11.9 Service Health Check Protocol

Every CRP cycle report MUST include a §7 health probe sweep. The VCC runs `health_checker.py` against all 5 SMP services before finalizing the report. Any service with `consecutive_failures >= 3` makes the entire cycle **NO-GO**.

### Health Endpoint Contract

Every SMP service MUST expose `GET /health` returning:
```json
{
  "service": "smp-fin-api",
  "status": "healthy",
  "version": "0.1.0",
  "uptime_seconds": 3600,
  "dependencies": {
    "supabase": {"status": "connected", "latency_ms": 12},
    "nats": {"status": "connected", "latency_ms": 3},
    "redis": {"status": "connected", "latency_ms": 5},
    "stripe": {"status": "connected", "latency_ms": 45},
    "ses": {"status": "connected", "latency_ms": 28}
  },
  "checks": {
    "rls_active": true,
    "migrations_current": true,
    "nats_subscriptions": 12,
    "cache_hit_rate": 0.87
  },
  "timestamp": "2026-02-27T19:30:00Z"
}
```
Services WITHOUT an HTTP port (`smp-fin-worker`) expose health via NATS request-reply on `citadel.finance.worker.health`.

### Implementation — `health_checker.py`

Place at `tools/health_checker.py`:
```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Service Health Checker — CRP §7 health probe sweep.

Runs liveness + readiness checks on all Finance Guild SMP services.
Outputs structured JSON for CRP integration.
Usage: python tools/health_checker.py [--json] [--fail-on-unhealthy]
"""

import os
import json
import time
import asyncio
from dataclasses import dataclass, field, asdict
from datetime import datetime, timezone
from typing import Optional

import httpx

# ── Service Registry ─────────────────────────────────────────────
SERVICES = [
    {"id": "smp-fin-api",    "url": "http://localhost:8093/health", "protocol": "http"},
    {"id": "smp-fin-ws",     "url": "http://localhost:8094/health", "protocol": "http"},
    {"id": "smp-fin-pdf",    "url": "http://localhost:8095/health", "protocol": "http"},
    {"id": "smp-fin-ai",     "url": "http://localhost:8096/health", "protocol": "http"},
    {"id": "smp-fin-worker", "url": None, "protocol": "nats",
     "nats_subject": "citadel.finance.worker.health"},
]

BLOCKING_THRESHOLD = 3  # consecutive failures before NO-GO


@dataclass
class DependencyStatus:
    name: str
    status: str       # "connected" | "disconnected" | "degraded"
    latency_ms: float = 0.0


@dataclass
class ServiceHealth:
    service_id: str
    status: str            # "healthy" | "unhealthy" | "unreachable"
    response_time_ms: float = 0.0
    version: str = "unknown"
    uptime_seconds: float = 0.0
    dependencies: list = field(default_factory=list)
    checks: dict = field(default_factory=dict)
    consecutive_failures: int = 0
    last_checked: str = ""
    error: Optional[str] = None
    blocking: bool = False


@dataclass
class HealthReport:
    timestamp: str
    total_services: int
    healthy_count: int
    unhealthy_count: int
    unreachable_count: int
    blocking: bool          # True if any service has consecutive_failures >= 3
    blocking_services: list  # service IDs that are blocking
    services: list           # list[ServiceHealth]


# ── State File (tracks consecutive failures across runs) ─────────
STATE_FILE = os.environ.get("HEALTH_STATE_FILE", ".health_state.json")


def load_state() -> dict:
    try:
        with open(STATE_FILE) as f:
            return json.load(f)
    except (FileNotFoundError, json.JSONDecodeError):
        return {}


def save_state(state: dict):
    with open(STATE_FILE, "w") as f:
        json.dump(state, f, indent=2)


# ── HTTP Health Check ────────────────────────────────────────────
async def check_http_health(service: dict, client: httpx.AsyncClient) -> ServiceHealth:
    service_id = service["id"]
    url = service["url"]
    start = time.monotonic()
    try:
        resp = await client.get(url, timeout=10.0)
        elapsed = (time.monotonic() - start) * 1000
        if resp.status_code == 200:
            data = resp.json()
            deps = []
            for dep_name, dep_info in data.get("dependencies", {}).items():
                deps.append(DependencyStatus(
                    name=dep_name,
                    status=dep_info.get("status", "unknown"),
                    latency_ms=dep_info.get("latency_ms", 0),
                ))
            return ServiceHealth(
                service_id=service_id,
                status=data.get("status", "healthy"),
                response_time_ms=round(elapsed, 1),
                version=data.get("version", "unknown"),
                uptime_seconds=data.get("uptime_seconds", 0),
                dependencies=[asdict(d) for d in deps],
                checks=data.get("checks", {}),
                last_checked=datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),
            )
        else:
            return ServiceHealth(
                service_id=service_id,
                status="unhealthy",
                response_time_ms=round(elapsed, 1),
                error=f"HTTP {resp.status_code}: {resp.text[:200]}",
                last_checked=datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),
            )
    except Exception as e:
        elapsed = (time.monotonic() - start) * 1000
        return ServiceHealth(
            service_id=service_id,
            status="unreachable",
            response_time_ms=round(elapsed, 1),
            error=str(e)[:200],
            last_checked=datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),
        )


# ── NATS Health Check (for worker) ───────────────────────────────
async def check_nats_health(service: dict) -> ServiceHealth:
    """Check worker health via NATS request-reply."""
    service_id = service["id"]
    nats_url = os.environ.get("NATS_URL", "nats://localhost:4222")
    try:
        import nats as nats_client
        nc = await nats_client.connect(nats_url)
        start = time.monotonic()
        resp = await nc.request(
            service["nats_subject"],
            b'{"check": "health"}',
            timeout=5.0,
        )
        elapsed = (time.monotonic() - start) * 1000
        await nc.close()
        data = json.loads(resp.data.decode())
        return ServiceHealth(
            service_id=service_id,
            status=data.get("status", "healthy"),
            response_time_ms=round(elapsed, 1),
            version=data.get("version", "unknown"),
            uptime_seconds=data.get("uptime_seconds", 0),
            checks=data.get("checks", {}),
            last_checked=datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),
        )
    except Exception as e:
        return ServiceHealth(
            service_id=service_id,
            status="unreachable",
            error=f"NATS check failed: {e}",
            last_checked=datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),
        )


# ── Orchestrator ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
async def run_health_sweep() -> HealthReport:
    """Run health checks on all Finance Guild services."""
    state = load_state()
    results = []

    async with httpx.AsyncClient() as client:
        tasks = []
        for svc in SERVICES:
            if svc["protocol"] == "http":
                tasks.append(check_http_health(svc, client))
            elif svc["protocol"] == "nats":
                tasks.append(check_nats_health(svc))
        results = await asyncio.gather(*tasks)

    # Update consecutive failure tracking
    for r in results:
        prev = state.get(r.service_id, {"consecutive_failures": 0})
        if r.status != "healthy":
            r.consecutive_failures = prev["consecutive_failures"] + 1
        else:
            r.consecutive_failures = 0
        r.blocking = r.consecutive_failures >= BLOCKING_THRESHOLD
        state[r.service_id] = {
            "consecutive_failures": r.consecutive_failures,
            "last_status": r.status,
            "last_checked": r.last_checked,
        }
    save_state(state)

    healthy = sum(1 for r in results if r.status == "healthy")
    unhealthy = sum(1 for r in results if r.status == "unhealthy")
    unreachable = sum(1 for r in results if r.status == "unreachable")
    blocking_svcs = [r.service_id for r in results if r.blocking]

    return HealthReport(
        timestamp=datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),
        total_services=len(results),
        healthy_count=healthy,
        unhealthy_count=unhealthy,
        unreachable_count=unreachable,
        blocking=len(blocking_svcs) > 0,
        blocking_services=blocking_svcs,
        services=[asdict(r) for r in results],
    )


def render_for_crp(report: HealthReport) -> str:
    """Render health report as text for CRP §7 embedding."""
    lines = [f"Service Health Sweep — {report.timestamp}"]
    lines.append(f"  {report.healthy_count}/{report.total_services} healthy")
    for svc in report.services:
        icon = "✅" if svc["status"] == "healthy" else "🚫" if svc["blocking"] else "⚠️"
        line = f"  {icon} {svc['service_id']}: {svc['status']} ({svc['response_time_ms']:.0f}ms)"
        if svc["consecutive_failures"] > 0:
            line += f" [failures: {svc['consecutive_failures']}]"
        if svc["error"]:
            line += f" — {svc['error'][:80]}"
        lines.append(line)
        # Dependency sub-lines
        for dep in svc.get("dependencies", []):
            dep_icon = "✅" if dep["status"] == "connected" else "🚫"
            lines.append(f"    {dep_icon} {dep['name']}: {dep['status']} ({dep['latency_ms']:.0f}ms)")
    if report.blocking:
        lines.append(f"  🛑 BLOCKING: {', '.join(report.blocking_services)}")
        lines.append("  Cycle verdict: NO-GO (health check failure)")
    else:
        lines.append("  ✅ All services healthy — no blocking issues")
    return "\n".join(lines)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    import argparse
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Finance Guild Health Checker")
    parser.add_argument("--json", action="store_true", help="Output raw JSON")
    parser.add_argument("--fail-on-unhealthy", action="store_true",
                        help="Exit code 1 if any service is blocking")
    args = parser.parse_args()

    report = asyncio.run(run_health_sweep())

    if args.json:
        print(json.dumps(asdict(report), indent=2))
    else:
        print(render_for_crp(report))

    if args.fail_on_unhealthy and report.blocking:
        exit(1)
```

### Usage

```bash
# Full health sweep with human-readable output
python tools/health_checker.py

# JSON output for CRP integration
python tools/health_checker.py --json

# CI gate — exit 1 if any service is blocking (consecutive_failures >= 3)
python tools/health_checker.py --fail-on-unhealthy
```

### CI Integration

Add to `.gitlab-ci.yml` as a pre-deploy gate:
```yaml
health-gate:
  stage: smoke-test
  script:
    - python tools/health_checker.py --fail-on-unhealthy
  rules:
    - if: $CI_COMMIT_BRANCH == "main"
  allow_failure: false  # Blocks deployment if unhealthy
```

## 11.10 Diff Check Enforcement — Blocking Gate

The three-layer diff check (§8) is a **hard gate**. No cycle report may be accepted with dirty, unacknowledged diffs.

### Acknowledged Drifts

If a drift is intentional (e.g., spec was updated mid-cycle), the VCC MUST either:
1. **In code:** Annotate the drifting file with `# DRIFT-ACK: <reason>` on the relevant line
1. **In config:** Add the SRS code + reason to `crp_config.yaml`:
```yaml
acknowledged_drifts:
  - srs_code: "SRS-FIN-019"
    reason: "Recurring billing spec updated mid-cycle — columns added"
    acknowledged_by: "mr.nobody"
    date: "2026-02-27"
```

### Enforcement Rules

- ✅ All three diff layers (Spec→Code, Cycle→Cycle, Blueprint→Blueprint) MUST be present in every CRP
- ✅ Each layer outputs `clean: true` or `clean: false` with itemized deltas
- ✅ `clean: false` on **any** layer without a matching `DRIFT-ACK` → cycle is **NO-GO**
- ✅ `diff_checker.py --all-layers --strict` MUST return exit code 0 for CI to pass
- 🚫 NEVER suppress diff output — even if "nothing changed", prove it with the full three-layer scan
- 🚫 NEVER bulk-acknowledge drifts without operator approval — each `DRIFT-ACK` must be reviewed

[CALLOUT] 🚨 **Diff check is a blocking CRP gate.** A cycle report with `clean: false` on any unacknowledged layer is automatically flagged NO-GO. The VCC MUST fix all drifts or obtain explicit operator acknowledgment before the cycle can be accepted.


---


# 12. CRP Automation — YAML Config, JSON Schema & Jinja2 Templates

This section provides the machine-readable definitions that power the Cycle Report Protocol. The VCC MUST use these to validate reports, render Notion blocks, generate Slack summaries, and produce CI artifacts.

    pattern: "\\b(FLOAT|DOUBLE PRECISION|REAL)\\b"

    pattern: "SELECT\\s+\\*\\s+FROM"
    glob: "*.py"

    glob: "*.py"

    message: "Pydantic models must not use Any type"

    glob: "*.tsx"

    pattern: 'localStorage\\.setItem\\(["\'](?:token|jwt|secret|key|password)'

    pattern: "dangerouslySetInnerHTML"

    severity: critical

  - id: RLS_ENABLED
    pattern: "CREATE TABLE(?!.*ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY)"

    glob: "*.tsx"

    unified_diff_artifact: true  # build/diffs/VCC-FIN-*.diff
    json_summary: true           # build/diffs/VCC-FIN-*.diff.json
    artifact_dir: "build/diffs"
    fail_cycle_on_critical_drift: true
