```yaml
  artifact_dir: "build/reports"
```

## 12.2 JSON Schema — `crp_report_schema.json`

Place at `config/crp_report_schema.json`. Used by `vcc_cycle_reporter.py` to validate every report before posting.
```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "https://citadel-nexus.com/schemas/crp/v1.0/cycle-report.json",
  "title": "VCC Cycle Report",
  "description": "Structured cycle report conforming to CRP v1.0",
  "type": "object",
  "required": [
    "cycle_id", "guild", "started_at", "ended_at", "author_chain",
    "commit_range", "total_commits", "total_files_changed",
    "total_insertions", "total_deletions", "sections"
  ],
  "properties": {
    "cycle_id": {
      "type": "string",
      "pattern": "^VCC-[A-Z]{2,5}-\\d{8}-\\d{4}$",
      "description": "Format: VCC-{GUILD}-{YYYYMMDD}-{HHMM}"
    },
    "guild": {
      "type": "string",
      "enum": ["FIN", "COM", "INT", "RES", "CRE", "BLD", "ENT", "WRT"]
    },
    "started_at": {"type": "string", "format": "date-time"},
    "ended_at": {"type": "string", "format": "date-time"},
    "author_chain": {
      "type": "array",
      "items": {"type": "string"},
      "minItems": 1,
      "description": "Claude model names used in this cycle"
    },
    "commit_range": {
      "type": "string",
      "pattern": "^[0-9a-f]{7}\\.\\.[0-9a-f]{7}$"
    },
    "total_commits": {"type": "integer", "minimum": 1},
    "total_files_changed": {"type": "integer", "minimum": 0},
    "total_insertions": {"type": "integer", "minimum": 0},
    "total_deletions": {"type": "integer", "minimum": 0},
    "sections": {
      "type": "object",
      "required": [
        "what_was_built", "guardrails", "flags",
        "drift", "next_cycle", "health"
      ],
      "properties": {
        "what_was_built": {
          "type": "object",
          "required": ["srs_codes_touched", "files_created", "files_modified"],
          "properties": {
            "srs_codes_touched": {
              "type": "object",
              "patternProperties": {
                "^SRS-FIN-\\d{3}$": {
                  "type": "object",
                  "required": ["name", "status"],
                  "properties": {
                    "name": {"type": "string"},
                    "status": {"type": "string", "enum": ["🔵 Spec'd", "🟡 In Progress", "🟢 Built", "🔴 Blocked", "🟠 Partial"]}
                  }
                }
              }
            },
            "files_created": {"type": "array", "items": {"type": "string"}},
            "files_modified": {"type": "array", "items": {"type": "string"}},
            "tables_migrated": {"type": "array", "items": {"type": "string"}},
            "rls_policies_added": {"type": "array", "items": {"type": "string"}},
            "components_scaffolded": {"type": "array", "items": {"type": "string"}}
          }
        },
        "guardrails": {
          "type": "object",
          "required": ["pass", "violations"],
          "properties": {
            "pass": {"type": "boolean"},
            "critical_count": {"type": "integer", "minimum": 0},
            "warning_count": {"type": "integer", "minimum": 0},
            "violations": {
              "type": "array",
              "items": {
                "type": "object",
                "required": ["rule", "file", "line", "severity"],
                "properties": {
                  "rule": {"type": "string"},
                  "file": {"type": "string"},
                  "line": {"type": "integer"},
                  "snippet": {"type": "string", "maxLength": 200},
                  "severity": {"type": "string", "enum": ["critical", "warning"]}
                }
              }
            }
          }
        },
        "flags": {
          "type": "object",
          "required": ["questions", "conflicts"],
          "properties": {
            "questions": {
              "type": "array",
              "items": {
                "type": "object",
                "required": ["file", "line", "text"],
                "properties": {
                  "file": {"type": "string"},
                  "line": {"type": "integer"},
                  "text": {"type": "string", "maxLength": 200}
                }
              }
            },
            "conflicts": {
              "type": "array",
              "items": {
                "type": "object",
                "required": ["file", "line", "text"],
                "properties": {
                  "file": {"type": "string"},
                  "line": {"type": "integer"},
                  "text": {"type": "string", "maxLength": 200}
                }
              }
            }
          }
        },
        "drift": {
          "type": "object",
          "required": ["items"],
          "properties": {
            "clean": {"type": "boolean"},
            "items": {
              "type": "array",
              "items": {
                "type": "object",
                "required": ["srs_code", "name", "status", "detail"],
                "properties": {
                  "srs_code": {"type": "string"},
                  "name": {"type": "string"},
                  "status": {"type": "string", "enum": ["missing", "orphaned", "stale", "partial"]},
                  "detail": {"type": "string"}
                }
              }
            }
          }
        },
        "next_cycle": {
          "type": "object",
          "required": ["srs_codes", "phase"],
          "properties": {
            "srs_codes": {"type": "array", "items": {"type": "string"}},
            "phase": {"type": "string"},
            "estimated_files": {"type": "integer"},
            "blockers": {"type": "array", "items": {"type": "string"}},
            "operator_questions": {"type": "array", "items": {"type": "string"}}
          }
        },
        "health": {
          "type": "object",
          "required": ["notion_sync"],
          "properties": {
            "notion_sync": {"type": "string", "enum": ["ok", "fail", "partial"]},
            "nats_events_published": {"type": "integer", "minimum": 0},
            "migrations_applied": {"type": "array", "items": {"type": "string"}},
            "migrations_pending": {"type": "array", "items": {"type": "string"}},
            "test_passed": {"type": "integer", "minimum": 0},
            "test_failed": {"type": "integer", "minimum": 0},
            "build_time_seconds": {"type": "number", "minimum": 0},
            "bundle_size_kb": {"type": "number", "minimum": 0}
          }
        }
      }
    }
  }
}
```

## 12.3 Jinja2 Templates

Place in `templates/crp/`. The VCC MUST use these templates — no inline string building.

### 12.3.1 Notion Block Template — `notion_report.json.j2`

Renders the CycleReport dataclass to Notion API block JSON. Used by `render_to_notion_blocks()`.
```javascript
{# templates/crp/notion_report.json.j2 — Notion API blocks for Cycle Report #}
{# Input: report (CycleReport), config (crp_config), SRS_CODES (dict) #}
[
  {"object": "block", "type": "divider", "divider": {}},
  {
    "object": "block",
    "type": "heading_2",
    "heading_2": {
      "rich_text": [{
        "type": "text",
        "text": {
          "content": "📊 Cycle  report.cycle_id  |  report.total_commits  commits | + report.total_insertions /- report.total_deletions  lines | Guardrails:  '✅' if report.guardrail_pass else '🚫' "
        }
      }],
      "is_toggleable": true,
      "children": [
        {# §1 Cycle Header #}
        {
          "object": "block", "type": "callout",
          "callout": {
            "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": "Range:  report.commit_range \nStarted:  report.started_at \nEnded:  report.ended_at \nAuthors:  report.author_chain | join(', ') \nFiles changed:  report.total_files_changed "}}],
            "icon": {"type": "emoji", "emoji": "🔧"},
            "color": "gray_background"
          }
        },

        {# §2 What Was Built #}
        {"object": "block", "type": "heading_3", "heading_3": {
          "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": "§2 What Was Built"}}]
        }},
        {% if report.srs_codes_touched %}
        {% for code, status in report.srs_codes_touched.items() %}
        {"object": "block", "type": "bulleted_list_item", "bulleted_list_item": {
          "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": " code  — {{ SRS_CODES.get(code, {}).get('name', 'Unknown') }} →  status "}}]
        }} "," if not loop.last 
        {% endfor %}
        {% else %}
        {"object": "block", "type": "paragraph", "paragraph": {
          "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": "No SRS codes explicitly referenced in commits."}}]
        }}
        {% endif %},
        {% if report.tables_migrated %}
        {"object": "block", "type": "paragraph", "paragraph": {
          "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": "Tables created/migrated:  report.tables_migrated | join(', ') "}}]
        }},
        {% endif %}
        {% if report.rls_policies_added %}
        {"object": "block", "type": "paragraph", "paragraph": {
          "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": "RLS policies added:  report.rls_policies_added | length "}}]
        }},
        {% endif %}

        {# §3 Guardrails Compliance #}
        {"object": "block", "type": "heading_3", "heading_3": {
          "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": "§3 Guardrails Compliance"}}]
        }},
        {% if report.guardrail_pass %}
        {"object": "block", "type": "callout", "callout": {
          "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": "All guardrails passed — no critical violations."}}],
          "icon": {"type": "emoji", "emoji": "✅"},
          "color": "green_background"
        }}
        {% else %}
        {"object": "block", "type": "callout", "callout": {
          "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": "VIOLATIONS:  report.guardrail_violations | selectattr('severity', 'eq', 'critical') | list | length  critical,  report.guardrail_violations | selectattr('severity', 'eq', 'warning') | list | length  warnings"}}],
          "icon": {"type": "emoji", "emoji": "🚫"},
          "color": "red_background"
        }},
        {% for v in report.guardrail_violations[:20] %}
        {"object": "block", "type": "bulleted_list_item", "bulleted_list_item": {
          "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": "[ v.severity | upper ]  v.rule  —  v.file : v.line  —  v.snippet | truncate(120) "}}]
        }} "," if not loop.last 
        {% endfor %}
        {% endif %},

        {# §4 Flags & Questions #}
        {"object": "block", "type": "heading_3", "heading_3": {
          "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": "§4 Flags & Questions"}}]
        }},
        {% if not report.vcc_questions and not report.vcc_conflicts %}
        {"object": "block", "type": "paragraph", "paragraph": {
          "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": "No flags raised."}}]
        }}
        {% else %}
        {% for q in report.vcc_questions %}
        {"object": "block", "type": "bulleted_list_item", "bulleted_list_item": {
          "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": "❓ VCC-QUESTION:  q.file : q.line  —  q.text | truncate(180) "}}]
        }},
        {% endfor %}
        {% for c in report.vcc_conflicts %}
        {"object": "block", "type": "bulleted_list_item", "bulleted_list_item": {
          "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": "⚠️ VCC-CONFLICT:  c.file : c.line  —  c.text | truncate(180) "}}]
        }} "," if not loop.last 
        {% endfor %}
        {% endif %},

        {# §5 Drift Report #}
        {"object": "block", "type": "heading_3", "heading_3": {
          "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": "§5 Drift Report"}}]
        }},
        {% if not report.drift_items %}
        {"object": "block", "type": "paragraph", "paragraph": {
          "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": "No drift detected — codebase matches spec."}}]
        }}
        {% else %}
        {% set status_emoji = {"missing": "🔴", "orphaned": "🟡", "stale": "⚪", "partial": "🟠"} %}
        {% for d in report.drift_items %}
        {"object": "block", "type": "bulleted_list_item", "bulleted_list_item": {
          "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": " status_emoji[d.status]  [ d.status | upper ]  d.srs_code   d.name  —  d.detail "}}]
        }} "," if not loop.last 
        {% endfor %}
        {% endif %},

        {# §6 Next Cycle Intent #}
        {"object": "block", "type": "heading_3", "heading_3": {
          "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": "§6 Next Cycle Intent"}}]
        }},
        {% if report.next_srs_codes %}
        {"object": "block", "type": "paragraph", "paragraph": {
          "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": "Target phase:  report.next_phase "}}]
        }},
        {% for code in report.next_srs_codes %}
        {"object": "block", "type": "bulleted_list_item", "bulleted_list_item": {
          "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": " code  — {{ SRS_CODES.get(code, {}).get('name', 'Unknown') }}"}}]
        }},
        {% endfor %}
        {% endif %}
        {% if report.blockers %}
        {"object": "block", "type": "paragraph", "paragraph": {
          "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": "Blockers:"}, "annotations": {"bold": true}}]
        }},
        {% for b in report.blockers %}
        {"object": "block", "type": "bulleted_list_item", "bulleted_list_item": {
          "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": "🛑  b "}}]
        }},
        {% endfor %}
        {% endif %}
        {% if report.operator_questions %}
        {"object": "block", "type": "paragraph", "paragraph": {
          "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": "Questions for operator:"}, "annotations": {"bold": true}}]
        }},
        {% for q in report.operator_questions %}
        {"object": "block", "type": "bulleted_list_item", "bulleted_list_item": {
          "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": "❓  q "}}]
        }},
        {% endfor %}
        {% endif %}

        {# §7 Health Metrics #}
        {"object": "block", "type": "heading_3", "heading_3": {
          "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": "§7 Health Metrics"}}]
        }},
        {
          "object": "block", "type": "callout",
          "callout": {
            "rich_text": [{"type": "text", "text": {"content": "Notion sync:  report.notion_sync_status \nNATS events:  report.nats_events_published \nMigrations applied:  report.migrations_applied | length  | Pending:  report.migrations_pending | length \nTests:  report.test_passed  passed,  report.test_failed  failed\nBuild time:  '%.1f' | format(report.build_time_seconds) s | Bundle:  '%.0f' | format(report.bundle_size_kb)  KB"}}],
            "icon": {"type": "emoji", "emoji": "📈"},
            "color": "purple_background"
          }
        }
      ]
    }
  }
]
```

### 12.3.2 Slack Summary Template — `slack_summary.json.j2`

Renders a compact Slack Block Kit message for the `#vcc-builds` channel.
```javascript
{# templates/crp/slack_summary.json.j2 — Slack Block Kit notification #}
{# Input: report (CycleReport), config (crp_config) #}
{
  "blocks": [
    {
      "type": "header",
      "text": {
        "type": "plain_text",
        "text": " '✅' if report.guardrail_pass else '🚫'  VCC Cycle Report —  report.cycle_id "
      }
    },
    {
      "type": "section",
      "fields": [
        {"type": "mrkdwn", "text": "*Commits:*  report.total_commits "},
        {"type": "mrkdwn", "text": "*Range:* ` report.commit_range `"},
        {"type": "mrkdwn", "text": "*Lines:* + report.total_insertions /- report.total_deletions "},
        {"type": "mrkdwn", "text": "*Authors:*  report.author_chain | join(', ') "}
      ]
    },
    {"type": "divider"},
    {
      "type": "section",
      "text": {
        "type": "mrkdwn",
        "text": "*§2 What Was Built*\n{% if report.srs_codes_touched %}{% for code, status in report.srs_codes_touched.items() %}•  code  →  status \n{% endfor %}{% else %}_No SRS codes referenced._{% endif %}"
      }
    },
    {% if not report.guardrail_pass %}
    {
      "type": "section",
      "text": {
        "type": "mrkdwn",
        "text": "*🚫 §3 Guardrail Violations*\n{% for v in report.guardrail_violations[:5] %}• `[ v.severity | upper ]`  v.rule  —  v.file : v.line \n{% endfor %}{% if report.guardrail_violations | length > 5 %}_...and  report.guardrail_violations | length - 5  more. See Notion._{% endif %}"
      }
    },
    {% endif %}
    {% if report.drift_items %}
    {
      "type": "section",
      "text": {
        "type": "mrkdwn",
        "text": "*§5 Drift*\n{% for d in report.drift_items[:5] %}•  d.status | upper :  d.srs_code   d.name \n{% endfor %}"
      }
    },
    {% endif %}
    {% if report.blockers %}
    {
      "type": "section",
      "text": {
        "type": "mrkdwn",
        "text": "*🛑 Blockers*\n{% for b in report.blockers %}•  b \n{% endfor %}"
      }
    },
    {% endif %}
    {% if report.operator_questions %}
    {
      "type": "section",
      "text": {
        "type": "mrkdwn",
        "text": "*❓ Operator Questions*\n{% for q in report.operator_questions %}•  q \n{% endfor %}"
      }
    },
    {% endif %}
    {
      "type": "context",
      "elements": [
        {
          "type": "mrkdwn",
          "text": "Tests:  report.test_passed ✅  report.test_failed ❌ | Notion:  report.notion_sync_status  | Build:  '%.1f' | format(report.build_time_seconds) s{% if not report.guardrail_pass %} |  config.notifications.slack.mention_on_violation {% endif %}"
        }
      ]
    }
  ]
}
```

### 12.3.3 Markdown Artifact Template — `cycle_report.md.j2`

Saved to `build/reports/VCC-FIN-YYYYMMDD-HHMM.md` for git commit as CI artifact.
```javascript
{# templates/crp/cycle_report.md.j2 — Markdown artifact for git/CI #}
{# Input: report (CycleReport), config (crp_config), SRS_CODES (dict) #}
#  report.cycle_id  — Cycle Report

> **Protocol:** CRP v config.protocol.version  | **Guild:**  report.guild  | **Guardrails:**  '✅ PASS' if report.guardrail_pass else '🚫 FAIL' 

## §1 Cycle Header

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Cycle ID | ` report.cycle_id ` |
| Started |  report.started_at  |
| Ended |  report.ended_at  |
| Authors |  report.author_chain | join(', ')  |
| Commit Range | ` report.commit_range ` |
| Total Commits |  report.total_commits  |
| Files Changed |  report.total_files_changed  |
| Insertions | + report.total_insertions  |
| Deletions | - report.total_deletions  |

## §2 What Was Built

{% if report.srs_codes_touched %}
| SRS Code | Feature | Status |
|----------|---------|--------|
{% for code, status in report.srs_codes_touched.items() %}
|  code  | {{ SRS_CODES.get(code, {}).get('name', 'Unknown') }} |  status  |
{% endfor %}
{% else %}
_No SRS codes explicitly referenced in commits._
{% endif %}

{% if report.tables_migrated %}
**Tables:**  report.tables_migrated | join(', ') 
{% endif %}
{% if report.rls_policies_added %}
**RLS Policies Added:**  report.rls_policies_added | length 
{% endif %}
{% if report.components_scaffolded %}
**Components:**  report.components_scaffolded | join(', ') 
{% endif %}

## §3 Guardrails Compliance

{% if report.guardrail_pass %}
✅ All guardrails passed — no critical violations.
{% else %}
🚫 **VIOLATIONS:**  report.guardrail_violations | selectattr('severity', 'eq', 'critical') | list | length  critical,  report.guardrail_violations | selectattr('severity', 'eq', 'warning') | list | length  warnings

| Severity | Rule | File | Line | Snippet |
|----------|------|------|------|---------|
{% for v in report.guardrail_violations %}
|  v.severity | upper  |  v.rule  | ` v.file ` |  v.line  | ` v.snippet | truncate(80) ` |
{% endfor %}
{% endif %}

## §4 Flags & Questions

{% if not report.vcc_questions and not report.vcc_conflicts %}
No flags raised.
{% else %}
{% for q in report.vcc_questions %}
- ❓ **VCC-QUESTION:** ` q.file : q.line ` —  q.text 
{% endfor %}
{% for c in report.vcc_conflicts %}
- ⚠️ **VCC-CONFLICT:** ` c.file : c.line ` —  c.text 
{% endfor %}
{% endif %}

## §5 Drift Report

{% if not report.drift_items %}
No drift detected — codebase matches spec.
{% else %}
| Status | SRS Code | Feature | Detail |
|--------|----------|---------|--------|
{% for d in report.drift_items %}
|  d.status | upper  |  d.srs_code  |  d.name  |  d.detail  |
{% endfor %}
{% endif %}

## §6 Next Cycle Intent

{% if report.next_srs_codes %}
**Target Phase:**  report.next_phase 
{% for code in report.next_srs_codes %}
-  code  — {{ SRS_CODES.get(code, {}).get('name', 'Unknown') }}
{% endfor %}
{% endif %}
{% if report.blockers %}

**Blockers:**
{% for b in report.blockers %}
- 🛑  b 
{% endfor %}
{% endif %}
{% if report.operator_questions %}

**Questions for Operator:**
{% for q in report.operator_questions %}
- ❓  q 
{% endfor %}
{% endif %}

## §7 Health Metrics

| Metric | Value |
|--------|-------|
| Notion Sync |  report.notion_sync_status  |
| NATS Events |  report.nats_events_published  |
| Migrations Applied |  report.migrations_applied | length  |
| Migrations Pending |  report.migrations_pending | length  |
| Tests Passed |  report.test_passed  |
| Tests Failed |  report.test_failed  |
| Build Time |  '%.1f' | format(report.build_time_seconds) s |
| Bundle Size |  '%.0f' | format(report.bundle_size_kb)  KB |

---
_Generated by VCC Cycle Reporter — CRP v config.protocol.version _
```

### 12.3.4 NATS Event Template — `nats_event.json.j2`

Published to `citadel.vcc.cycle.report` for downstream consumers (n8n, dashboards, alerting).
```javascript
{# templates/crp/nats_event.json.j2 — NATS JetStream event payload #}
{# Input: report (CycleReport) #}
{
  "event": "vcc.cycle.report",
  "version": "1.0",
  "timestamp": " report.ended_at ",
  "data": {
    "cycle_id": " report.cycle_id ",
    "guild": " report.guild ",
    "commit_range": " report.commit_range ",
    "total_commits":  report.total_commits ,
    "insertions":  report.total_insertions ,
    "deletions":  report.total_deletions ,
    "guardrail_pass":  'true' if report.guardrail_pass else 'false' ,
    "critical_violations":  report.guardrail_violations | selectattr('severity', 'eq', 'critical') | list | length ,
    "warning_violations":  report.guardrail_violations | selectattr('severity', 'eq', 'warning') | list | length ,
    "drift_count":  report.drift_items | length ,
    "questions_count":  report.vcc_questions | length ,
    "conflicts_count":  report.vcc_conflicts | length ,
    "srs_codes_touched":  report.srs_codes_touched | tojson ,
    "test_passed":  report.test_passed ,
    "test_failed":  report.test_failed ,
    "notion_sync": " report.notion_sync_status ",
    "author_chain":  report.author_chain | tojson ,
    "has_blockers":  'true' if report.blockers else 'false' ,
    "next_phase": " report.next_phase "
  }
}
```

## 12.4 Template Loader — `crp_templates.py`

Helper module that loads and renders all Jinja2 templates. Place at `tools/crp_templates.py`.
```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""CRP Template Loader — Jinja2 rendering for all CRP output formats."""

import json
import yaml
from pathlib import Path
from dataclasses import asdict
from typing import Any

from jinja2 import Environment, FileSystemLoader, select_autoescape

# ── Paths ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
REPO_ROOT = Path(__file__).parent.parent
TEMPLATE_DIR = REPO_ROOT / "templates" / "crp"
CONFIG_PATH = REPO_ROOT / "config" / "crp_config.yaml"
SCHEMA_PATH = REPO_ROOT / "config" / "crp_report_schema.json"


# ── Config Loader ────────────────────────────────────────────────
def load_config() -> dict:
    """Load CRP YAML config."""
    with open(CONFIG_PATH) as f:
        return yaml.safe_load(f)


def load_schema() -> dict:
    """Load CRP JSON schema."""
    with open(SCHEMA_PATH) as f:
        return json.load(f)


# ── Jinja2 Environment ───────────────────────────────────────────
def get_jinja_env() -> Environment:
    """Create Jinja2 env with CRP template directory."""
    return Environment(
        loader=FileSystemLoader(str(TEMPLATE_DIR)),
        autoescape=select_autoescape(["json"]),
        trim_blocks=True,
        lstrip_blocks=True,
        keep_trailing_newline=True,
    )


# ── Renderers ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
def render_notion_blocks(report: Any) -> list[dict]:
    """Render CycleReport to Notion API block JSON."""
    config = load_config()
    env = get_jinja_env()
    template = env.get_template("notion_report.json.j2")
    rendered = template.render(
        report=report,
        config=config,
        SRS_CODES=config.get("srs_codes", {}),
    )
    return json.loads(rendered)


def render_slack_message(report: Any) -> dict:
    """Render CycleReport to Slack Block Kit JSON."""
    config = load_config()
    env = get_jinja_env()
    template = env.get_template("slack_summary.json.j2")
    rendered = template.render(report=report, config=config)
    return json.loads(rendered)


def render_markdown(report: Any) -> str:
    """Render CycleReport to Markdown string."""
    config = load_config()
    env = get_jinja_env()
    template = env.get_template("cycle_report.md.j2")
    return template.render(
        report=report,
        config=config,
        SRS_CODES=config.get("srs_codes", {}),
    )


def render_nats_event(report: Any) -> dict:
    """Render CycleReport to NATS event payload."""
    env = get_jinja_env()
    template = env.get_template("nats_event.json.j2")
    rendered = template.render(report=report)
    return json.loads(rendered)


# ── Validator ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
def validate_report(report_dict: dict) -> list[str]:
    """Validate a report dict against the CRP JSON schema.
    Returns list of error messages (empty = valid).
    """
    try:
        import jsonschema
    except ImportError:
        return ["jsonschema not installed — skipping validation"]

    schema = load_schema()
    validator = jsonschema.Draft202012Validator(schema)
    errors = []
    for error in sorted(validator.iter_errors(report_dict), key=str):
        errors.append(f"{error.json_path}: {error.message}")
    return errors


# ── Artifact Writer ──────────────────────────────────────────────
def write_artifacts(report: Any, cycle_id: str) -> dict[str, Path]:
    """Write all output artifacts to build/reports/."""
    config = load_config()
    artifact_dir = REPO_ROOT / config.get("output", {}).get("artifact_dir", "build/reports")
    artifact_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

    paths = {}

    # JSON artifact
    json_path = artifact_dir / f"{cycle_id}.json"
    report_dict = asdict(report) if hasattr(report, "__dataclass_fields__") else report
    json_path.write_text(json.dumps(report_dict, indent=2, default=str))
    paths["json"] = json_path

    # Markdown artifact
    md_path = artifact_dir / f"{cycle_id}.md"
    md_path.write_text(render_markdown(report))
    paths["markdown"] = md_path

    # Validation report
    errors = validate_report(report_dict)
    if errors:
        err_path = artifact_dir / f"{cycle_id}.validation_errors.txt"
        err_path.write_text("\n".join(errors))
        paths["validation_errors"] = err_path

    return paths
```

## 12.5 Updated `vcc_cycle_reporter.py` Integration

Add this to the bottom of `vcc_cycle_reporter.py` (Section 11.4), replacing the hardcoded `render_to_notion_blocks` with the Jinja2 template engine:
```python
# ── Add to vcc_cycle_reporter.py after build_report() ────────────
from tools.crp_templates import (
    render_notion_blocks,
    render_slack_message,
    render_markdown,
    render_nats_event,
    validate_report,
    write_artifacts,
    load_config,
)


def post_cycle_report(report: CycleReport) -> dict:
    """Full CRP pipeline: validate → render → post → notify → archive."""
    config = load_config()
    results = {"cycle_id": report.cycle_id}

    # 1. Validate against JSON Schema
    report_dict = asdict(report)
    errors = validate_report(report_dict)
    if errors:
        print(f"⚠️  Validation warnings: {len(errors)}")
        for e in errors[:5]:
            print(f"   {e}")
    results["validation_errors"] = errors

    # 2. Post to Notion (Jinja2 rendered)
    if config.get("output", {}).get("notion", True):
        blocks = render_notion_blocks(report)
        headers = {
            "Authorization": f"Bearer {NOTION_TOKEN}",
            "Notion-Version": config["notion"]["api_version"],
            "Content-Type": "application/json",
        }
        for attempt in range(config["notion"]["retry"]["max_attempts"]):
            try:
                resp = requests.patch(
                    f"{NOTION_API}/blocks/{VCC_INSTRUCTIONS_PAGE_ID}/children",
                    headers=headers,
                    json={"children": blocks},
                )
                resp.raise_for_status()
                results["notion"] = "ok"
                break
            except Exception as e:
                wait = config["notion"]["retry"]["backoff_seconds"][attempt]
                print(f"Notion attempt {attempt+1} failed: {e}. Retrying in {wait}s...")
                import time; time.sleep(wait)
        else:
            results["notion"] = "fail"

    # 3. Post to Slack
    if config.get("notifications", {}).get("slack", {}).get("enabled"):
        slack_payload = render_slack_message(report)
        webhook_url = os.environ.get("VCC_SLACK_WEBHOOK_URL", "")
        if webhook_url:
            try:
                resp = requests.post(webhook_url, json=slack_payload)
                results["slack"] = "ok" if resp.ok else f"fail:{resp.status_code}"
            except Exception as e:
                results["slack"] = f"fail:{e}"

    # 4. Publish NATS event
    if config.get("notifications", {}).get("nats", {}).get("enabled"):
        nats_payload = render_nats_event(report)
        subject = config["notifications"]["nats"]["subject"]
        # VCC should use its existing NATS connection here
        results["nats_subject"] = subject
        results["nats_payload"] = nats_payload

    # 5. Write file artifacts
    if config.get("output", {}).get("json_artifact") or config.get("output", {}).get("markdown_artifact"):
        paths = write_artifacts(report, report.cycle_id)
        results["artifacts"] = {k: str(v) for k, v in paths.items()}

    return results
```


# 13. NATS → Redis Cache Invalidation Map

Every NATS event handler in `smp-fin-worker` MUST call `invalidate_cache()` for the affected resources. This map is the **single source of truth** for what gets busted when an event fires. The `useFinanceWS` hook on the frontend mirrors this logic via `EVENT_TO_QUERY_KEY` (see Appendix A, Section 2).

## 13.1 Invalidation Map

Place at `src/api/finance/cache.py`.
```python
# src/api/finance/cache.py

from typing import Callable
import hashlib, json

REDIS_PREFIX = "finance"
DEFAULT_TTL = 300  # 5 minutes

# ── Key Generators ──────────────────────────────────────────────

def _list_key(tenant_id: str, resource: str, filters: dict | None = None) -> str:
    """Cache key for paginated list endpoints."""
    base = f"{REDIS_PREFIX}:{tenant_id}:{resource}_list"
    if filters:
        h = hashlib.md5(json.dumps(filters, sort_keys=True).encode()).hexdigest()[:8]
        return f"{base}:{h}"
    return f"{base}:all"

def _detail_key(tenant_id: str, resource: str, entity_id: str) -> str:
    return f"{REDIS_PREFIX}:{tenant_id}:{resource}:{entity_id}"

def _dashboard_key(tenant_id: str) -> str:
    return f"{REDIS_PREFIX}:{tenant_id}:dashboard"

def _activity_key(tenant_id: str) -> str:
    return f"{REDIS_PREFIX}:{tenant_id}:activity_feed"

def _revenue_key(tenant_id: str) -> str:
    return f"{REDIS_PREFIX}:{tenant_id}:revenue_chart"

def _customer_key(tenant_id: str, customer_id: str) -> str:
    return f"{REDIS_PREFIX}:{tenant_id}:customer:{customer_id}"


# ── Invalidation Map ─────────────────────────────────────────────
# Key: NATS subject suffix (after "citadel.finance.")
# Value: list of key-pattern callables to bust

INVALIDATION_MAP: dict[str, list[Callable[[str, dict], list[str]]]] = {

    # ── Invoices ─────────────────────
    "invoice.created": [
        lambda tid, d: [_list_key(tid, "invoice"), _dashboard_key(tid), _activity_key(tid)],
    ],
    "invoice.sent": [
        lambda tid, d: [
            _list_key(tid, "invoice"),
            _detail_key(tid, "invoice", d["entity_id"]),
            _dashboard_key(tid),
            _activity_key(tid),
        ],
    ],
    "invoice.paid": [
        lambda tid, d: [
            _list_key(tid, "invoice"),
            _detail_key(tid, "invoice", d["entity_id"]),
            _dashboard_key(tid),
            _activity_key(tid),
            _revenue_key(tid),
            _customer_key(tid, d.get("customer_id", "")),
            _list_key(tid, "payment"),
            _list_key(tid, "customer"),
        ],
    ],
    "invoice.voided": [
        lambda tid, d: [
            _list_key(tid, "invoice"),
            _detail_key(tid, "invoice", d["entity_id"]),
            _dashboard_key(tid),
            _activity_key(tid),
            _customer_key(tid, d.get("customer_id", "")),
        ],
    ],
    "invoice.overdue": [
        lambda tid, d: [
            _list_key(tid, "invoice"),
            _detail_key(tid, "invoice", d["entity_id"]),
            _dashboard_key(tid),
        ],
    ],

    # ── Payments ─────────────────────
    "payment.received": [
        lambda tid, d: [
            _list_key(tid, "payment"),
            _list_key(tid, "invoice"),
            _detail_key(tid, "invoice", d.get("invoice_id", "")),
            _dashboard_key(tid),
            _activity_key(tid),
            _revenue_key(tid),
            _customer_key(tid, d.get("customer_id", "")),
            _list_key(tid, "customer"),
            _list_key(tid, "commission"),
        ],
    ],
    "payment.failed": [
        lambda tid, d: [
            _list_key(tid, "payment"),
            _detail_key(tid, "invoice", d.get("invoice_id", "")),
        ],
    ],
    "payment.refunded": [
        lambda tid, d: [
            _list_key(tid, "payment"),
            _list_key(tid, "invoice"),
            _detail_key(tid, "invoice", d.get("invoice_id", "")),
            _dashboard_key(tid),
            _revenue_key(tid),
            _list_key(tid, "credit_note"),
            _customer_key(tid, d.get("customer_id", "")),
        ],
    ],

    # ── Quotes ───────────────────────
    "quote.created": [
        lambda tid, d: [_list_key(tid, "quote"), _dashboard_key(tid), _activity_key(tid)],
    ],
    "quote.accepted": [
        lambda tid, d: [
            _list_key(tid, "quote"),
            _detail_key(tid, "quote", d["entity_id"]),
            _dashboard_key(tid),
            _activity_key(tid),
        ],
    ],
    "quote.declined": [
        lambda tid, d: [
            _list_key(tid, "quote"),
            _detail_key(tid, "quote", d["entity_id"]),
        ],
    ],
    "quote.expired": [
        lambda tid, d: [
            _list_key(tid, "quote"),
            _detail_key(tid, "quote", d["entity_id"]),
        ],
    ],

    # ── Contracts ────────────────────
    "contract.signed": [
        lambda tid, d: [
            _list_key(tid, "contract"),
            _detail_key(tid, "contract", d["entity_id"]),
            _dashboard_key(tid),
            _activity_key(tid),
            _list_key(tid, "invoice"),  # auto-invoice may be created
        ],
    ],

    # ── Customers ────────────────────
    "customer.created": [
        lambda tid, d: [_list_key(tid, "customer")],
    ],
    "customer.updated": [
        lambda tid, d: [
            _list_key(tid, "customer"),
            _customer_key(tid, d["entity_id"]),
        ],
    ],
    "customer.tier_upgrade": [
        lambda tid, d: [
            _list_key(tid, "customer"),
            _customer_key(tid, d["entity_id"]),
            _dashboard_key(tid),
        ],
    ],

    # ── Commissions ──────────────────
    "commission.calculated": [
        lambda tid, d: [_list_key(tid, "commission")],
    ],
    "commission.approved": [
        lambda tid, d: [
            _list_key(tid, "commission"),
            _detail_key(tid, "commission", d["entity_id"]),
        ],
    ],

    # ── Disputes ─────────────────────
    "dispute.created": [
        lambda tid, d: [
            _list_key(tid, "invoice"),
            _detail_key(tid, "invoice", d.get("invoice_id", "")),
            _dashboard_key(tid),
            _list_key(tid, "dispute"),
        ],
    ],
    "dispute.resolved": [
        lambda tid, d: [
            _list_key(tid, "invoice"),
            _detail_key(tid, "invoice", d.get("invoice_id", "")),
            _dashboard_key(tid),
            _list_key(tid, "dispute"),
            _revenue_key(tid),
        ],
    ],

    # ── Dashboard ────────────────────
    "dashboard.refresh": [
        lambda tid, d: [_dashboard_key(tid), _activity_key(tid), _revenue_key(tid)],
    ],
}


# ── Invalidation Engine ──────────────────────────────────────────

async def invalidate_cache(redis_client, tenant_id: str, event_subject: str, event_data: dict) -> int:
    """Invalidate all Redis keys affected by a NATS event.
    
    Args:
        redis_client: Upstash Redis client
        tenant_id: UUID string
        event_subject: NATS subject suffix (e.g. 'invoice.paid')
        event_data: Event payload dict
    
    Returns:
        Number of keys invalidated
    """
    handlers = INVALIDATION_MAP.get(event_subject, [])
    if not handlers:
        return 0
    
    keys_to_bust = set()
    for handler in handlers:
        keys_to_bust.update(handler(tenant_id, event_data))
    
    # Remove empty keys
    keys_to_bust = {k for k in keys_to_bust if k and not k.endswith(':')}
    
    if keys_to_bust:
        # Pipeline delete for efficiency
        pipe = redis_client.pipeline()
        for key in keys_to_bust:
            pipe.delete(key)
        await pipe.execute()
    
    return len(keys_to_bust)
```

## 13.2 Worker Event Handler Pattern

Every event handler in `smp-fin-worker` MUST follow this pattern:
```python
# src/workers/finance_event_handler.py

async def handle_finance_event(msg):
    """Universal NATS event handler for cache invalidation + side effects."""
    event = FinanceEvent.model_validate_json(msg.data)
    subject_suffix = msg.subject.replace('citadel.finance.', '')
    
    # 1. Always invalidate cache first
    busted = await invalidate_cache(
        redis_client, event.tenant_id, subject_suffix, event.model_dump()
    )
    logger.info(f"Cache: busted {busted} keys for {subject_suffix}")
    
    # 2. Push to WebSocket subscribers
    await ws_manager.broadcast_to_tenant(
        event.tenant_id,
        {'type': subject_suffix, 'data': event.data, 'timestamp': event.timestamp}
    )
    
    # 3. ACK the message
    await msg.ack()
```

# 14. Typed `financeApi` Client Module

The React components reference `financeApi.getInvoices(filters)` etc. This is the complete typed client the VCC MUST generate. It wraps `apiFetch` from Appendix A Section 3.3.
```typescript
// src/lib/financeApi.ts

import { apiFetch, ApiError } from './apiClient';
import type {
  Customer, CustomerCreateInput,
  Invoice, InvoiceCreateInput, InvoiceLineItem,
  Quote, QuoteLineItem,
  Payment, TextToPayInput, TextToPayResult,
  DashboardStats, ActivityItem,
  Service, TaxRate, Commission,
  IntegrationStatus,
  Paginated,
  AIGeneratedLineItem,
} from '@/types/finance';
import { v4 as uuidv4 } from 'uuid';

type ListParams = {
  cursor?: string;
  limit?: number;
  search?: string;
  sort_by?: string;
  sort_dir?: 'asc' | 'desc';
  [key: string]: unknown;
};

function qs(params: Record<string, unknown>): string {
  const filtered = Object.entries(params).filter(([, v]) => v != null && v !== '');
  return filtered.length ? '?' + new URLSearchParams(
    filtered.map(([k, v]) => [k, String(v)])
  ).toString() : '';
}

export const financeApi = {

  // ── Dashboard ─────────────────────────────────
  getStats: (token: string) =>
    apiFetch<DashboardStats>('/api/finance/dashboard/stats', { token, method: 'GET' }),

  getActivity: (token: string, cursor?: string) =>
    apiFetch<Paginated<ActivityItem>>(
      `/api/finance/dashboard/activity${qs({ cursor, limit: 20 })}`,
      { token, method: 'GET' }
    ),

  // ── Invoices ──────────────────────────────────
  getInvoices: (token: string, params: ListParams & { status?: string; overdue_only?: boolean } = {}) =>
    apiFetch<Paginated<Invoice>>(
      `/api/finance/invoices${qs(params)}`,
      { token, method: 'GET' }
    ),

  getInvoice: (token: string, id: string) =>
    apiFetch<Invoice>(`/api/finance/invoices/${id}`, { token, method: 'GET' }),

  createInvoice: (token: string, data: InvoiceCreateInput) =>
    apiFetch<Invoice>('/api/finance/invoices', {
      token, method: 'POST', body: JSON.stringify(data),
      idempotencyKey: uuidv4(),
    }),

  updateInvoice: (token: string, id: string, data: Partial<InvoiceCreateInput>) =>
    apiFetch<Invoice>(`/api/finance/invoices/${id}`, {
      token, method: 'PUT', body: JSON.stringify(data),
    }),

  sendInvoice: (token: string, id: string, method: 'email_link' | 'text_to_pay', opts?: { phone?: string; message?: string }) =>
    apiFetch<Invoice>(`/api/finance/invoices/${id}/send`, {
      token, method: 'POST',
      body: JSON.stringify({ method, ...opts }),
      idempotencyKey: uuidv4(),
    }),

  voidInvoice: (token: string, id: string) =>
    apiFetch<Invoice>(`/api/finance/invoices/${id}/void`, {
      token, method: 'POST', idempotencyKey: uuidv4(),
    }),

  // ── Text-to-Pay ───────────────────────────────
  sendTextToPay: (token: string, data: TextToPayInput) =>
    apiFetch<TextToPayResult>('/api/finance/payments/text-to-pay', {
      token, method: 'POST', body: JSON.stringify(data),
      idempotencyKey: uuidv4(),
    }),

  recordManualPayment: (token: string, data: { invoice_id: string; amount: number; method: string; description?: string }) =>
    apiFetch<Payment>('/api/finance/payments/manual', {
      token, method: 'POST', body: JSON.stringify(data),
      idempotencyKey: uuidv4(),
    }),

  // ── Quotes ────────────────────────────────────
  getQuotes: (token: string, params: ListParams & { status?: string } = {}) =>
    apiFetch<Paginated<Quote>>(
      `/api/finance/quotes${qs(params)}`,
      { token, method: 'GET' }
    ),

  getQuote: (token: string, id: string) =>
    apiFetch<Quote>(`/api/finance/quotes/${id}`, { token, method: 'GET' }),

  createQuote: (token: string, data: any) =>
    apiFetch<Quote>('/api/finance/quotes', {
      token, method: 'POST', body: JSON.stringify(data),
      idempotencyKey: uuidv4(),
    }),

  sendQuote: (token: string, id: string) =>
    apiFetch<Quote>(`/api/finance/quotes/${id}/send`, {
      token, method: 'POST', idempotencyKey: uuidv4(),
    }),

  acceptQuote: (token: string, id: string) =>
    apiFetch<Quote>(`/api/finance/quotes/${id}/accept`, {
      token, method: 'POST', idempotencyKey: uuidv4(),
    }),

  declineQuote: (token: string, id: string, reason?: string) =>
    apiFetch<Quote>(`/api/finance/quotes/${id}/decline`, {
      token, method: 'POST', body: JSON.stringify({ reason }),
    }),

  convertQuoteToInvoice: (token: string, id: string) =>
    apiFetch<Invoice>(`/api/finance/quotes/${id}/convert-to-invoice`, {
      token, method: 'POST', idempotencyKey: uuidv4(),
    }),

  // ── AI Quote Generation ───────────────────────
  generateAIQuote: (token: string, data: { customer_id?: string; job_description: string }) =>
    apiFetch<{ line_items: AIGeneratedLineItem[]; suggested_total: number; market_context: any }>(
      '/api/finance/quotes/ai-generate',
      { token, method: 'POST', body: JSON.stringify(data) }
    ),

  // ── Customers ─────────────────────────────────
  getCustomers: (token: string, params: ListParams & { is_archived?: boolean; tag?: string } = {}) =>
    apiFetch<Paginated<Customer>>(
      `/api/finance/customers${qs(params)}`,
      { token, method: 'GET' }
    ),

  getCustomer: (token: string, id: string) =>
    apiFetch<Customer>(`/api/finance/customers/${id}`, { token, method: 'GET' }),

  createCustomer: (token: string, data: CustomerCreateInput) =>
    apiFetch<Customer>('/api/finance/customers', {
      token, method: 'POST', body: JSON.stringify(data),
    }),

  updateCustomer: (token: string, id: string, data: Partial<CustomerCreateInput>) =>
    apiFetch<Customer>(`/api/finance/customers/${id}`, {
      token, method: 'PUT', body: JSON.stringify(data),
    }),

  // ── Service Catalog ───────────────────────────
  getServices: (token: string) =>
    apiFetch<Paginated<Service>>('/api/finance/catalog', { token, method: 'GET' }),

  createService: (token: string, data: any) =>
    apiFetch<Service>('/api/finance/catalog', {
      token, method: 'POST', body: JSON.stringify(data),
    }),

  // ── Tax Rates ─────────────────────────────────
  getTaxRates: (token: string) =>
    apiFetch<Paginated<TaxRate>>('/api/finance/tax-rates', { token, method: 'GET' }),

  // ── Commissions ───────────────────────────────
  getCommissions: (token: string, params: ListParams & { status?: string } = {}) =>
    apiFetch<Paginated<Commission>>(
      `/api/finance/commissions${qs(params)}`,
      { token, method: 'GET' }
    ),

  approveCommission: (token: string, id: string) =>
    apiFetch<Commission>(`/api/finance/commissions/${id}/approve`, {
      token, method: 'POST',
    }),

  // ── Integrations ──────────────────────────────
  getIntegrationStatus: (token: string) =>
    apiFetch<IntegrationStatus>('/api/finance/integrations/status', { token, method: 'GET' }),

  connectStripe: (token: string) =>
    apiFetch<{ onboarding_url: string }>('/api/finance/integrations/stripe/connect', {
      token, method: 'POST',
    }),

  disconnectStripe: (token: string) =>
    apiFetch<void>('/api/finance/integrations/stripe/disconnect', {
      token, method: 'POST',
    }),

  connectMercury: (token: string, apiKey: string) =>
    apiFetch<void>('/api/finance/integrations/mercury/connect', {
      token, method: 'POST', body: JSON.stringify({ api_key: apiKey, read_only: true }),
    }),

  getMercuryBalance: (token: string) =>
    apiFetch<{ balance: number; last_updated: string }>('/api/finance/integrations/mercury/balance', {
      token, method: 'GET',
    }),

  // ── PDF ───────────────────────────────────────
  getInvoicePDF: (token: string, id: string) =>
    apiFetch<{ pdf_url: string }>(`/api/finance/invoices/${id}/pdf`, { token, method: 'GET' }),

  getQuotePDF: (token: string, id: string) =>
    apiFetch<{ pdf_url: string }>(`/api/finance/quotes/${id}/pdf`, { token, method: 'GET' }),

  // ── Refunds / Credit Notes ────────────────────
  createRefund: (token: string, data: { payment_id: string; amount?: number; reason?: string }) =>
    apiFetch<Payment>('/api/finance/payments/refund', {
      token, method: 'POST', body: JSON.stringify(data),
      idempotencyKey: uuidv4(),
    }),

  // ── Search ────────────────────────────────────
  search: (token: string, query: string, types?: string[]) =>
    apiFetch<{ results: Array<{ type: string; id: string; title: string; snippet: string }> }>(
      `/api/finance/search${qs({ q: query, types: types?.join(',') })}`,
      { token, method: 'GET' }
    ),
};
```

### Usage in Components

```typescript
// Every component uses financeApi like this:
const { data, isLoading } = useQuery({
  queryKey: ['invoices', tenant.id, filters],
  queryFn: () => financeApi.getInvoices(token, filters),
});
```

# 15. Status Transition State Machines

The VCC MUST enforce these transitions server-side. Any transition not in these maps MUST return `INVALID_STATUS_TRANSITION` (HTTP 422). The frontend uses these to determine which action buttons to show.

## 15.1 Invoice Status Machine

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> draft
    draft --> sent: send()
    draft --> void: void()
    sent --> viewed: customer opens link
    sent --> paid: webhook: invoice.paid
    sent --> partial: partial payment
    sent --> overdue: cron: past due_date
    sent --> void: void()
    viewed --> paid: webhook: invoice.paid
    viewed --> partial: partial payment
    viewed --> overdue: cron: past due_date
    viewed --> void: void()
    overdue --> paid: webhook: invoice.paid
    overdue --> partial: partial payment
    overdue --> void: void()
    partial --> paid: remaining paid
    partial --> overdue: still outstanding past due
    partial --> void: void()
    paid --> refunded: full refund
    paid --> disputed: webhook: dispute.created
    disputed --> paid: dispute won
    disputed --> write_off: dispute lost
    void --> [*]
    refunded --> [*]
    write_off --> [*]
```
```python
# src/api/finance/state_machines.py

INVOICE_TRANSITIONS: dict[str, set[str]] = {
    'draft':    {'sent', 'void'},
    'sent':     {'viewed', 'paid', 'partial', 'overdue', 'void'},
    'viewed':   {'paid', 'partial', 'overdue', 'void'},
    'overdue':  {'paid', 'partial', 'void'},
    'partial':  {'paid', 'overdue', 'void'},
    'paid':     {'refunded', 'disputed'},
    'disputed': {'paid', 'write_off'},
    # Terminal states — no transitions out
    'void':     set(),
    'refunded': set(),
    'write_off': set(),
}

QUOTE_TRANSITIONS: dict[str, set[str]] = {
    'draft':     {'sent'},
    'sent':      {'viewed', 'accepted', 'declined', 'expired'},
    'viewed':    {'accepted', 'declined', 'expired'},
    'accepted':  {'converted'},  # → invoice or contract
    # Terminal states
    'declined':  set(),
    'expired':   set(),
    'converted': set(),
}

CONTRACT_TRANSITIONS: dict[str, set[str]] = {
    'draft':     {'sent'},
    'sent':      {'viewed', 'signed', 'expired', 'cancelled'},
    'viewed':    {'signed', 'expired', 'cancelled'},
    # Terminal states
    'signed':    set(),
    'expired':   set(),
    'cancelled': set(),
}

RECURRING_TRANSITIONS: dict[str, set[str]] = {
    'active':    {'paused', 'completed', 'cancelled'},
    'paused':    {'active', 'cancelled'},
    # Terminal states
    'completed': set(),
    'cancelled': set(),
}

COMMISSION_TRANSITIONS: dict[str, set[str]] = {
    'pending':     {'approved', 'disputed'},
    'approved':    {'paid', 'clawed_back'},
    'disputed':    {'approved', 'clawed_back'},
    # Terminal states
    'paid':        {'clawed_back'},
    'clawed_back': set(),
}


def validate_transition(machine: dict[str, set[str]], current: str, target: str) -> bool:
    """Check if a status transition is valid. Raise HTTPException if not."""
    allowed = machine.get(current, set())
    if target not in allowed:
        from fastapi import HTTPException
        raise HTTPException(422, detail={
            'error': 'INVALID_STATUS_TRANSITION',
            'message': f'Cannot transition from {current} to {target}',
            'details': {'current': current, 'target': target, 'allowed': sorted(allowed)}
        })
    return True
```

## 15.2 Frontend Action Button Map

Use this to determine which buttons to render per status:
| **Entity** | **Status** | **Available Actions** |
| Invoice | `draft` | Edit, Send, Send via TTP, Void, Preview PDF |
| Invoice | `sent` / `viewed` | Resend, Send TTP, Void, Download PDF, Record Manual Payment |
| Invoice | `overdue` | Send Reminder, Send TTP, Void, Record Manual Payment |
| Invoice | `partial` | Send Reminder, Send TTP, Void, Record Manual Payment |
| Invoice | `paid` | Download PDF, View Receipt, Issue Refund |
| Invoice | `disputed` | Upload Evidence (read-only otherwise) |
| Invoice | `void` / `refunded` / `write_off` | Download PDF (read-only) |
| Quote | `draft` | Edit, Send, Preview PDF |
| Quote | `sent` / `viewed` | Resend, Download PDF |
| Quote | `accepted` | Convert to Invoice, Convert to Contract |
| Quote | `declined` / `expired` / `converted` | Download PDF (read-only) |

The VCC blueprint spans 7 documents. Use this index to find what you need.
| **Document** | **Contains** | **Use When** |
| **This page** — VCC Build Instructions & Guardrails | Sections 1–16: Identity, Yeses/Nos, Build Order, Conventions, Env Vars, Checklist, LLM rules, Pitfalls, Definition of Done, CRP, Automation, Cache Map, financeApi, State Machines, this Index | Starting any task. Read Section 2 (Yeses) and Section 3 (Nos) before every file you generate. |
| **Parent Spec** — Finance Guild UI Layout & Dashboard Spec (Dev Handoff) | Sections 1–22: All wireframes, component specs, SRS codes (Section 19), REFLEX triggers (Section 20), SMP services (Section 21), database schema DDL (Section 13) | Understanding _what_ to build. This is the canonical source of truth. If it conflicts with this page, the spec wins. |
| **Schema Page** — fg_* Schema & RLS Policies | Raw DDL for all `fg_*` and `finance_*` tables, complete RLS policies, ENUMs, indexes, trigger functions | Writing migrations, RLS policies, or any SQL. Copy DDL exactly — do not modify column names or types. |
| **Appendix A** — API Schemas, Auth & Routing | Pydantic v2 request/response models, TypeScript type definitions, Supabase Auth integration flow, AuthProvider, JWT validation, frontend route config, AuthGuard, EntitlementGuard, FinanceLayout | Generating route files, schema files, types, auth middleware, or frontend route config. |
| **Appendix B** — Templates, Events, Errors & Seed Data | Email templates (10), SMS templates (4), n8n workflow registry (10 workflows), NATS event payloads, Stripe webhook event map, complete error code catalog (40+ codes), seed data, responsive breakpoints, number generators | Building notification handlers, webhook routes, error responses, mobile layouts, or setting up dev environment. |
| **Appendix C** — Entitlements, RBAC, Policy Layers & Service Rebrand | Entitlement keys + tier matrix, RBAC role→permission table, policy enforcement middleware, Guilds rebrand name mapping, route/NATS/DB rename instructions | Implementing entitlement gates, role checks, or renaming services to Guilds branding. |
| **Appendix D** — Website Rebuild Functions Package & Notion Feedback Loop | Notion↔VCC sync functions, page hydration, diff engine, block-level content push, feedback loop module, website rebuild package | Posting cycle reports to Notion, syncing spec changes, or rebuilding the marketing site. |

[CALLOUT] 📌 **Read order for a new VCC session:** This page (Sections 1-3) → Parent Spec (Sections 13, 19, 20) → Schema Page (DDL for target tables) → Appendix A (schemas for target routes) → Appendix B (error codes + events) → Start building.

- Add phone_number TEXT column to call_transcripts (for fast caller lookup)
- Add transcript_text GENERATED ALWAYS AS (transcript->>'text') STORED (auto-extracts text)
- Add indexes for phone_number and created_at for query performance

**citadel_crew_api.py Updates:**
- save_call_transcript(): persists post-call webhook transcript + metadata to DB
- get_recent_transcripts(): queries call_transcripts by phone_number (was broken before)
- post_call_webhook(): now saves transcript FIRST, then distills via Bedrock
- distill_context(): supports both DB transcript_text and fallback inline text
- PostCallRequest: added conversation_id, transcript_text, agent_id fields

**Result:**
Post-call distillation pipeline now executes: save → fetch → distill → cache → NATS.
Previously, get_recent_transcripts() failed (column_does_not_exist), so distillation never fired.
